American Press Comments on Silver Policy 42

San Francisco: Several newspapers widely circulated throughout the country published editorials today stating that the silver policy was a political action by the government under pressure from the silver faction in Congress. This action will increase the insecurity of business, but it is recognized that the silver policy encourages international use of silver and that a gold-based currency system is indeed desirable. If agreed upon by all countries, a bimetallic standard with 75% gold reserves and 25% silver reserves is more effective than the current gold standard. However, contrary to expectations, there is still no hope for international agreement. If the United States unilaterally implements this system, it will inevitably have currency conflicts with other countries, which will increase international disputes, and this move is also very dangerous domestically. (National News Agency dispatch on the 27th)

Competition in the Atlantic Skies Between Airplanes and Airships 43

French Aviator Flies Directly to New York

Zeppelin Airship Goes to Brazil

(New York) Today, an Associated Press reporter on the Mahadden mail ship, which was sailing from New York to London, received a wireless message from aviators Rossi and Cordu, who were 260 miles east of New York. The reporter reported that the sea was calm, the sky was clear, and the wind was light. Rossi and Cordu departed from the Le Bourget airfield near Paris at 5:10 AM on the morning of the 26th to fly to the United States, intending to fly to California in order to break their long-distance flight record. Their plane is a monoplane with 500 horsepower. (National News Agency dispatch on the 27th)

(New York) Wireless stations here received a report from French aviators Codos and Rossi, saying, "We are currently flying over Nova Scotia (Note: a province on the Atlantic coast of eastern Canada). Steering is extremely difficult. Nothing is visible outside. Everything is safe." Currently, all radio stations along the Atlantic coast of the United States have been ordered by their superiors to monitor the arrival of the two aviators. Radio stations along the coast of Canada have also received similar orders. According to Dr. Kimball, Director of the New York Weather Bureau, the climate along the Atlantic coast is still conducive to flight. The only concern is that Codos and Rossi may encounter rain in the Nova Scotia area. However, the wind direction is currently maintaining its normal state. Normally, at this time of year, the wind here is often from the west, but it has suddenly turned to an east wind, which is unusual. It is likely that if Codos and Rossi decide to fly over New York City and then west, they will use this east wind to fly directly from Nova Scotia to New York. Dr. Kimball also said that looking at the current weather map, the climate is surprisingly similar to that measured in 1930 when Coste and Bellonte made their first east-to-west transatlantic flight. It is truly strange. At that time, Coste and Bellonte flew with the wind and circled through areas of high and low pressure to reach Curtiss Airfield. Now, Codos and Rossi are also in the same situation and can arrive with the wind. As for the speed of the two aviators, it is generally estimated that it was 200 kilometers per hour in the first 15 hours of flight. (Havas dispatch on the 27th)

New York: According to a wireless message received here from the "Le Bourget" plane piloted by French aviators Codos and Rossi, the plane is requested to proceed as usual. The plane sends out messages at any time to notify the location it passes through. From this, it can be estimated that Codos and Rossi have flown over the border between Nova Scotia and New Brunswick, and at 5:20 AM local time, they flew over Halifax. The Bruner area of Newfoundland is known as the "North Atlantic Graveyard," and the climate is very harsh. Now, Codos and Rossi have flown over this area and are 965 kilometers away from New York. In the eastern United States, although they have a tailwind, a storm is rising in the rocky mountains, and it is a southwest wind, which is not conducive to flight. It is generally estimated that the average speed of the plane is now 165 kilometers per hour, and it will accelerate afterwards, as the gasoline in the plane is gradually decreasing. If they enter the United States from Lower Canada into Titroia, and then to San Diego, the distance is shorter than going through New York. (Havas dispatch on the 28th)

(New York) The "Le Bourget" plane piloted by French aviators Codos and Rossi sent out a wireless message saying that the engine is not working well and may arrive in New York at 3:00 PM (Greenwich time). After arriving, it may stop moving forward, and it is not certain. (Havas dispatch on the 28th)

Boston: The French ship Champolion, which frequently communicates by wireless with French aviators Rossi and Codos, sent out a wireless short report stating that the two aviators plan to land at the Floyd Bennett Field in New York. This is where the two started their flight to Syria last year, setting a new record. The reason has not been explained. It is likely that the plane they are flying is not flying very well or that the weather is bad en route, and they are using too much fuel, so they may not be able to fly to the California coast. But in any case, if the two arrive safely in New York, their achievement should not be taken lightly. New York is preparing to give them a grand welcome. At 1:00 PM today, the two were clearly flying near the Massachusetts coast. (Reuters dispatch on the 28th) St. Louis: French aviator Mermoz, accompanied by three companions, began his long-distance flight across the South Atlantic today in the three-engine plane "Arc-en-Ciel," hoping to overtake the Zeppelin airship and reach Natal, Brazil. The plane took off at 3:00 PM this afternoon, hoping to overtake the German airship in the Atlantic sky in order to reach Brazil first. The Zeppelin airship departed from Germany at 7:30 PM on Saturday, and when the "Arc-en-Ciel" took off from the Paris airfield, it was 44 and a half hours behind the Zeppelin airship when it left the west coast of Africa. (National News Agency dispatch on the 28th)

Internal Instability Still Remains in Austria 44

Vienna: The Austrian government's decision to expand the powers of the special court has sparked demonstrations by the Socialist Party. Last night, workers gathered and marched in the Simmering area, shouting slogans such as "Long live freedom," "Down with tyranny," and "Down with Dollfuss." It is said that there was gunfire, but this has not been confirmed. The military and police are on alert to prevent disturbances. It is said that troops have been sent to trouble spots such as Styria. The Austrian government has decided to allow the special court to impose the death penalty on all those who plot to undermine the safety of life or property, whether they are principals or accessories. (Reuters dispatch on the 27th)

Vienna: This morning, police found a bomb weighing four and a half pounds outside the Stock Exchange building. The scheduled time of explosion was 6:30 PM. If it had not been found, the consequences would have been devastating. The Austrian official news agency is located in the building, and Reuters and other world news agencies are also located there. The purpose was clearly to destroy the Austrian news agency, as 6:30 PM is the time when the agency begins its work. The authorities are currently investigating. (Reuters dispatch on the 27th)

Hungary Seeks Closer Ties with Austria 45

Bomb Explodes at European War Memorial 47

(Paris) Parisian Military Governor General Goiran, Minister Enget, Madame Joffre, and many other prominent figures were nearly injured this morning. They, together with representatives of the Italian Embassy and members of the Garibaldi Association (an Italian group that fought for France), went to the Chas Cemetery to open a specially constructed memorial to commemorate the Italian volunteers who joined the French army in 1914. As the group was about to reach its destination, a bomb suddenly exploded next to the memorial, injuring two gravediggers who were taken to the hospital. However, the memorial was undamaged. The incident caused considerable consternation, but the opening ceremony was held as planned. It is not yet known who planted the bomb. (Reuters dispatch on the 27th)

Soviet Union Raises Wages 48

Because of the Increase in Bread Prices

(Moscow) The Soviet authorities issued the following order: Due to frequent droughts and partial crop damage in the southern regions of the Soviet Union, grain market prices have increased, resulting in various consequences. This phenomenon has forced the People's Committee and the Central Committee of the Party to raise the excessively low prices of bread rations. The People's Committee and the Central Committee of the Party are aware that once bread ration prices increase, the situation of low-wage workers and employees will be difficult. Therefore, they ordered that from June 1, 95 million rubles per month be allocated to increase the monthly wages of low-wage workers and employees in the Soviet Union. This amount will require 665 million rubles by the end of this year. In addition, with the increase in social insurance funds allocated by the state due to the increase in wages, the total amount of monthly wage increases will be 107 million rubles, that is, a total increase of 749 million rubles by the end of the year. (TASS dispatch on the 28th)

Disarmament Conference Reopens: Henderson Strives to Rescue the Crisis 49

American and Russian Representatives to Present Proposals Today

Turkey to Announce Restoration of Military Installations in the Straits

(Geneva) After a long recess, the steering committee of the Disarmament Conference convened this afternoon. Chairman Henderson, in his opening remarks, stated that there were many rumors regarding the future of the Disarmament Conference, some of which seemed to accept failure. He hoped that the steering committee would unanimously recommend to the General Commission to acknowledge the gravity of the situation and to demonstrate an unwavering determination to advance efforts to achieve a disarmament treaty. Henderson reviewed the recent trends in disarmament talks, mentioning the French memorandum of April 17. He noted that the French memorandum stated that France would immediately reduce its armaments, but could not agree to other countries immediately rearming. The General Commission of the Disarmament Conference is scheduled to meet tomorrow afternoon at 1:30 PM, at which time US Representative Davis and Russian Representative Litvinov will both speak. (Reuters, 28th)

(Geneva) The Bureau of the Disarmament Conference is scheduled to hold a closed meeting at 3:30 PM today. The meeting will be very brief. After a short statement by Chairman Henderson, several delegations will express their wish to reserve their declarations for the General Commission. The General Commission will likely be convened by the Bureau to meet the following day. It is generally hoped that the situation of the Disarmament Conference will be clarified by then. The General Commission meeting will last for a week, after which the Bureau will reconvene to determine the conclusions reached. However, in any case, most delegations do not advocate transferring the Disarmament Conference case to the League of Nations Council. Even if the General Commission's discussions are not progressing well, most delegates would rather declare the Disarmament Conference adjourned again than transfer it to the Council. (Havas, 28th)

(Geneva) Reuters has learned from well-informed sources that Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü will make an extremely important statement to the Disarmament General Commission regarding the Dardanelles and Bosphorus Straits, stating that Turkey no longer considers itself bound by the provisions of the Treaty of Lausanne, which stipulates that no military installations should be placed in these two areas. (Reuters, 27th)

(Geneva) British Lord Privy Seal Eden, US Representative Davis, Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov, and US observer Wilson all arrived here today. Davis had a lengthy meeting with Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson, discussing the procedures of the Disarmament Conference. (Reuters, 27th)

(Paris) At 10:00 PM tonight, Foreign Minister Barthou led the French delegation to Geneva to attend the General Commission meeting of the Disarmament Conference. Members of the delegation included Minister of Marine Pietri, Deputy Chief of the Army General Staff General Gamelin, and his principal assistants. British Foreign Secretary Simon, Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü, and Greek Minister to France and Vice-Chairman of the Disarmament Conference Politis also traveled to Geneva in the same train. According to a previous dispatch from this agency's correspondent in Yugoslavia's capital, Titulescu and Litvinov recently came here from France. It is possible that Titulescu negotiated with Litvinov here. (Havas, 27th)

A joint air defense exercise was held in Oran, French Algeria, Africa, by a squadron of seaplanes stationed in the port of Oran and the Mediterranean Fleet stationed outside the port. The theme of the exercise was aircraft bombing naval formations. At the start of the exercise, sirens and bugles sounded simultaneously throughout the city. All churches also rang their bells to warn residents. Electricity was immediately cut off, and the entire city was plunged into darkness. Only the sounds of airplanes and seaplanes shuttling back and forth in the sky could be heard, while the sound of cannons and machine guns roared. The exercise stopped at dawn. (Havas, 28th)

Anti-Japanese Sentiment in Dutch Territories 55

Restricting the Import of Fifty-Six Types of Goods

And Banning Japanese Ships from Docking

Osaka According to a dispatch from a certain source, the Dutch East Indies government is increasingly oppressing Japanese businesses. Proposals for import restrictions discussed between Japan and the Netherlands, apart from cotton products, include as many as fifty-six types of miscellaneous goods. At the same time, the extreme anti-Japanese attitude of the commercial company licensing system is being used to deal with negotiations. On the other hand, under the policy of favoring domestic ships, Japanese ships will be prohibited from docking at Balikpapan and one other port where South Seas mail ships dock. Therefore, if the above cases are realized, Japanese goods may not be able to maintain 30% of the current total trade volume of 150 million yuan, or it may be reduced to 15%, i.e., 20 to 30 million yuan, which is quite worrying. Even the Batavia system, which currently imports 50 million yuan from the Dutch East Indies to Japan, may be on the verge of crisis. (Electric Communication, 28th)

Group Immigration of "Pseudo-Manchukuo" to Hinata 57

Prince Chichibu Scheduled to Depart

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Colonial Affairs, regarding the Brazilian restrictions on immigration, has been cooperating with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to urge the Brazilian government to reconsider and is studying countermeasures. On the other hand, it is concentrating its main efforts on the Manchurian industrial immigration policy as a follow-up measure. After concrete negotiations with the Army, the Ministry of Finance, the Kwantung Army, the Kwantung Government, and the South Manchuria Railway, it plans to implement this fundamental policy starting next year. That is, the Manchurian Self-Defense Agricultural Immigration Plan, which has been trialed since 1932 (500 people per year), will end this year. From next year onwards, agricultural immigration plans of 500,000 people in 20 years, 200,000 people in 10 years, 100,000 people in 5 years, and 30,000 people per year will be established. The scope of agricultural immigration will be further expanded to include industrial, commercial, mining, and other industrial immigrants, so that groups can formally immigrate in order to develop the industries of Japan and Manchuria and increase the common welfare of the people. Various direct and indirect necessary institutions, such as immigration land companies and immigration associations merged by Japan and Manchuria, should be established in sequence. (Japan United Press, 28th)

France Advocates Increasing Permanent Council Members of the League of Nations 60

The Soviet Union, Poland, and Spain Each Get a Seat

The Number of Non-Permanent Council Seats Increased Simultaneously

(Paris) Recently, the rumor of the Soviet Union joining the League of Nations has been rampant. If the Soviet Union joins the League of Nations, it will demand to obtain one of the permanent council seats of the Executive Council. Therefore, Poland will inevitably make the same request, making the resolution quite difficult. Recently, French Foreign Minister Barthou declared in the House of Representatives that this problem can be resolved by proposing a compromise solution. The method is to increase the number of permanent council seats of the Executive Council and increase the number of non-permanent council seats in the same proportion. In this way, the Soviet Union, Poland, and Spain can each obtain a permanent council seat. However, this method is expected to be opposed by Argentina or other member states. It is reported that France also intends to propose abolishing the permanent council seats when possible, but this reform plan is also afraid of encountering opposition from Italy and other parties. Therefore, according to general predictions here, the issue of the permanent council seats of the Executive Council is worthy of serious consideration by delegations from various countries. Although France has repeatedly guaranteed Poland and treated it with sincerity, Poland and Russia are competing for the leadership of the Slavic countries. If the League of Nations grants the Soviet Union a permanent council seat but withholds it from Poland, it will inevitably be unacceptable to Poland. Furthermore, it is not a good plan for the League of Nations to gain a new member state and lose another member state. (Havas, 27th)

Japan Prepares to Participate in Naval Preliminary Conference 61

Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Navy Agree

But Hope Not to Discuss the Far East Issue

(Tokyo) As a result of discussions between the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Navy, Foreign Minister Hirota will submit a draft instruction to Ambassador Matsudaira in London to the Cabinet for approval tomorrow. It is reported that the Japanese government has expressed its appreciation for the British sincerity in disarmament and accepted the suggestion to open bilateral talks. Japan does not object to the convening of a general conference by the countries of the naval treaty at any time, if it is deemed appropriate. However, Japan firmly believes that the naval conference does not need to discuss the Nine-Power Treaty, the Far East issue, and political issues, as these matters have already been thoroughly discussed by the League of Nations. Therefore, the Japanese government firmly believes that the next naval conference will only discuss defense and naval power. (Reuters, 28th)

France Asks That Russia Also Participate 62

The Situation After the Washington Conference Has Changed

(Paris) The French government has likely received a note from the British government, the content of which is probably the same as the note sent by Britain to the governments of Washington and Tokyo. In the note, the British government stated that according to the provisions of the Washington Naval Treaty, when the treaty expires in 1935, another naval conference should be convened. Now, Britain suggests that before the 1935 naval conference is convened, the countries concerned should first engage in preparatory talks. These talks will likely involve the exchange of opinions between the two sides of each country in accordance with normal diplomatic procedures, with London as the center of contact. If all the invited countries participate in these talks, then France does not seem to reject participation. According to general observations, in recent years, the scope of naval issues has expanded greatly. In addition to the old issues, several new issues have been added, such as the Soviet Union being recognized by most countries after the signing of the Washington Treaty. This fact is one of the new issues. Although the Soviet Union is not a signatory to the Washington Treaty, it has now been recognized by most countries, which is tantamount to joining the group of great powers. Although the current Soviet navy is very weak, it seems that the naval limitation treaty is unlikely to be implemented without the participation of the Soviet Union. (Havas, 27th)

A Glimpse of the Attitudes of Britain and the United States 63

(Washington) Rear Admiral Woodward of the Naval Department recently declared that the current situation in Europe and the rest of the world makes the cause of disarmament hopeless. He said, "Every time at an international conference, the United States always loses something. Under such circumstances, the only policy that the United States should adopt is to strengthen its military, sharpen its weapons, and urgently prepare for national defense to meet the needs of the times, and not to slack off in the slightest. The world situation is as we have witnessed it, and it is probably impossible for countries to abandon armaments. The United States has always supported the movement for sincere disarmament, but does not want to be drawn into the whirlpool of European political machinations."

British Bao Bicheng Overseas Dominion Minister Thomas delivered a speech on British Empire Day, stating briefly that Britain has always decided to fulfill the obligations that Britain has signed, but we must firmly express to the world that the only purpose we seek is peace. Regardless of how difficult the current environment is, what the London government is doing its best to maintain is peace. In some parts of the world, there are now various factors that are enough to create a situation that is more dangerous than before the Great War of 1914, but Britain, to the extent possible, is implementing disarmament. Britain's implementation of reducing armaments is almost reaching the limit of danger. (Havas, 27th)

The Process of British Foreign Secretary Simon Initiating the Naval Preliminary Conference 65

(Washington) Non-official circles studying why Britain is promoting the preliminary talks of the 1935 naval disarmament conference today claimed to have learned the inside story as follows: Japan wanted to hold preliminary talks, but was unwilling to be the first to propose it because it was not sure of success. The United States also vaguely expressed its willingness to participate in these talks, but for the same reason, it was also unwilling to be the initiator. Non-official circles believed that British Foreign Secretary Simon had occasionally made an oral suggestion to the American Ambassador to Britain Bingham, saying that this time may be the most appropriate time to open negotiations. Unexpectedly, it was accepted by the United States. Once Simon said it, a team of horses could not catch up, so he had no choice but to invite Japan, France, Italy, and other countries to participate together. (National News Agency, 27th)

At this conference, it seems that only technical issues and procedural matters will be discussed, without discussing issues of policy or doctrine. Britain has sent proposals to Japan, the United States, France, Italy, and others, among which the United States has now expressed its consent to participate in the preliminary conference. Central and National Government Memorial Week Reports 67

Chen Zhaoying...Party Affairs in Fujian Province

Lin Sen...People's Livelihood

(Nanjing) At 9:00 AM on the 28th, the Central Government held the 132nd Memorial Week for the Premier, attended by Central Committee members Ye Chucang, Chen Zhaoying, Liu Shouzhong, Chen Ce, Deng Jiayan, Wang Qi, Li Ciwen, and all staff, totaling about 600 people. Chairman Ye Chucang presided, and Chen Zhaoying reported on party affairs and the situation of suppressing bandits in Fujian Province, briefly stating that party affairs in Fujian Province were scattered during the previous rebellion of Chen Mingshu. However, due to a shortage of funds, the progress of establishing lower-level party branches and preparing for the provincial representative assembly was slightly slow. Furthermore, the suppression of bandits in Fujian Province has been very successful. The bandit areas have now been reduced to only five counties, and it is hoped that they can be cleared up in the short term. Although the situation in the province is special compared to other provinces, Chairman Chen has been able to cope with ease and take appropriate measures in Fujian. Today, he will study with everyone from a narrow perspective, that is, the issue of personal clothing, food, housing, and transportation. At this time when the New Life Movement is being vigorously implemented throughout the country, our lives, every move, should never forget the four characters of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. This is the true new life. The ancients had people who would rather starve to death than lose their integrity, which is enough to prove that clothing, food, housing, and transportation are all related to propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. He hoped that everyone would encourage each other. (Central News Agency, 28th)

International Commercial Telegram

May 28th Reuters Special Commodity Report 76

(Gold and Silver)

London Gold Price: The London gold price today is 130 shillings and 8.5 pence, up 1.5 pence.

London Silver Bullion: The London silver market spot price is unchanged, remaining at 19.5 pence. Futures fell 0.0625 to 19.5 pence. The market was uneventful and closed steady.

New York Silver Bullion: The banking sector is quiet but stable. Although there is an expectation of higher prices, operators are watching and not entering the market. The market price is about 45 to 50 pounds sterling higher than London. The forward opening price for July to December has decreased by 5 to 10 pounds sterling compared to last Saturday, and January is longer pounds sterling.

Bombay Silver Bullion: The Bombay silver market closed steady, with prices unchanged. The spot price is 53 rupees and 11 annas.

(Exchange Rates)

British-American: The London foreign exchange market saw slight demand for US dollars, but the market was quiet. The opening exchange rate for British-American was 5 dollars and 9.125 cents, up 0.125 from last Saturday's closing rate. It fell slightly in the morning, with the latest price at 5 dollars and 8.6875 cents, down 0.4375 from the opening price. Also, one US dollar equals 3 shillings and 11.186 pence in British gold.

British-French: The opening rate remained at 77 francs 09, and only rose 6 pounds sterling at noon, to 77 francs 15, with no further changes.

American-British: The opening exchange rate for American-British was 5 dollars and 8.75 cents, down 0.25 from last Saturday's closing rate. It gradually decreased after opening, reaching 5 dollars and 8.25 cents, but then recovered to 5 dollars and 8.75 cents, the same as the opening price.

(Cotton and Wheat)

American Cotton: The opening was quiet, and later, due to poor Liverpool telegrams, retail sales loosened prices. The weather is suitable for planting cotton, and sentiment is mixed.

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market rose due to speculators buying new Broach cotton. The closing price for July-August Broach cotton was 197 rupees 375, up 1 rupee 375 from Saturday.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market, at 1:00 PM, the July price was 5.93, up 3 pounds sterling from Saturday.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market, the July price fell half a penny to 4 shillings and 6.625 pence.

(Rubber)

London: Rubber was calm. At noon, the transaction price for July-September was 6 pence, down 0.062 yuan from Saturday's closing price.

New York: Rubber opened weak, due to the low London telegrams. Dealers sold, while speculators bought. The market is now awaiting new impetus. Prices are about 40 to 45 pounds sterling lower than London.

(Securities)

New York: The securities market this morning regarded the Washington news as good, and opened firmly, with a resurgence of the upward trend. Public confidence in the actual position of the securities market is still good, but labor strikes are a factor limiting trading. Merchants are unwilling to take risks and await new developments. A few days ago, many people went to steal them, hammering and damaging part of them. Ultimately, they were not stolen due to their size. The county government has now ordered the villagers to protect them. (28th Special Dispatch)

Britain, France, and Italy Strive to Expand Their Air Forces (British Correspondence) 103

The New Trend of Arms Race Among Nations

Soviet Union's Chemical Warfare Preparedness Emerges as a Force

Dark clouds are gathering over Europe, and everywhere there is the possibility of causing war. However, the reason why no unexpected disaster has occurred at present is not because the countries concerned do not want to take this opportunity to settle old scores, restore their declining economic strength, and break the status quo. It is only because they are all restricted by domestic factors. The economic panic has not yet been overcome, anti-war sentiment is still quite strong, and none of the countries themselves have a sure chance of winning. Therefore, at this time, no country dares to challenge lightly.

The European stalemate is doomed in this chaotic situation. Britain certainly does not need to argue about firmly grasping the helm of the European continent, but she cannot but be concerned about European affairs. The control of the world's commercial markets cannot be easily let go. Now the dominance of the navy and army seems to be a thing of the past. Although they still each occupy their own position, their importance has indeed gradually diminished. The emerging military force!! The air force is gradually becoming the focus of military affairs. Britain certainly does not want to fall behind in this regard. At present, the strength of the British air force is that the total number of squadrons in its domestic flight team is 75, and there are 23 squadrons overseas, including 13 fighter squadrons, 10 teams organized in coordination with the army and navy, 34 light bomber squadrons, 10 heavy bomber squadrons, 1 communications aircraft squadron, and 7 flying boat squadrons. The total number of aircraft incorporated into the squadrons is estimated to be about 1,500. The budget for the 1933 fiscal year was £19,638,600. The aviation personnel include 3,150 officers and 25,042 enlisted men. Furthermore, in view of the current tense situation in Europe and the deteriorating atmosphere in the Far East, it is necessary to have further plans. Therefore, the number of squadrons of British domestic aircraft will be expanded to 89, the number of personnel will be expanded to 40,000, and the number of aircraft will be increased to 2,072.

Britain is so focused on the expansion of the flight team. France, which is known as the world's number one air force, certainly does not want to be outdone. Her air force (except for a small number of naval air forces) has 35 fighter squadrons, 46 reconnaissance and observation squadrons, 9 light bomber squadrons, 18 heavy bomber squadrons, and 2 cover squadrons, totaling 110 squadrons. In addition, there are 18 balloon squadrons and 24 squadrons of overseas troops. The number of aircraft is about 3,000. The budget for the 1933 fiscal year was 16,904,130,000 francs. The personnel include 2,090 officers and 30,412 enlisted men. In the future, she will expand to 210 squadrons and increase to 5,900 aircraft. The European power second only to France, Italy, wants to compete with her for hegemony in the Mediterranean and wants to gain control in Central Europe. Therefore, Italy is also expanding its air force. Her current strength is 36 fighter squadrons, 28 reconnaissance squadrons, 31 bomber squadrons, 14 training squadrons, and 14 squadrons of unknown types, totaling 123 squadrons. In addition, there are two balloon squadrons. The air force organized in coordination with the army has four regiments. The air force strength in the colonies is outside. The number of aircraft is about 1,500. The budget for 1933-34 is 6,959,480,000 lira. Her air force personnel include 2,437 officers, 4,088 non-commissioned officers, and 25,029 soldiers. Her expansion plan has not yet found

concrete figures.

The Soviet Union is a mysterious country in the world, especially its military organization, which has never been publicly announced. However, after her first five-year plan was quite successful, everyone knows that it contains extremely serious military implications. In January of this year, according to a certain expert's estimate, the Soviet Union's air force has 46 fighter squadrons, 87 reconnaissance squadrons, 46 bomber squadrons, and 31 attack and other squadrons, totaling 210 squadrons. In addition, there are 13 balloon squadrons and 32 naval aircraft squadrons. The total number of aircraft is about 3,000. Her chemical warfare preparedness is especially sufficient to show the characteristics of her air force.

The major European countries are making such efforts in air force preparation. As for the so-called arms reduction, everyone knows that it is just diplomatic rhetoric. (April 25th in London)

Prelude to Cooperation Between Japanese Political Parties Japan Correspondence 104

(The Last Gasp of Parliamentary Politics)

(The Sole Symbol of Warlord Autocracy)

Since the Japanese military instigated the September 18th Incident, exciting the passions of the general populace, the Japanese constitutional government and parliamentary discussions have not only been weak in themselves, but the military has also paid little attention to them, and the majority of the people have become weary of them. For example, the Seiyukai party, which held an absolute majority of 300 seats in the Diet, was unable to legally obtain power. Even after its leader was assassinated by an active-duty military officer, it took a year and a half before anyone dared to openly question it. This fully demonstrates the incompetence of the parliament and further proves that political parties without a financial background do not have the trust of the majority of the people.

The reason why Japanese parliamentary politics has been able to continue to this day is that, politically speaking, Japan has not completely broken away from feudal relations. Therefore, its elder statesmen still have considerable power in political actions. Although Prince Saionji Kinmochi does not have the same power in the military as Yamagata Aritomo, he has a special position in politics. He strongly advocates constitutional politics, believing that parliament is necessary no matter what. Therefore, the current situation can be temporarily maintained by Saitō, and the form of parliament can also exist. Furthermore, no matter how tyrannical the Japanese warlords are, and no matter how dissatisfied the young officers are, they are only dissatisfied with the people in power in the current government (in other words, the cabinet). There is no question about the entire system. In that case, as long as the current system is preserved, the parliamentary politics supported by capitalists will still have room to exist. Moreover, they still need them to manage finances.

The struggle between the financial groups and the warlords almost came to blows in the early spring of this year. Initially, the military retreated step by step, but later it launched a counterattack by using the issue of discipline. As a result, the political parties were utterly defeated. Now the military has a more solid and powerful new arrangement in military affairs. This arrangement is no weaker than that of the September 18th Incident, but it is not easy to determine when and what event will be used to launch it. Therefore, the financial groups are even more backward in comparison. The financial groups and those who support parliament have now decided to unite the Seiyukai and Minseitō parties, eliminate partisan disputes and personal emotional conflicts, and engage in what is called policy coordination. On the surface, they all say that after Japan withdrew from the League of Nations, there is a great trend of isolation in the international community, and at the same time, there is international economic competition and pressure on Japan in trade. However, in fact, although Japan's domestic economic life is showing a lively scene due to the stimulation of the military-industrial industry, those who benefit are only a very small minority. The general public is still groaning under the recession, and life is extremely difficult. For example, the former Chief Executive of Korea, Hiraoka Sadatarō, even went so far as to forge writings of Emperor Meiji to swindle money because he had no means of living. The plight of those in the middle and lower classes can be inferred from this. In such a torrent of life's difficulties, what the Japanese rulers (whether warlords or financial groups) fear most is the deterioration of ideology. In the past, in the era when there was more freedom of speech, there was always a group of people who tended to engage in legal movements. Now, although there are no obvious signs of major deterioration on the surface, in reality, reactionary organizations are developing very rapidly. Whether among industrial workers in cities, students in schools, tenant farmers and hired laborers in rural areas, there is extremely strong deterioration. Even the so-called various patriotic organizations on the right wing are certainly stubbornly conservative, but they are the same in wanting to break the status quo, and they often use violent means. Therefore, for their own survival, financial capitalists, on the one hand, help the warlords to advocate their extraordinary times theory, and at the same time, they want to find ways to consolidate their own position. Maintaining the existence of parliament is the most important step. Therefore, the political and civil parties are negotiating and paying special attention to the rice problem and the issue of ideological education.

The preliminary steps for cooperation between the political and civil parties are, in terms of technology: (1) The two parties take turns as chairman during meetings; (2) The time and place of the meeting are decided by the responsible persons of the two parties after consultation, and then communicated to the chairman, who notifies the attending representatives; (3) The content of the meeting will only be published publicly after both parties have consulted and believe that it can be published; (4) The secretaries-general of the two parties are responsible for this meeting.

This is the wonderful method that they believe is the most powerful and most capable of overcoming the current contradictions. It is also the result of Saionji's advocacy of maintaining constitutional politics after he arrived in Tokyo. However, it is a big question whether this kind of movement can achieve political results. As for a few large financial groups such as Mitsui, Mitsubishi, and Furukawa, they may take this opportunity to expand their monopoly in Japan. They also have considerable confidence in extending it to the four northeastern provinces. However, these methods will never save Japan's urgent situation. If they want to expand overseas again, they will run into obstacles. Talking about winning with a majority in parliament and using members to subdue the warlords is simply like dreaming, because the Seiyukai already has an absolute majority of seats there. In short, the future development of the Japanese political situation, whether in diplomacy or military affairs, will be dominated by the warlords. At most, the financial groups will only be slightly larger vassals. Therefore, the conspiracies of the military should be given special consideration, and the trend of the Japanese political situation should be discerned from the actions of the military. (May 23rd, Tokyo)

Stalled Private Sale of the East China Railway; China, Japan, and Russia Actively Prepare for War 105

(Japanese Side Constantly Transports Troops)

(Soviet Russia Concentrates Forces to Fortify Defense)

Harbin Correspondence: Recently, the war preparations of both Japan and Russia have become increasingly tense. The Japanese army is currently actively concentrating on the northern border of the Northeast.

The eastern line takes Tielinghe Station as its base camp, and more than 20,000 Japanese troops are stationed in Suifenhe. The western line takes Hailar as its base camp, and the number of troops stationed there is unknown, but they are still being transported. In addition, for the convenience of military transportation, the Japanese are also working hard to build railways from Dunhua to Dongning, from Mudanjiang via Mishan to Sanxing, and from Bei'an Town to Heihe. At the same time, the Russians have concentrated 140,000 troops, 400 aircraft, 300 tanks, 13 armored vehicles, and 12 submarines in Vladivostok between Manchuria and Vladivostok, and are still working hard to replenish them. As for our volunteer army, there are still more than 30,000 people near Mishan, and it is said that they are also receiving assistance from the Russian side. Therefore, although Japan and Russia have reopened discussions on the private sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, it is difficult to hope that they will not break down and thus lead to a final duel, judging from the situation of the military deployments of both sides. (Northeast News Agency)

Huang Musong Passes Through Ya'an 106

Liu Wenhui Offers Opinions on Resolving Sino-Tibetan Disputes

Ya'an Correspondence: Huang Musong, the special envoy dispatched by the National Government to pay respects to the Dalai Lama, passed through Ya'an, western Sichuan, on his way to Tibet via Sichuan and Kang. He met with Liu Wenhui, the commander-in-chief of the Sichuan-Kang Border Defense, and inquired about the recent situation of the disputes between Kang and Tibet, as well as his opinions on the future of resolving Sino-Tibetan disputes. Liu offered Huang detailed opinions based on the key points of his years of dealing with Tibet. His original words are as follows: "Since the second year of the Yongzheng reign of the late Qing Dynasty, the offices of chief and deputy resident ministers in Tibet were established. Throughout the Qing Dynasty, there was never a shortage of these officials. Therefore, during the period when Lian Yu and Zhang Yingtang were stationed in Tibet at the end of the Qing Dynasty, even though Britain and Russia made all kinds of plans for Tibet, and the Qing court and Lian Yu also took wrong measures, the Qing Dynasty's control over Tibet never lost its shape. Since the revolution, no senior official of the central government has personally set foot in Tibet. As a result, the relationship between China and Tibet has become increasingly estranged, and in fact, it has even become isolated. Now, the arrival of Envoy Huang in Tibet is truly the first of its kind in the twenty years of the Republic of China. Its significance is extremely great and can be called the first in the history of Sino-Tibetan relations in the Republican era. A new development of all Sino-Tibetan events and relations is rooted here. Now that I have passed through Ya'an, and you have inquired about my humble views, Wenhui's responsibility lies in offering my meager advice.

First, regarding the Sino-Tibetan issue, from the perspective of its historical evolution, the Sino-Tibetan relationship began with the marriage of Princess Wencheng in the early Tang Dynasty and ended with the Tang Dynasty, which was the golden age of Tibet. China and Tibet were nephew and uncle states. The Song Dynasty paid tribute respectfully and was subordinate without doubt. The Yuan Dynasty especially revered Tibetan monks, and governed the area as a province. They treated them with kindness and bestowed upon them the honorific titles of Dharma King and National Preceptor, and allowed them to be hereditary. Therefore, throughout the Ming Dynasty, there were no Tibetan troubles. Until the Qing Dynasty, the Kangxi, Yongzheng, and Qianlong emperors used both kindness and authority to deal with Tibet, which was very harmonious. Therefore, the territory and sovereignty of Tibet have belonged to us from the beginning. The historical facts are clear and obvious. From the perspective of disputes, since Britain conquered India in the twenty-first year of the Qianlong reign, Warren Hastings and Samuel Turner entered Tibet. From the fifteenth year of the Jiaqing reign, emissaries who secretly explored Tibet were sent to Tibet constantly, which laid the roots of the Sino-Tibetan issue. Later, it gradually evolved into all the outstanding issues of today. In the twenty-eighth year of the Guangxu reign, the Qing court even considered concluding a secret treaty with Russia regarding Tibet. Since the British invaded Tibet and engaged in negotiations with us, the treaties that have been documented began with the "Chefoo Convention" in the second year of the Guangxu reign, followed by the "Sino-British Burma Convention" in the twelfth year of the Guangxu reign, the "Indo-Tibetan Convention" in the sixteenth year of the Guangxu reign, the "Calcutta Indo-Tibetan Convention" in the nineteenth year of the Guangxu reign, and the "Tibet-India Supplementary Convention" concluded by Tang Shaoyi and the British envoy Satow in the thirty-third year of the Guangxu reign (the "Anglo-Tibetan Convention" of the thirtieth year of the Guangxu reign was attached to this convention). In the "Anglo-Russian Entente" of the thirty-third year of the Guangxu reign, there were also provisions regarding Tibet. Since the Republic of China, there have been protests by the British envoy Sir John Jordan in the first year of the Republic, and our reply. In the second year of the Republic, there was the "Mongolian-Tibetan Treaty" under the manipulation of Britain and Russia, and the extremely important Simla Conference also began in that year. In February of the third year of the Republic, Britain suddenly proposed a new proposal to divide Inner and Outer Tibet. In April, the conference ended, and Chen Yifan signed a draft treaty without authorization. On May 1st, the government issued a telegram rejecting it. The Simla Conference thus broke down. Since then, there have been four more negotiations: one during the era when Yuan Shikai was brewing the imperial system in the fourth year of the Republic, the second during the declaration of war against Germany in the sixth year of the Republic, the third was the "Rongba Chaqia Armistice Agreement" concluded by Chen Xialing in the seventh year of the Republic, which had a term of one year. Therefore, in May of the eighth year of the Republic, the British envoy urged the negotiations very urgently, because they believed that the term of the Chen Agreement had expired. The fourth was the Nine-Power Treaty of the Washington Conference, which respected China's sovereignty and eliminated the provisions regarding special regions in China. In fact, this was in extreme conflict with the British policy towards Tibet, but its actual effect was equal to zero. In the twentieth year of the Republic, the Dabai Incident was fortunately resolved by the central government's power and the bravery of the soldiers, who drove the Tibetan army to the west bank of the Jinsha River and signed the "Gangtuo Agreement," which is probably the most recent treaty between China and Tibet. In general, the course of the Sino-Tibetan issue is extremely complex, and can be divided into different scopes: A. External, which involves Britain, India, Russia, and Mongolian Tibet, and it is not yet known whether it will involve Japan and Manchuria in the near future. B. Domestic, which involves Kang Tibet, Qing Tibet, and Yunnan Tibet. However, these two items also have mutual influences and involvements, but their main points are actually different. To put it bluntly, those belonging to item A, if you want to solve it, the parties involved are not only China and Tibet, but the issues involved are unusually heavy. Those belonging to item B are centered on the Kang Tibet dispute. According to the current situation, it is up to the central government to preside over it, and the neighboring provinces cooperate with it. No matter what method is adopted, it seems not difficult to achieve considerable results. After consultation and decision, we can then plan the negotiations of item A. According to my personal humble opinion, it may be smoother.

Second, regarding the Kang Tibet issue, the key to resolving the Kang Tibet dispute lies first in the border issue. According to the late Qing Dynasty's efforts to pass through the area, the Zhao brothers were appointed to govern Sichuan and Kang respectively. Zhao Erfeng relied on strong support and handled the matter freely. First, he laid the foundation for the territory. The methods he adopted were no more than three: 1. Forcing the Tusi to change to a flowing official system; 2. Conquering the wild Fan and making them surrender; 3. Recovering the Qing court's local areas. His power reached Jiangda, and he took Danta Mountain as the boundary with Tibet. Then Zhao was transferred to the position of Sichuan governor, and Fu Songqiu replaced him. He was planning to implement the establishment of a province, but the Republic of China was established, and the political situation changed. It was not completed. At that time, the Dalai Lama was in exile in India and took advantage of the opportunity to return to Tibet with the help of Britain, and launched a large-scale internal invasion, which even fell to Ba'an Lihua. Cai Songpo Yin Changheng was ordered to send troops and defeated the Tibetan army greatly, and recovered the old territory. After that, it failed again. Since then, those guarding the border have not been focused on the border. Not only could they not plan to recover it, but they also planned to establish a province to shield Sichuan and consolidate national defense. They even retreated to Ganzi and concluded the Rongba Chaqia Agreement, which aroused the Tibetan side's contempt and made the mad claim to advance to the South Bridge of Qiongzhou. In the twenty-first year of the Republic and this year, the two internal invasions were fortunately unsuccessful. Now that the Dalai Lama has passed away, the special envoy is coming west. This is probably a good opportunity to resolve the Kang Tibet border issue. As for the way to resolve it, from the perspective of its historical evolution, Danta Mountain should be the boundary. Secondly, from the perspective of the situation, the area of ​​Xikang should at least be extended to west of Changdu, because it can defend if retreating, and support if advancing by connecting Qing and Dian. But according to the current facts, if Tibet sincerely surrenders to the central government, then based on the meaning of the five ethnic groups being one family, reducing diplomatic difficulties, avoiding Tibetan suspicion and fear, in the situation of making all kinds of concessions, two benchmarks can be drafted:

1. According to the previous Qing Dynasty Tibetan settlement, all the land under the jurisdiction of the Hutuktu should be given to Tibet, because the jurisdiction and succession of the Hutuktu all belong to the resident minister in Tibet. In this way, Zhala Gongjue Changdu should all belong to Tibet. All the land under the jurisdiction of the Tusi should all belong to Kang, because the jurisdiction and succession of the Tusi all belong to the Sichuan Governor. In this way, the counties of Yanjing Jiangka Sanyan Baiyu Tongpu Dige Dengke Shiqu should all be returned to Kang according to their original jurisdiction. 2. Temporarily rely on the Gangtuo Agreement, starting from the lower reaches of the Jinsha River south of Wucheng, and going upstream to Dengke, all the east and west banks should be the Kang Tibet border line, and the original jurisdiction of the counties on the east bank that are on the west bank should still be returned to the old system. As for Yanjing County, which belongs to Kang's jurisdiction, the headquarters also appointed a county magistrate. After the Gesang Rebellion, it temporarily belonged to Gongga's autonomy. Now that Gongga has passed away, his will also sent representatives to request that the headquarters recover it. Now, because the Tibetan side has the Jiangka Rebellion, the headquarters has not sent troops to take over for the sake of avoiding their doubts. Its final return to Kang is a natural trend. However, if you want to take the above path, there must be a prerequisite, that is, the central government must have a solid grasp of Tibet. If Changdu does not belong to the territory of Xikang, then the gateway to Xikang will be wide open, and the key to border defense will not be available. If China and Tibet do not become one family, and Kang Tibet does not truly blend together, then if the Tibetan border is attacked by foreign invaders one day, Kang will also find it difficult to defend itself. (National News Agency)

Fujian Province Reorganizes Security Regiments 107

Xiao Qian Goes to Jiangxi to Request Instructions on Everything

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Provincial Security Office, considering that the local militias in the upper and lower counties not only lacked supplies and training, but also levied taxes on the spot and arrested people arbitrarily, which was deeply harmful to society, especially requested and obtained the approval of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to reorganize them all into security regiments for the sake of control. A total of fifteen regiments were established, requiring more than 300,000 yuan of military pay per month. However, even though these people have been enlisted, their wild nature is still difficult to tame. Incidents of disobeying orders and disturbing the people still occur from time to time. Some time ago, Chen Yucai, the fourth regiment stationed in Quanzhou, and Lin Jing, the seventh regiment stationed in Xingzhou, were disarmed by the Southern District Security Sub-Office for resisting troop transfers. After the mutinous soldiers escaped, many became bandits. Recently, the bandit atmosphere in the border area of Fuqing, Yongtai, and Minhou counties has become very strong. They have surrounded and seized regimental weapons, burned civilian houses, and kidnapped men and women, which was done by Lin Jing's remnants. The Security Office has repeatedly received reports from the county governments, requesting that troops be sent to suppress them. The office believes that the recent successive changes in the security regiments are due to some bad soldiers who are difficult to restrain and take risks, and half of them are also due to the old militia leaders who have been quiet for too long and miss action, colluding with their former troops and plotting wrongdoing. Currently, it has ordered the regiments to strictly eliminate bad soldiers to avoid affecting the entire regiment. It will improve the treatment of pure and good elements to reassure their minds. It will pay special attention to the actions of lower-level cadres such as platoon leaders. Those who dare to rebel and become bandits will be relentlessly suppressed. Those former militia leaders who behave improperly will also be investigated separately. In addition, Xiao Qian, the deputy director of the Security Office, took a boat to Shanghai on the 20th and then went to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to report on the current situation of the security team and request instructions on reorganization matters. He will probably return to the province in about two weeks. The security regiment will undergo a reorganization, or a re-establishment and downsizing, and another deputy commander will be set up to assist in training, with the aim of becoming an elite force. (May 23rd)

Statistics on National Local Public Bonds 108

(Total Amount of More Than 20.4 Million)

(The 21st Army of Sichuan Issues the Most)

Beijing News: In recent years, financial resources have been exhausted. Whenever provincial and municipal governments encounter something to do and face financial difficulties, they issue public bonds as the only solution. Over the years, the numbers are staggering. This kind of method greatly hinders rural revitalization. At the end of last year, the Rural Revitalization Committee sent a telegram to all people's organizations across the country, ordering them to report the details of local land tax surcharges and exorbitant taxes, so that they could be rectified. Reports have been successively submitted to the meeting. At the same time, they also received very detailed information on the issuance of public bonds by local governments, as well as the types and names of these bonds. The committee has sent them to the National Financial Conference for reference. It is reported that there have been as many as 61 types of local public bonds issued by provinces and cities since 1927. Among them, there are 51 types of provincial public bonds and 10 types of municipal public bonds. The total amount of provincial public bonds is more than 18.7 million yuan, and the total amount of municipal public bonds is more than 1.7 million yuan, totaling more than 20.4 million yuan. In terms of provinces, the 21st Army of Sichuan issued the most, with a total of 12 types issued since 1930, totaling 48.2 million yuan. Other provinces (Jiangxi) had 8 million yuan of financial treasury bonds for reorganization, 40,000 yuan of short-term treasury bonds with interest added for circulation, and recently issued two more types, one is the Yuping Railway Public Bond of 12 million yuan, and one is the Road Construction Circulation Bond of 4 million yuan, with a total issuance amount of 24.4 million yuan, most of which has not yet been repaid. (Anhui) The Anhui Provincial Public Bond, issued in recent years, is the short-term public bond for the construction of highways, issued in 1929 and continued in 1931, with a total of more than 560,000 yuan. In 1932, interest-bearing treasury bonds of 500,000 yuan were issued again. In the spring of 1933, the Sheyu Road Public Bond of 500,000 yuan was issued. (Zhejiang) Since 1928, there have been seven types of construction public bonds, etc., with a total amount of more than 30 million yuan. (Hubei) The Hubei Provincial Public Bond, issued in recent years, includes the two types of Hubei Xiaoshanhou Public Bond in 1931 and 1932, totaling 6 million yuan. (Hunan) Hunan Province issued two types of public bonds in the past year, namely the Hunan Provincial Public Bond (formerly known as the National Salvation Loan) and the Hunan Provincial Construction Public Bond. The former has an issuance amount of 5 million yuan, and the latter has an issuance amount of 10 million yuan. (Jiangsu) The provincial public bonds issued by Jiangsu in recent years, in addition to the silk industry short-term public bond jointly issued with Zhejiang, issued a construction public bond of 7 million yuan in 1930, but there are still many previous public bonds that have not been repaid. Other provinces such as Hebei also have public bonds issued. (28th)

Murder Case Discovered at Hequekou 110

Tao A'yuan, a resident of Hequekou in Punan, usually makes a living by recruiting private salt peddlers. Furthermore, he is addicted to gambling, which is hated by salt peddlers. Meningococcal Meningitis Discovered in the City 111

Wu Meiting, an apprentice at the Da Wuzhou Pharmacy on Ximenwai Street in Songjiang, 17 years old, suddenly suffered from fever and headache the day before yesterday. The body temperature was as high as 39 degrees, and the pulse was extremely rapid. The person in charge of the pharmacy sent him to the local Songjiang County Hospital for treatment. Zhang Shaoxiu, the director of the hospital, and Dr. Shi Ganlin performed a spinal tap examination and confirmed that it was epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis. He is now being injected with blood serum, and it is difficult to have confidence in obtaining it for a while. According to Zhang and others, the spread of this meningitis is extremely rapid. Once infected, it is appropriate to seek treatment as soon as possible, and it is especially necessary to isolate from family members to prevent infection. At the time of the rainy season, public health in the city should be paid attention to.

Suzhou

Wu County Implements Public Sale of Silkworm Eggs 112

The silkworms in this county have already been released on leaves during the major sleep, and they are about to climb the cocoon frame. Therefore, the cocoon merchants are preparing to set up cocoon collection agencies. The farmers are accustomed to pre-ordering silkworm eggs for the next year after the spring cocoons are sold. The Wu County Sericulture Improvement Zone is preparing for the public sale of silkworm eggs in accordance with the silkworm egg control measures promulgated by the Construction Department. The East and West Dongting Mountains will be divided into cocoon control zones, and the Hukou Provincial Women's Sericulture School, the Xiatsujiao Provincial Su Agricultural School, the Mudu, Guangfu, Wangting, Xiangshan, Nanbei Bridge, Shanren Bridge, and Xumenwai Huoyan Silkworm Egg Manufacturing Plant will be selected. A special public sale office will be organized at each location, and public sale measures will be formulated and implemented immediately.

Wuxi

Adulterer Slashes Husband in Tragedy 114

Lu Zhihuan, a resident of Ninguiren, Tonghui Road, near Huinong Bridge, is 44 years old and works as a handyman at the Zizai Baoxin Rice Mill. His wife, Chen, is 32 years old and also works as a female worker at the Ganshen Silk Factory. He has a son and a daughter, and the relationship between the husband and wife is not bad. Unexpectedly, three years ago, Chen became acquainted with Jia Yaoting, who used to be the squad leader of the merchant corps patrol team and a police officer of the Second Branch. At first, the two sides were quite secretive. In December of last year, Jia managed to move upstairs to Lu's house. On the surface, he was his neighbor, but secretly he continued to commit adultery with Chen. The matter was discovered by her husband, Lu Zhihuan, who could not help but be jealous. The two sides often had quarrels. On the evening of the 27th, at about 10 o'clock, Zhihuan and Yaoting had another dispute over a trivial matter. Unexpectedly, Yaoting's murderous intention suddenly arose. He immediately took a kitchen knife and slashed at Zhihuan indiscriminately. Zhihuan's head, arms, waist, and other parts of the body were cut more than ten times, covered in blood, and the wounds were as deep as an inch. He was extremely painful and fainted at once, and fell to the ground, unconscious. Zhihuan's father, Hengfang, saw that his son was being slashed and stepped forward to try to restrain Yaoting, causing his left hand to be slashed. Later, after someone reported it to the nearby patrol police, the adulterer Jia Yaoting and the adulterous woman Lu Chen were taken to the jurisdiction of the Sixth Public Security Bureau and transferred to the General Bureau for interrogation. At the same time, someone carried the injured man to the Brothers Hospital for treatment, and his life was in danger.

Qian Shunjin, a resident of Guangqin Road, along with two female workers from a silk factory, went to see the Nan Shui Xian Temple memorial celebration in the city the day before yesterday (the 26th). Yesterday (the 28th), all the foundry workers in the city went on strike in support of those who had been detained, expanding the situation and causing considerable local anxiety. Local News

Finance Minister Kong Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning; Discusses Exceptionally Successful Financial Conference; Regulations to be Enacted to督促Implementation 120

According to the Central News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Deputy Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, presided over the National Financial Conference in Beijing, which closed the day before yesterday (the 27th). Kong arrived in Shanghai on the Beijing-Shanghai night express train at 7 AM yesterday. He went to his private residence on Xihams Road for a brief rest. At around 10 AM, he went to the Central Bank on the Bund to work. In the afternoon at 4 PM, after attending the Central Bank Board of Directors meeting, he met with reporters from various newspapers. Excerpts of Kong's remarks are as follows: (Question) What are your thoughts on this Financial Conference? (Answer) At the beginning of this Financial Conference, with the financial chaos and tax revenue depletion in various provinces and cities, the people of the country were deeply concerned that the problems discussed at this conference would not be resolved satisfactorily. I was also quite doubtful. However, after the conference began, financial officials from remote cities came to attend the meeting despite the hardship. Over the course of seven days, more than one hundred cases were resolved. From beginning to end, they worked tirelessly. The most important financial issues at present, such as land registration, farmland consolidation, abolishing miscellaneous taxes, and compiling budgets, were thoroughly discussed. The implementation measures can be carried out by the financial authorities after the conference, according to the agreed-upon plan, one by one.

This will eliminate the previous problems of decisions being made without action or action without completion. I am exceptionally pleased with the successful outcome of this conference and the enthusiasm of the members. I feel that there are still solutions for the future of national finance. (Question) Are there any reward regulations for provinces and cities that implement the resolutions of the Financial Conference? (Answer) Rewards and punishments are the great tools of national governance. All cases resolved at this Financial Conference should be strictly ordered to be implemented by the financial authorities of each province and city, who will be held responsible. Those with excellent results will be rewarded, and those who do not implement them effectively will be punished. The Ministry of Finance will formulate regulations, submit them to the Executive Yuan, and then to the National Government for approval and implementation. (Question) How will the crackdown on prize-linked savings be carried out? What steps will be taken regarding the Sino-French Wan Guo Two Associations? (Answer) Although the crackdown on prize-linked savings was discussed at this conference, this matter is significant and involves complex issues. The Ministry will conduct in-depth research to ensure the best possible handling. (Question) When the business tax is implemented, if the provinces and cities still object due to foreign enclaves, will the national merchants also be delayed to show uniformity? (This includes special circumstances such as Shanghai, where Chinese and foreigners are mixed together.) (Answer)

The state collects taxes, and the people have the obligation to pay them. The implementation of the business tax requires national merchants to bear this tax obligation. As for provinces and cities with foreign concessions, at a time when our extraterritorial rights have not been fully recovered, foreign nationals may object and not want to pay this tax.

The government should negotiate with justice, and there will be solutions in the future. However, we can never delay the implementation of the tax for Chinese stores because foreigners object, resulting in a lack of tax revenue. (Question) The stamp tax and liquor license tax have been resolved to be prioritized for local financial income, which shows that the central government is sympathetic to the financial difficulties of local governments. However, how will the central government's financial income be compensated as a result of this slight shortfall? (Answer) The allocation of the above two taxes to local governments represents the central government's sympathy for local governments and the cooperation between the central and local governments. Previously, these two taxes belonged to the national tax, and the management was not perfect, and the tax revenue was not prosperous. Now that they have been allocated to the local governments, it is their responsibility to strictly eliminate tax evasion and increase tax revenue. It is hoped that proper consolidation will enrich local tax revenue, providing great assistance to local construction and solving local financial problems. The central government's finances will also be managed without effort. There is no distinction between the central and local governments. As for saving unnecessary expenses and opening up sources of income, those in charge of the central finance should have an overall plan. (Question) Can it be expected that all provinces and cities will fully comply with the implementation of local budgets starting in the second half of the year? (Answer) The purpose of this conference is to be feasible. Although local governments in our country have had budgets in the past, many are incomplete. Now that it has been resolved, the implementation of local budgets starting in the second half of the year must be followed. (Question) Wang Yitang is preparing to go to Japan to restore the Huì Yè Bank. If this is true, how will the government respond? (Answer) I have not heard of Wang's preparations to restore the Huì Yè Bank and cannot comment.

City Chamber of Commerce and Eleven Other Organizations Host Banquet for the Panchen Lama Last Night; Chairman Wang Xiaolai Delivers Welcome Speech; Wishing Him to Relieve Western Concerns After Returning to Tibet 123

Since completing the Kalachakra initiation ceremony in Hangzhou, the Panchen Lama has come to Shanghai for a short stay of ten days before going to Beijing to discuss returning to Tibet. The city's public organizations, recognizing the Panchen Lama's ten years of support for the central government, harmonizing border affairs, and striving for unification, hosted a banquet at the City Chamber of Commerce last night at 7 PM, to fulfill the duties of the host. Over a hundred people attended. Chairman Wang Xiaolai delivered a speech, and the Panchen Lama rose to respond. Details are recorded below:

(Venue Decoration)

A yellow colored archway was erected at the entrance of the City Chamber of Commerce at Tianhou Palace, with the words "Welcome" illuminated by electric lights. A yellow banner reading "Shanghai Public Organizations Welcome the Panchen Lama" was hung below. Banners were also hung at the two gates. Yellow silk ribbons were hung at the entrance on the ascent to the second floor, and yellow silk was hung on the third floor, creating a solemn atmosphere.

(List of Attendees)

The organizations represented at last night's banquet were the City Chamber of Commerce, Local Coordination Association, General Labor Union, Securities Industry Association, Chinese Jisheng Association, Chinese Moral Association, Chinese Red Cross Society, World Red Swastika Society, Shanghai South District Firefighting Federation, Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association, Shaoxing Seven Counties Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association, and eleven other organizations. (Chairman's Speech)

Chairman Wang Xiaolai delivered a welcome speech, saying, "Lama Buddha, esteemed guests, it is an honor for our association to have the Panchen Lama grace us with his presence today. China and Tibet have the closest relationship. Since Emperor Taizong of Tang married Princess Wencheng to Tubo Yezong Nongzan in the fifteenth year of Zhenguan (641 AD), there has been a history of one thousand two hundred and ninety-four years. Since the founding of the Republic of China, the five races have been one family, and the relationship between China and Tibet has become even more intense. This time, the Master sponsored the Kalachakra initiation ceremony in Hangzhou, promoting the true meaning of Buddhism. Our admiration for the Master has become even brighter and more upright. Today, the Master is returning to Beijing from Shanghai and will return to Tibet to preside over political and religious affairs. This is not only unanimously welcomed and supported by the Tibetan compatriots, but we also feel joy and encouragement. We deeply hope that the Master will preside over the Tibetan government as soon as possible. The Master's personality, qualifications, scholarship, and doctrines are enough to make people sincerely and wholeheartedly submit. The national compatriots are eagerly awaiting the early establishment of Tibetan government on track and coordination with the intentions of the Central Government, and are paying attention to it day and night. The Chinese nation is known as five races, but geographically, historically, and genetically, it has long been mixed into one. Now, although the compatriots in the Northeast have fallen under iron hooves and are suffering oppression, the Central Government still has the strength to slowly deal with it and gradually seek recovery, establishing a comprehensive plan to deal with the aggressors. Tibet is more than three thousand miles from east to west and more than a thousand miles from north to south, making it the highest plateau in the world. Its abundant resources and vast area make it an important western border of our country. Strong neighbors surround it, and the people's livelihood is not stable. This is why the whole country is deeply worried. Therefore, the security of Tibet is a major issue for the whole country that cannot be ignored. The Master has been a member of the Central Political Committee for many years and deeply understands the principles of the General and the intentions of the Central Government. The accompanying staff also understand the overall situation and are outstanding. Recently, Heaven has favored us, and the campaign flag points west. From now on, the Central Government will have no worries about the west, and the compatriots will be able to enjoy peace and happiness. Chinese culture can cross the Hengduan Mountains and spread throughout Tibet. Construction and transportation can cross the snow-capped mountains and the Yarlung Tsangpo River, and progress by land, sea, and air. This trip is something we can rely on. This is what we deeply hope for the Master, in addition to admiration. Lama Buddha, Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai City General Labor Union, Shanghai City Securities Industry Association, China Jisheng Association, China Moral Association, Shanghai China Red Cross Society, World Red Swastika Society, Shanghai Hunnan District Fire Rescue League, Ningbo Shanghai Compatriot Association, Shaoxing

Shanghai Local Coordination Association of Seven Counties and other organizations."

China and Tibet have a long history, and they have a great relationship with China in terms of religion and politics. Since Dr. Sun Yat-sen's successful revolution, the five races have been one family, and the relationship between China and Tibet has become even closer. Although we are now suffering from foreign aggression everywhere, as long as we follow Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will, unite, and unite the five races into one family, we can become stronger and stronger day by day. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will is very great, and we are willing to accept it with great enthusiasm and strive to implement it politically and religiously. However, I ask myself that I have limited ability and am ashamed of not being able to make any achievements, but I am very willing to use political power and religious power to work hard to promote the Three People's Principles and make China and Tibet more intimate (now I want to go back to Beijing and

Discuss with the Central Government the policy of governing Tibet after the death of the Dalai Lama, so that I can return early and put Tibetan politics on track to live up to your expectations, and I hope everyone will give me guidance at any time.)"
