Archbishop Cai Ning Returned to Shanghai from Songjiang Last Night; Departs North to Beiping Today 124

According to the New Sound Society, Archbishop Cai Ning, the representative of the Holy See in Rome, went to Sheshan in Songjiang to lead the faithful in pilgrimage to the Holy Mother. He returned to Shanghai last night and is scheduled to go north this afternoon to take up his new post. The details are as follows:

(Grand Occasion Upon Arrival in Songjiang)

At 6:00 AM on the 26th, Mr. Cai, accompanied by Consultant Bishop Antonius Yu, departed from Xujiahui in his own car, driven by President Sang. They arrived in Songjiang at 6:45 AM. County Magistrate Jin Tigian, along with Police Chief Zhou of the Public Security Bureau and believers, welcomed them at the station. After Mr. Cai alighted from the car and greeted the crowd, he boarded a sedan chair carried by four men and proceeded towards Qiujiawan. The county government military band, the Public Security Bureau police squad, and the Zhenzheng Middle School Boy Scouts led the way. After changing into ceremonial robes at the church, he celebrated Mass. Afterward, he met with local priests to inquire about church affairs, followed by a welcome from local believers and students. (Pilgrimage to Sheshan)

Catholic believers from Shanghai, Huai'an, Yangzhou, and other places were organized by the Catholic Promotion Association into a pilgrimage group to Sheshan in Songjiang to pay homage to the Holy Mother. In advance, they contacted the two railway administrations to prepare a special train from Shanghai South Station to Yaojinggang. At 4:00 AM, the train departed from South Station and arrived at Yaojinggang. Then, they boarded a prepared small steamer to Sheshan. Along the way, police officers and road protection soldiers dispatched by the Songjiang County Government accompanied and protected them. They did not arrive at Sheshan until around 8:00 AM. After the homage, at 3:30 PM, they took the small steamer from Sheshan to Yaojinggang and boarded the prepared special train from Yaojinggang to Shanghai South Station, returning to Shanghai around 9:00 PM.

(Leadership of Cai Ning)

The Catholic believers participating in the pilgrimage group, totaling over two thousand from Shanghai, Huai'an, Yangzhou, and other places, were led by President Lu Bohong and General Managers Zhu Zuoting and Lu Zhonglin. In addition to the participation of all students from Shanghai Zhengxiu Primary and Secondary Schools, a military band was also prepared to play music. After arriving at Sheshan, they first paid homage to the various memorial pavilions. Then, Archbishop Cai Ning led the male and female Catholic believers in a grand ceremony at the Church of the Holy Mother, followed by Mass. At 2:30 PM, the Holy Eucharist was blessed, and a group photo was taken with more than seventy priests present. At 3:30 PM, the Shanghai pilgrimage group returned to Shanghai. At 4:00 PM, Bishop Cai visited the nearly completed Great Church and the observatory on the mountaintop, accompanied by all the seminarians from the Sheshan Grand Seminary. The 28th was the Feast of Our Lady Help of Christians. Bishop Cai held a grand ceremony of welcoming the Holy Mother and Mass in Zhongshan. The lectors and singers were seminarians from the Xujiahui Grand Seminary, and the solemn atmosphere was extraordinary and grand. At noon, he left the mountain for Songjiang.

(Returned to Shanghai Last Night)

After President Lu Bohong of the Catholic Promotion Association raised funds to build Ruose Hospital on Songjiang Station Road, he specially opened up a plot of land to the left of the hospital to build a Church of the Holy Mother, which took ten months to complete. At 3:00 PM yesterday, the dedication ceremony was held, and Archbishop Cai Ning was invited to the hospital to bless it. Shanghai Aurora University purchased land in Songjiang to build a new building for its affiliated high school, and Bishop Cai also performed the cornerstone laying ceremony. At 8:00 AM, Archbishop Cai Ning left Sheshan for Songjiang to attend the dedication ceremony of the Church of the Holy Mother. At 4:00 PM, eighteen groups, including the Songjiang Party and government organizations, as well as the Chamber of Commerce and the Lawyers Association, jointly held a farewell meeting at the New Songjiang Society. At 6:00 PM, accompanied by President Lu Bohong and others, he returned to Shanghai from Songjiang by car.

(Departure North)

Archbishop Cai Ning returned to Shanghai last night and is scheduled to depart north on the Shanghai-Beiping through train at 4:05 PM today. Archbishop Cai, along with Consultant Antonius Yu, will be on board. Shanghai bishops, priests, believers, and students will go to the North Railway Station to bid farewell, and the Zhengxiu Primary and Secondary School military band will play music at the station to add to the sendoff. The through train is expected to arrive in Yanzhou, Shandong, at 3:30 PM on the 30th. At the invitation of Bishop Han of the district, Mr. Cai will stay for one day. On the 31st, he will hold a Mass in the Yanzhou church and preside over the Holy Eucharist procession. He will take the train at Shenshi (3-5 PM) and continue north. He is expected to arrive in Tianjin at 7:00 AM on June 1st. All circles in Tianjin will hold a grand welcome meeting. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has telegraphed the resident office in Tianjin to host the welcome. Mr. Cai is scheduled to go to Beiping on the afternoon of the 2nd to take office at the Apostolic Delegation to China at No. 6, Nai Zifu Jia.

(Broadcasting Farewell)

At 4:05 PM today, when Special Envoy Cai departs north, the Supervisory Office of the National Catholic Action Association in Shanghai will specially broadcast a farewell program from 4:00 PM to 5:00 PM at the Guohua Radio Station to wish him a safe journey. It will also report the itinerary of Special Envoy Cai to the faithful along the Jinghu-Tianjin-Beiping-Yushu (Northeast) lines, so that they can go to the nearest stations to welcome and pay their respects. Also, because the birthday of the Roman Pope is on the 31st, birthday greetings will be included in the songs. The call sign of the radio station is XHHN, with a frequency of 1200 kilocycles. The program is as follows: (1) Play the Departure March; (2) Report on the departure and pray for a safe journey; (3) Report on the grand welcome by the Shanghai faithful; (4) Sing the welcome song, "Report the Gospel to the Brothers"; (5) Report on the audience with the Chairman of the National Government and the grand banquet by Shanghai officials and gentry; (6) Sing the welcome song, "Welcome! Welcome!"; (7) Report on Sheshan pilgrimage and the news of the special envoy's departure north; (8) Sing "Victory Song of Quito"; (9) Celebrate the Pope's birthday; (10) Sing "Long Live the Pope"; (11) Musical Recessional.

Gu Yubo, Lin Kanghou, and Others Established Daxin Industrial Bank; Basic Capital of One Million Yuan; All Shares Fully Subscribed; Grand Opening in September 126

Mr. Gu Yubo, the Chinese manager of the insurance department of the China Business Company, gathered financial giants Lin Kanghou, Yu Zuoting, Xu Jichin, Qian Chengxu, and others in April of this year to launch a large-scale bank, named Daxin Industrial Bank, with a capital fund of one million yuan, fully paid up at one time. The preparations are now nearing completion. The details are as follows:

Origin of Establishment: The origin of the establishment of Daxin Industrial Bank is rooted in the fact that since the winds of economic recession in Europe and the United States have spread across the globe, the economic aggression of the powers against our country has intensified. Looking back at our country, banditry has not been eliminated, internal strife is frequently heard, and natural disasters 灾 and man-made calamities are intertwined. Others scheme against us in such a way, while our own lack of vigor is such that the national economy is becoming increasingly dire. Thus, cash is concentrated in the cities, while the countryside is on the verge of bankruptcy. Because of the bankruptcy of the countryside, the decline of all industries is accelerated. If this continues, the future crisis is truly unspeakable. To remedy this, passively, obstacles must be removed to reduce the burden on the people, and actively, resources must be pooled to jointly plan economic construction. However, in terms of construction, it is imperative to discern the urgency and divide the steps. In the past, agricultural products could be directly transported and sold in cities, and banks could regulate their finances. But now that the countryside is on the verge of bankruptcy, its agricultural products are unable to be transported and are stagnating, which has a huge impact on the cities. The way to remedy this lies in the banks penetrating deep into the countryside, assisting them, and seeking the improvement of the countryside, which is the most urgent task at present. In addition, developing inland resources and studying Northwest affairs are also the wishes of this bank. However, at the beginning of the establishment, it is felt that the resources are weak, but if we can approach it with perseverance, then who knows if the Northwest cause will not progress from research work to actual development? (The following is omitted) Northwest Support: Daxin Industrial Bank was initiated by Mr. Gu Yubo, and twenty-seven financial figures in Shanghai, including Lin Kanghou, Chen Liting, Zheng Hongnian, Qian Chengxu, Shen Jingzhong, Fan Dusheng, Shao Daren, and Chen Yaonan, all unanimously joined as founders. Mr. Gu personally went to Mr. Yu Youren to express his opinions on this matter, which was deeply appreciated by President Yu. Yu Zuoting, Xu Jichin, Jiang Baili, Tang Haian, Xu Fu, and others all unanimously served as supporters. Mr. Gu, in view of the urgency of developing the Northwest, specially telegraphed the Northwest authorities and consulted back and forth, which has received the full support of the Northwest authorities. He specially telegraphed Mr. Fan Dusheng, an important figure in the Northwest, to go south to participate in the preparations. Mr. Fan has arrived in Shanghai and has been in contact with Mr. Gu for several days, progressing smoothly. The preparatory office has been set up at No. 302, Guohua Building.

Subscription of Shares: The bank is a joint-stock limited company, with a capital of one million yuan temporarily set. Seven-tenths have been subscribed by the founders, and three-tenths have been subscribed by the Northwest side. Therefore, the basic capital of one million yuan has been fully subscribed. The head office will be established in Shanghai, and branches will also be established in important commercial ports of various provinces. Its business includes deposits, loans, remittances, discounts, foreign exchange, buying and selling securities, and safe deposit boxes, as well as savings. The shares are divided into one hundred yuan per share, with a total of ten thousand shares. Shareholders with more than thirty shares may be elected as directors, and shareholders with more than ten shares may be elected as supervisors. The collection of shares will be handled by the Central Bank, the Bank of Communications, the Shanghai Women's Bank, the Shanghai Municipal Bank, and Hengxun, Yichang, and other money shops, from May 20th to the end of July, as the share payment period. The official opening is scheduled for September. The location of the head office is approximately on Nanjing Road.

Summary of Dangerous Riverbank Projects in Jiangxi Province 131

Last year, the China Relief Society jointly organized the Fuyou and Dayou major work relief projects in Jiangxi with the China Morality Society. The Relief Society also jointly organized the Jiangxi Nanchang Guangfeng Weiju Dike Project with the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Society and the Morality Society, including the construction of water gates and the construction of the Wanshe Bridge. The Weiju Dike project used more than 70,000 yuan in relief funds. According to reports from the dike directors Huang Wenzhi and others of Gan Province, the Xihu Dike in Gan Province is the most important dike in the province and is of great importance. Although it is now well-built, there are many dangerous areas. The most dangerous areas have been built and collapsed repeatedly in the past, which can serve as a lesson. To make it permanent, it is necessary to stack boulders along the base of the dike to provide protection. The conference has great merits and virtues, and it is proposed to specially maintain it, select dangerous areas to purchase stones and stack them, so as to resist wind and waves and achieve lasting peace. The Weiju Dike is a very large and dangerous project in Nanchang, Jiangxi. Stacking boulders is to prevent water surges and wind waves. The association previously sent Director Li Yunmen to investigate and estimate the price of boulders at about 30,000 to 40,000 yuan. The association has undertaken too many work relief projects in recent years, and the relief funds have been exhausted, making it difficult to continue. Now that spring water is rising, dangerous projects are in danger, and the lives of dike residents are at stake, as are the interests of farmland. We hope that charitable people at home and abroad will help each other, save lives, and benefit farmland, which is related to the national economy and people's livelihood. With everyone's efforts, it is easy to lift, and with the accumulation of small things, it becomes a great achievement. Saving people is truly more meritorious than building a seven-level pagoda.

The Grass and Wool Hat Industry Association Requests an Increase in Import Duties on Foreign Goods; The Ministry of Industry Has Consulted the Ministry of Finance and the Tariff Commission to Handle It 132

The Tax Office States That Import Wool Hats Are Taxed Ad Valorem

The Shanghai Grass and Wool Hat Industry Association stated that in recent years, foreign goods have been flooding the market, with falling prices and dumping, resulting in the gradual decline of the Chinese grass hat industry. Factories cannot support themselves and have closed down one after another. In order to provide relief, they have specially submitted requests to the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Finance, the Tax Department, and the Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, requesting a thorough investigation of the value of foreign

imported wool hats, to tax them ad valorem, and to increase the import tax on grass and wool hats, so as to save the decline and maintain domestic goods. The details are as follows:

(Submission to the Ministry of Industry) 133

Submission requesting an increase in the import tax on foreign wool hats. According to repeated statements from factory members, the Chinese wool hat industry has always been difficult to develop due to the flooding of foreign goods. Recently, foreign prices have plummeted, and foreign wool hats have been imported into our country, making competition even more fierce. As a result, the business of the Chinese wool hat industry is declining, making it impossible for each factory member to support itself. The association believes that the Chinese industry is still young. Most of the raw materials used for wool hats are supplied from foreign countries. When these raw materials are imported, import duties should be paid according to regulations. When the raw materials are made into wool hats and exported for sale, export duties must also be paid.

It is not like importing foreign goods, which only requires paying import duties, which is a lighter burden. A lighter burden makes it easier to promote sales, and a heavier burden makes competition difficult. Therefore, the ease of dumping foreign goods and the difficulty of developing domestic goods are closely related to the weight of taxation. The association is a Shanghai wool hat industry group and cannot sit idly by while the industry is collapsing. After careful discussion and repeated consideration by each factory member, we submit a document to the Ministry, requesting that the tax rate on foreign imported wool hats be increased, so that foreign wool hats will be difficult to compete with, and domestic wool hats will be able to promote sales. The people's livelihood and industry will be dependent on this. We are extremely urgent.

(Submission to the Tax Department) 134

Submission requesting a thorough investigation of the value of foreign imported wool hats, to tax them ad valorem, in order to be fair. According to reports from factory members, the import of foreign wool hats is taxed at 40% according to the national tariff. However, the customs' tax assessment standard is often based on the bank remittance documents and invoices of the goods. There are many who report the actual value of the remittance price or the invoice sent, but there are also many who use cunning tricks, i.e. remit only half of the total value of the goods, with the other half being an account receivable, or report only half of the invoice value, thereby obscuring

the customs, so as to reduce their taxes. For example, when foreign wool hats are imported, each dozen is taxed based on an estimated customs value of only 3 to 5 yuan based on the remittance or invoice, while the market price is more than 10 to 20 yuan in national currency.

This can be clearly proven. When competing with domestic wool hats in business, domestic goods will inevitably suffer greatly, and the customs' tax collection will also lose its fair principle. The association is a hat industry group and must state the facts to the Tax Department for the sake of the interests of the industry. We sincerely request that you investigate and verify the wholesale price of foreign imported wool hats on the market in the future, and use it to collect taxes, so as to be fair. If the customs cannot determine the value by itself, you may send a letter to the association, and we will investigate it on your behalf,

or purchase the same goods directly from the source for reference, so as not to lose fairness. We would be very grateful.

(Original Approval Orders) 135

(1) Approval order from the Ministry of Industry: The submission has been noted. We have consulted the Ministry of Finance and forwarded it to the National Tariff Commission for consideration when revising the tariff. Please be informed of this approval. (2) Approval order from the Tax Department: The submission has been noted. The fact that the factory has made this report shows that it is concerned about tax revenue, which is commendable. However, the points mentioned seem to be unclear about the facts. The customs assess the value of imported wool hats based on real-time market prices. According to the assessment files, the tax-paid price per dozen is mostly between 8 yuan and 30 yuan in customs gold units, and not 3 yuan to 5 yuan as stated in the submission. If the factory can truthfully report a certain shipment that was hastily valued by the customs, resulting in a low price, we would be happy to hear it. This approval. (3) Approval order from the Customs Superintendent: It concerns the investigation of market prices for import wool hats for taxation, which has been approved by the Tax Department.

News on the Anglo-American Tobacco Factory Strike Yesterday; The Strike Committee Petitioned Yesterday; The Social Affairs Bureau Will Mediate Today 137

According to the Dagong News Agency, the Anglo-American Tobacco Factory strike remains at a stalemate. The Strike Committee

petitioned the Party Department yesterday, and the Social Affairs Bureau is scheduled to convene a mediation meeting today. The details are as follows:

Calling for Questioning: The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, believing that the Anglo-American strike is a serious matter, reported to the Municipal Government for instructions on how to handle it and decided to convene a mediation committee this morning (29th) to conduct mediation. However, in order to solicit the opinions of the workers, the Bureau first summoned the labor union leaders Chen Peide, Lou Jingguan, and others to the Bureau for questioning at 11:00 AM yesterday. Wang Gang, the director of the mediation section, met with them. After inquiring in detail about the strike situation, he ordered the workers' representatives to send official representatives to the Bureau tomorrow (today) to await mediation. However, he hoped that the dispute would not be expanded to avoid causing accidents.

Meeting of the Strike Committee: The Strike Committee convened its third meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday. Thirty-nine strike committee members attended. Chairman Chen Peide reported on Chairman Chiang's telegram to the municipal Party and government organs, setting a deadline for resumption of work. However, he hoped that the strike would not be expanded and that there would be an orderly struggle before the strike was resolved. Then, the following were discussed: (1) A proposal to appoint representatives to attend the mediation meeting convened by the Social Affairs Bureau tomorrow. Resolution: Chen Peide and Lou Jingguan were appointed as representatives, and other strike committee members attended as observers. (2) A proposal to invite all sectors in Pudong to provide assistance in the afternoon. Resolution: Passed. (3) A proposal to notify all workers to strictly observe order before the strike is resolved. Resolution: Transferred to the Maintenance Section. (4) A proposal to ask workers from the three factories to express the same opinion. Resolution: Omitted. The meeting adjourned.

Expanding Propaganda: Workers at the factory convened a propaganda meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday. It was decided to expand the organization of the propaganda meeting, with Fei Keguang appointed as director, Wang Ajin as commander, and Hong Maoquan, Zhang Zhenxuan, Tang Jintang, and Zhang Awu as squadron leaders. Each squadron was divided into three detachments, with twenty people in each detachment. All departed immediately to expand propaganda in various districts, requesting all sectors to stop buying and smoking various cigarettes produced by the company before the strike is resolved. In addition, the female workers' propaganda team also departs in batches every day to promote awareness, so as to attract social attention.

Declaration from the Industrial Sector: Pudong labor unions issued a joint declaration yesterday to support Anglo-American workers, stating that the Anglo-American Tobacco Company in Pudong suddenly and without reason closed its factory without the approval of our national Party and government organs, intending to dismiss a large number of workers who have worked the longest and have the highest wages, in order to evade the pensions of each worker, and falsely accusing the workers of not being obedient to command, leading to a collective strike and resistance, forcing them to extremes. The situation has been going on for many days, but the company has not yet woken up. If this continues, how can the workers' livelihoods be imagined? Moreover, we fear that once this bad example is set, other capitalists will follow suit, and the compatriots of other factories will become the Anglo-American workers of today. Thinking about the future, we cannot help but feel chilled. The labor unions deeply feel the pain and are duty-bound to go through fire and water. Therefore, from today onwards, we will notify all workers to uphold the determination not to buy, sell, or transport products of the Anglo-American Tobacco Company, so as to urge the company to wake up and restore the factory. That is when the labor unions withdraw their decision. We sincerely declare this, and we beg for the public's judgment. The Italian Postal Company's Cargo Ship Finally Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday, Delayed by Two Weeks, Cargo Undamaged 140

The Italian postal company cargo ship "Cortellina" arrived from Europe carrying over 20,000 pieces of cargo destined for China. Originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 15th of this month, it unexpectedly ran aground off the coast of Annam due to fog. The shipowner telegraphed Shanghai to report the grounding and that the ship would be out of service. However, the telegram did not specify the reason, so the Shanghai company telegraphed for clarification. Subsequently, the coastal authorities managed to salvage the cargo ship. After a lengthy towing process, it was freed from the shoal. The shipowner inspected the hull and found no major damage, so it continued its voyage to Shanghai, finally arriving yesterday. However, the arrival was delayed by two weeks. Among the cargo on board, cotton was the most abundant, totaling 20,000 bales, all purchased by Japanese merchants, possibly for transshipment to the Orient. The remaining 300 tons of cargo were unloaded in Shanghai. The cargo did not suffer any damage from the grounding and unloading commenced today.

Obstacles on the Jianghai Shipping Routes, Hydrographic Office Notifies Merchants to Take Caution 141

Bai Mao Sandbar Enlarges: The Bai Mao Sandbar at the mouth of the Yangtze River is a vital passage for ships navigating the Yangtze. Recently, the Bai Mao Sandbar has suddenly expanded, extending southwest along the river for a significant two nautical miles. The expanded sandbar is located at 121 degrees 13 minutes East longitude and 31 degrees 40 minutes North latitude. The endpoint has a depth of five zhe, located 93 degrees due north of the Tang Saikou beacon. Fearing that passing merchant ships might be affected without knowing, the Hydrographic Office has issued an urgent notice to all ships.

Jigu Reef Obstruction: Jigu Reef outside the Wusong Estuary is a commonly navigated area for ships traveling between the Northern and Southern Seas. Recently, the British ship "Hilltmarle" was entering the port when it encountered an obstruction of submerged objects in the sea near Jigu Reef, at 170 degrees due north, approximately one and three-quarters nautical miles, 122 degrees 23 minutes East longitude and 31 degrees 9 minutes North latitude. This obstruction poses a hazard to ships. What the object is remains unknown. The Naval Hydrographic Office plans to dispatch a vessel to survey the area. In the meantime, ships are being notified to exercise extra caution when navigating the area.

Public Association Candidate Committee Member Promoted to Executive Committee Member, Completing Term, Not Eligible for Re-election According to Law 143

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously inquired with the Social Affairs Bureau regarding whether a candidate committee member, upon filling the term of a predecessor and the next election, would be subject to the restriction of not being eligible for re-election. The following response has been received: "Acknowledged. Upon investigation, if a candidate committee member has been promoted according to law, then the date of completion, regardless of length, naturally means that they are subject to the same restriction as official committee members of not being eligible for re-election at the next election. Please notify accordingly."

(Government and Business Jointly Operated) 145

The Agricultural and Commercial Bank was originally established in Beijing during Gao Lingwei's tenure as Minister of Agriculture, with a paid-up capital of 1.73 million yuan and the right to issue banknotes. Rental Dispute in Xicheng Lane Heard Yesterday, Court Scheduled to Open Trial Today, Tenants Held a General Meeting Yesterday 152

The rental dispute in Xicheng Lane at the intersection of Ximen Road and Maran Road in the French Concession is scheduled to be heard by the court today. The tenants held a general meeting yesterday to discuss the matter and notified all tenants to attend the court hearing. It is said that various groups have also sent representatives to attend and observe the proceedings. The details are recorded below:

Court Hearing: The landlord, Yi Yuan Company, filed a lawsuit with the Second Special District Court against 36 tenants for refusing to sign a contract. Through lawyer Wu Zhenming, the company requested the court to order the tenants to vacate the premises on the grounds that they had not signed a lease agreement, and requested a preliminary execution. The court accepted the lawsuit and scheduled a hearing for 2 PM today in the Sixth Court. The tenants have engaged barrister Wu Kaisheng to represent them in court. The tenants themselves will be in court to await the hearing.

Tenants General Meeting: The lane's branch convened a temporary emergency general meeting last night at 8 PM at the Citizen's Fourth Branch in Anxin Temple, Bailan Road. Over a hundred people attended, with Li Ruzhang as chairman and Yu Jingqing as secretary. After reporting the purpose of the meeting, the following resolutions were passed: (1) During the court hearing today, in addition to barrister Wu Kaisheng representing them in court, all 36 tenant households will attend the hearing. The remaining tenants will attend to observe the proceedings. (2) The fraudulent rent receipts will be collected on the spot and submitted as evidence during the court hearing, and a lawsuit for false accusation will be filed separately. (3) The new contract will be universally denied because its terms are harsh and there is no legal basis for it. (4) The presiding judge is requested to pay attention to the plaintiff's lawsuit to find out under which legal regulations the accusation is based. (5) The landlord's second contradictory notice will be presented, and the presiding judge will be requested to reject the plaintiff's unreasonable lawsuit. (6) The presiding judge is requested to reserve the right to claim damages and file a counterclaim separately. (7) All tenants are notified to pay attention. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Notification to Tenants: The lane's branch announced to all tenants yesterday:

"Regarding the landlord's unreasonable lawsuit, the court has scheduled a hearing for 2 PM today (the 29th) at the Sixth Court of the Second Special District Court on Xuehuali Road, Lujiawan. All tenants who have been sued must attend the hearing on time and bring a recent rent receipt as evidence. All tenants who have not been sued, because they may be forced to sign the new contract, must also attend to observe the proceedings to strengthen our resolve and clarify the facts. This is an urgent notice, please pay attention."

Observers from Various Circles: The Rent Reduction Committee of this city, the Citizen's Association of the First Special District, and the Citizen's Association of the Second Special District, and various district branches, consider this case to be of great importance. It is reported that they have sent representatives to attend the court hearing today to observe the proceedings.

Itinerant Magicians Have Many Tricks, Even Mud Bodhisattvas Can Speak, Six Gold Sovereigns and a Gold Box Lost, Clerk of a Cloth Store Tricked Repeatedly, Pitiful and Laughable 160

Gu Dehua, a 34-year-old from Suzhou, has been working as a clerk at the Gongyi Foreign Cloth Store at 520 Tianjin Road. He has no past faults and is trusted by the manager. On the 7th of this month, Gu was visiting a friend at the Far Eastern Hotel on Xizang Road when he saw a sign hanging in front of room 214 of the hotel, which read "Huan You Ke" (Itinerant Official), a fortune teller. He could not help but be moved by curiosity, and immediately knocked on the door and entered, asking for his fortune to be told. At that time, a young man in the room saw Gu arrive, quickly stood up and offered him a seat. After a brief conversation, the young man claimed to be Zhao Zhewun, only 24 years old, originally from Nanjing, and a disciple of Huan You Ke. He said that his master was away on business, and boasted that he had obtained his master's secrets and could inherit his mantle. Gu was thus

swayed by sweet words 161

and asked him to tell his fortune. Zhao touched Gu's facial features and both hands, and then spoke nonsense, saying that Gu's fate was extremely bad. If he wanted to avoid misfortune and seek good fortune, he would have to resolve the stars, otherwise disasters would frequently occur, and he would inevitably face great calamities, etc. Gu asked how much it would cost. Zhao asked for a fortune-telling fee of four yuan and eight dimes, but if he wanted to resolve the stars, he would have to prepare six gold sovereigns. This matter was important, and his master should perform the ritual himself. He then arranged for Gu to meet with his master on the 9th to discuss the matter. Gu paid the fortune-telling fee and left. On the 9th, he went as agreed. In addition to Zhao, there was another person sitting in the room. Gu thought that this person might be Huan You Ke, but after they exchanged names, he knew that it was not him.

Also a Fortune Teller 162

His real name was Ding Hongyuan, and his signboard name was Dongfang Bo. His residence was at No. 62, Lane 58, Minti Niyin Road in the French Concession. Dongfang Bo's itinerant magic was more skilled than Zhao's. Before he could finish a few words, Gu obeyed him. He immediately did as he was instructed, going outside to buy a mud sculpture of a small Bodhisattva, placing it in an empty cigarette can, lining the can with yellow cloth, and wrapping it in red silk. After Gu had wrapped the can, Dongfang Bo told him to hold the can to his ear and ask a question, and the can would definitely answer. Gu first asked his name and age, and indeed he vaguely heard an answer, and the answer was correct. Gu could not help but

was overjoyed 163

Then he asked if he could get rich. Unexpectedly, the answer was that he would be able to make 300,000 in wealth in the future. Gu was even more ecstatic. In fact, at this time, Gu's psychological state had changed greatly due to Dongfang Bo's words. The so-called answer from the can was purely from Dongfang Bo, who was standing next to Gu, taking advantage of the gap when Gu's mind was not distracted. Gu was bewitched by the sweet words, and those involved in the matter were blinded, and he deeply believed in the supernatural. Dongfang Bo saw that Gu had taken the bait, and continued to advise Gu to resolve the stars and quickly prepare the gold sovereigns as needed. By the 11th, Gu spent 127 yuan and four dimes to get

five gold sovereigns 164

Holding them, he went to the Far East. The magicians also ordered him to place the gold sovereigns in an empty cigarette can and accompany them to the Suzhou Creek, where they threw the can into the river, saying that this was the method of resolving the stars. In fact, the gold sovereigns in the can had already been stolen in secret. However, the magicians had originally asked for six gold sovereigns, but Gu had only given them five, so they ordered him to prepare the remaining one by the 15th to avoid losing all his previous efforts. On the due date, Gu brought the gold sovereign, but the magicians had already left the Far East and set up a secret room at the Great China Hotel, Room 425. When Gu arrived, the magicians still ordered him to do as before, going to the Bund of Edward Road by the river, and again

They made him toss the can

into the Huangpu 165

Unexpectedly, he was deceived twice, but he was still not aware of it. Dongfang Bo and others continued to deceive him, saying that he still needed a gold box in the shape of a matchbox, containing 85 yuan in banknotes, for application. Gu did not dare to disobey, and prepared it on the 21st. At this time, the magicians had changed the room to Room 445. After they met, they still went to the Huangpu River, and Dongfang Bo threw the box remotely. In a flash, the real thing was in his pocket, and they went back to their residence. In the period from May 7 to the 21st, Gu lost a total of 534 yuan. The funds were

secretly taken from the business 166

and his colleagues told the manager, and he questioned Gu and told him why he was deceived. Gu didn't believe it at first, but then he suspected, so he went to the Far East Hotel on the 26th to negotiate with the magicians and ask for the money back. Unexpectedly, Dongfang Bo and others relied on their strength and numbers at that time, and not only did they not return the money, but they forced Gu to agree that the money was given voluntarily. Gu did not dare to resist at that time. Ye Xiaoying, a young girl from Shaoxing, 29 years old and graceful, met Zhang Zhonghe, a local youth (currently 21 years old and employed at the Jianghai Customs) last year, and immediately fell in love at first sight. When yesterday evening came, Zhang made an excuse to go out and did not return for a long time. Xiaoying, deeply infatuated, thought that Zhang Zhonghe was an ungrateful person. She immediately summoned the tea room attendant, gave them one silver dollar, and bought opium to swallow. After 8 PM, she went to room 540 on the same floor, where her close friend had opened a room, and inquired about Zhang's whereabouts. Suddenly, her complexion changed drastically, and her tone became abnormal. Her girlfriend's husband, Mr. Huang, noticed this, interrogated her severely, and she finally revealed the truth. She was rushed to the Baolong Hospital for treatment.

Inland River Steamships Repeatedly Robbed; Trade Association Petitions for Strict Arrest 169

The Hengji steamship of the China Merchants Inland River Steamship Bureau on North Suzhou Road in this city was robbed by bandits at Zhangjiakou, where Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces meet, at the end of last month, suffering heavy losses. They had reported it to the local authorities, requesting investigation and arrest to ensure the safety of travelers, but it has not yet been apprehended. On the 25th of this month, the Lisun steamship of the Lixing Steamship Bureau, running the Shanghai-Lake route, was robbed by more than ten bandits speaking a local accent and carrying weapons at the same location while returning from the lake to Shanghai. More than ten pieces of passenger cargo were lost, the account money in the accounting room and passengers' clothes were swept away. After an hour, they whooped and boarded a prepared small boat and left. Not long after, the Liji steamship of the China Merchants Bureau, also returning from the lake to Shanghai, was also robbed by bandits. After checking the losses, it amounted to about three or four thousand yuan. After the two bureaus had the incident, they immediately prepared documents to petition the local authorities for strict arrest, and also requested the Inland River Steamship Industry Association to present separate petitions to Chen, the chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, Lu, the chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, and Liu, the captain of the Zhejiang Water Police Security Team, requesting them to promptly dispatch officers to investigate and arrest, to ensure the safety of travelers, and attached a list of losses. The above petitions were sent by telegraph yesterday.

April's Foreign Trade Deficit Exceeds 59 Million Yuan; Surplus of Raw Gold and Silver is Also Very Large 170

The International Trade Bureau announced yesterday the general situation of international trade in April, saying that the foreign trade situation in April this year was prosperous in sales and transfers, but still felt weakened compared to the same period last year. The total import volume in April was 100,960,369 yuan, and the total export volume was 41,123,563 yuan, resulting in a deficit of 59,836,806 yuan. Imports increased by 1,532,354 yuan compared to the previous month, and exports also increased by 1,008,142 yuan. The cumulative deficit for the four months of this year has reached 218,555,681 yuan, a decrease of 30.51% compared to the same period last year. The details are as follows:

Imports and Exports by Country: In terms of imports and exports by country, there have been no major changes compared to the past. The United States still maintains the top spot for imports, followed by Japan, and then England and Germany. In terms of exports, the United States also ranks first, followed by Hong Kong, then Japan and England. Exports to Russia this month also reached 1,623,755 yuan, an increase of 1,541,712 yuan in exports compared to the previous month, which is gratifying for the people of the country. Although exports to Japan this month have increased slightly, the number is extremely small. However, Japan's imports to us have increased by 3.9% compared to the previous month, and its trend of progress is indeed worthy of attention.

Imports and Exports by Port: In terms of imports and exports by port this month, Shanghai alone reached more than 59 million yuan in imports, a decrease of more than 6 million yuan compared to the previous month, while exports increased by nearly 2 million yuan. In other places such as Tianjin, exports decreased while imports increased, which is the result of Japanese goods dumping. The general situation in Guangzhou, Jiaozhou, and other places is stable, but the exports of Hankou Port are still extremely sluggish, while imports have increased, which is not optimistic.

Major Imports: In terms of major imported goods this month, cotton accounted for 6,007,815 gold units, hardware accounted for 5,383,368 gold units, rice accounted for 4,655,846 gold units, wheat accounted for 1,977,732 gold units, cotton cloth accounted for 1,703,315 gold units, sugar accounted for 1,139,588 gold units, and kerosene accounted for 1,006,430 gold units. The import volume of various commodities has declined compared to the previous month. Compared with the same period last year, except for an increase of more than one million gold units in hardware imports and a slight increase of 600,000 gold units in cotton, the other commodities have mostly decreased, especially wheat, kerosene, and rice, which is indeed a good phenomenon.

Major Exports: In terms of major export commodities, fur accounted for 4,529,150 yuan, tea accounted for 1,506,003 yuan, egg products accounted for 2,455,144 yuan, cotton yarn accounted for 1,756,572 yuan, raw silk accounted for 1,740,723 yuan, and tung oil accounted for 1,718,591 yuan. Compared with the previous month, the export value of various commodities has mostly increased, except for a slight decrease in fur and cotton yarn. Compared with the same period last year, tea, fur, and egg products have increased, while raw silk, cotton yarn, and tung oil have decreased.

Surplus of Raw Gold and Silver: As for the export of gold and silver, the import of silver coins and raw silver this month totaled 388,945 yuan, while the export was 15,152,635 yuan. There were no imports of gold coins and raw gold, while exports reached 2,798,139 gold units. In total, the surplus of raw silver and silver coins was 15,541,580 yuan, and the surplus of raw gold and gold coins was 2,798,139 gold units.

Match Prices Raised Consistently in Six Provinces: Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hubei, Hunan, and Jiangxi 171

Increase Rate Varies for Each Brand; Further Price Increases Are Planned Successively

China's match industry has been greatly affected by the dumping of foreign matches, and its business has been extremely depressed. More than 20 manufacturers in Hebei and Shandong provinces have gone bankrupt as a result. The National Match Industry Federation, in view of this, organized a Match Price Maintenance Association in order to maintain business. In addition to holding a meeting last month to discuss organizational methods, it reconvened member manufacturers the day before yesterday (the 25th) to discuss ways to increase prices. According to Mr. Dong Shaolin, the secretary-general of the association, who spoke to a Dagongshe reporter yesterday, the Match Price Maintenance Committee is organized by match manufacturers in the six provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hubei, Jiangxi and Hunan, and has decided to implement the increase in match prices in the above six provinces starting from the 25th of this month. The increase rate varies for each brand of match, approximately ranging from one-tenth to five-tenths of the original price. Further price increases are planned successively within the possible range.

Shanghai Municipal Council's Public Bonds to be Issued on Schedule; Explanation by the Head of the Finance Department 172

The Shanghai Municipal Council has now decided to issue public bonds for 7 million yuan, which is part of the 15.5 million yuan in bonds authorized by this year's taxpayers' annual meeting. According to the Head of the Finance Department's explanation to the Finance Committee, he has carefully considered the interest rate for this new public bond. If the general economic situation improves, it will definitely affect the current low interest rates. Therefore, he suggests that for the long term, this bond should be fixed for 10 to 30 years, with an annual interest rate of 5%, and the funds received at the time of issuance will exceed the face value by 2.5%. According to this calculation, the annual interest rate for investors, calculated for 30 years, is approximately 4.84%. As for the repayment of principal, it will be done according to the use of the fund. However, the bonds from 1924, 1925, 1926, and 1927 should be repaid first. The 1924 public bond has been scheduled to be repaid on December 31st of this year. It seems that an opportunity can be given to the registered ticket holders to convert the bond into a new public bond. The terms of conversion will be formulated later. The new public bonds will be issued in the Chinese standard silver coins commonly used in this city. Regarding the weight and fineness of the silver coins, he believes that there is no need to explain further, because if regulations are added, taxpayers will inevitably have to prepare another fund to guarantee the fineness of the silver coins. Moreover, the credit of the Municipal Council is better today than ever before, and there is no need to adopt this dangerous principle. The opening of the new public bonds is scheduled to take place on May 31st. The Head of the Finance Department also stated that the registration and transfer of the Municipal Council's public bonds has always been free of charge. However, in view of the complexity of the transfer procedures, the expenditure on office expenses cannot but be increased. He believes that in the future, the general practice can be followed and a handling fee can be charged. He suggests that starting from this year's new public bonds, a fee of one yuan per bond will be charged for the transfer of bonds. All of the above suggestions have been adopted by the Finance Committee and approved by the Board of Directors for implementation.

Establishing the Shanghai United Regatta Preparatory Committee: The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo-Qiantang Railway Bureaus hosted leaders of universities and sports organizations in Shanghai at the Qingyang Port Railway Garden Hotel on May 27th. At 9:00 AM, Deputy Director Wu Shaozeng of the Railway Bureau and senior officials of the bureau, along with representatives from the two railway sports associations, accompanied them by car from the North Station. After arriving at Qingyang Port, a tea party was held in the Garden Hotel. Deputy Director Wu stood up to give a speech, saying that it was an honor to have the representatives present. Director Huang of their bureau had originally planned to come to host them, but he was not feeling well this morning and could not attend. He asked Shaozeng to apologize on his behalf and welcomed everyone with the utmost respect. He said that there were two meanings to inviting everyone today: (1) Today is the second day of the regatta held by foreigners at Qingyang Port, and it happens to be the fifth day of the opening of the Qingyang Port Garden Hotel of their railway. He invited everyone to come here for sightseeing, provide guidance, and take the opportunity to visit the grand regatta. (2) Their bureau believes that the railway's most important task is of course the issue of travel for the general public. At the same time, it also has a considerable mission in promoting education and various social issues, especially in promoting outdoor sports. Today, he wants to discuss it with everyone. Rowing competitions are a full-body exercise and can demonstrate the spirit of cooperation, which is very beneficial. Qingyang Port is an excellent location for regattas. Foreigners hold regattas here every year, but Chinese people do not have this sport. Their bureau believes that the biggest problem with today's Chinese youth is their physical weakness. The way to remedy this is to promote equal emphasis on physical training and academic research, and to replace improper entertainment with entertainment that benefits the body. Also, because Chinese people's habits are more inclined towards stillness than activity, outdoor and active entertainment should be promoted. Therefore, he especially invited everyone to exchange opinions. It seems that rowing competitions can be promoted. If you agree, please promote it together. Their bureau will do its best to assist within the possible range. For example, all arrangements and equipment can be handled by their bureau. Each time you travel by train, their bureau can provide considerable preferential treatment. However, the only hope they have is to enable young people to use their holidays to engage in sports here and spend some time outdoors, so that diligent students do not confine themselves to small rooms all day long, and dissolute people do not only go to dance halls and theaters, in order to benefit their bodies and minds. However, they do not want to tempt young people with the beautiful facilities and comfortable services of the Garden Hotel and increase their consumption. This point should be solemnly stated in advance. On the fifth day of the fifth month of the Chinese lunar calendar, there is the Dragon Boat Festival. Now, the fifth day of the fifth month of the Gregorian calendar is the anniversary of the founding of the revolutionary government. It is also possible to designate this day as the day for rowing competitions, adopting the legacy of the Dragon Boat Festival and promoting the spirit of sports and cooperation among Chinese people, which seems to be very interesting and valuable. Subsequently, Mr. Weng Zhilong, Mr. Hu Wenyao, Mr. Ou Kuian, and Mr. Lao Jianshao successively expressed their opinions. It was decided to establish the Shanghai United Regatta Preparatory Committee on the spot, and Weng Zhilong (Tongji), Wang Fudan (Jiangnan), Pan Tinggan (Jiaotong), Yu Jie (Jinan), Wu Shijie (Fudan), Ou Kuian (Daxia), Zhu Shijun (Guanghua), and others were elected as preparatory committee members, with Weng Zhilong as the chief committee member. Then, the organizational and funding issues were discussed. It was decided that regarding the organizational issue, the articles of association should be drafted first, and Wang Fudan, Shen Guoquan, Yu Jie, Wu Shijie, and He Chunhui were appointed as committee members, with Wang Fudan as the chief committee member. Regarding the funding issue, a concrete plan should be drafted first, and Ou Kuian, Wang Fudan, Lao Jieming, Li Qiulin, Hu Wenyao, Lu Zhiming, and Cao Shengsan were appointed as committee members, with Wang Fudan as the chief committee member. It was also decided that a general meeting of representatives of universities and sports organizations would be held at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA at 9:00 AM on June 10th (Sunday) to determine organizational and economic issues and to carry out preparatory matters. The Railway Bureau will be responsible for preparing and sending out invitations for the dinner party. The tea party ended at 11:30 AM. The representatives toured the various parts of the hotel for a week. At noon, they had lunch under the hotel's veranda. After lunch, they took a steamboat to watch the foreign regatta and traveled downstream to the suburbs of Kunshan to enjoy the scenery on the water. At around 4:00 PM, they returned to the hotel by boat. On this day, the weather was clear and sunny, the flowers and trees in the garden were competing in beauty, the springs and rocks were displaying their charm, the clear waves on the harbor were sparkling with green, and the trees were flowing with splendor. In addition, the visitors attending the regatta were endless, and the tourists in the Garden Hotel were as knowledgeable as those in the countryside, which was truly an unprecedented spectacle.

Establishment of the Fuyin School Board of Directors 175

The Fuyin School for the Deaf and Mute at Kangjia Bridge on Xijesifei Road in this city was founded by Mr. Fu Bulan, the principal of the Hongqiao Road School for the Blind, according to the will of his father, Dr. Fu Lanya. Since its establishment eight years ago, it has achieved remarkable results. Its curriculum, equipment, specialized teachers, and novel teaching methods have long been praised by public opinion, which is unnecessary for us to elaborate on. It is now known that the school, in order to strive for perfection, rescue the disabled, and seek the development of this special education, has repeatedly invited charitable figures from all walks of life to serve as school directors to support it. Many major charities have also been able to enthusiastically support it and agree to serve as school directors. Therefore, a founding meeting was held in the school auditorium at 5:00 PM yesterday, and student achievements and speech performances were displayed to entertain the new directors. Those who attended included Zhu Shaoping, Wang Yiting, Pan Gongzhan, Chen Heqin, Zhang Ji, Mrs. Wu Tiecheng (represented by Ms. Yang Yixi), Zhang Jiongbo (represented by Ms. Zhang Hanpingqing), and more than a dozen others. Zhu Peide, Huang Shaoxiong, Wang Zhengting, and others were unable to attend due to other matters. Principal Fu presided over the meeting. First, the chairman reported the school's history, current situation, and future hopes as follows: In the autumn of the 15th year of the Republic of China, the Hangzhou School for the Deaf and Mute, due to lack of funds, asked the School for the Blind in Shanghai for help. In that year, a civil house in Kangjia Bridge on Xijesifei Road was rented as the school building, and the current Fuyin School for the Deaf and Mute was established. At that time, there were only a dozen students. It has been painstakingly managed to this day. Currently, there are a total of 63 male and female students. The school's operating expenses rely entirely on students paying tuition. However, the annual tuition of less than 7,000 yuan is far from covering the 9,000 yuan in expenses. There are eleven faculty and staff members, some of whom are graduates of specialized departments, some are graduates of art schools, some have studied at universities, and some are graduates of the school's normal school. Graduates of the normal school have served as teachers in schools for the deaf and mute in Harbin and Wuchang, two in each. One person is employed at this school (there is currently one normal school student). Many graduates of the school for the deaf and mute are working in the Commercial Press and the World Book Company, some are working as painters, some are working as pharmacists, some are teaching, and some are specializing in art. The rest are largely unknown. The hope for the future is to obtain a larger and better school building so that the disabled can be fully accommodated, and it is urgently necessary to establish a school foundation to seek the progress of the cause, which depends on the enthusiastic donations of the directors. After the chairman's report, Wang Yiting, Pan Gongzhan, Zhu Shaoping, Zhang Ji, Chen Heqin, and others successively gave speeches, mostly praising the school's achievements, admiring Mr. Fu's spirit of engaging in charitable education, and wishing him continued progress and success. After the speeches, Zhu Shaoping temporarily proposed to elect the chairman of the board of directors, and Mrs. Wu Tiecheng was immediately elected as chairman. The first meeting of the board of directors was held at the same time, and four resolutions were passed: (1) Everyone should donate money to help a certain number of students who cannot afford to pay tuition as a standard. (2) A letter should be sent to the municipal government requesting a donation of a piece of public land for the construction of a school building. (3) Director Pan should come forward and request a subsidy from the Municipal Bureau of Education. (4) Everyone should donate a certain amount of money on the spot. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM.

Verdict on the Red Pill Case on Haig Road: The Main Culprit is at Large, Accomplices Convicted 179

On the 16th of this month, detectives Li Acai and Xu Peichun of the French Police apprehended Li Guisheng, a Chongming native, at the intersection of Route Tenant and Route Pesson in the Route Tenant area, for privately selling red pills. They confiscated six bags of red pills, totaling 6,000 pills. According to Li's confession, the manufacturing site was located at No. 1, Lane 857, Haig Road. When the detectives rushed to the address to make arrests, the owners of the operation, Chen Ruisheng, Tang Songtao, and Liu Fu, had already fled upon hearing the news. Only one apprentice, Li Zhaoming, from Pudong, was apprehended. Manufacturing equipment and materials for red pills, such as red and white powder and coffee essence, were found under the floorboards behind the living room. They were handed over to the Second Special Court for public prosecution. The trial has concluded, and the sentencing date has been set. This information has been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday was the sentencing date. The police escorted the two criminals, Li and Cai, to the court. Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the criminal court and sentenced Li Guisheng to one year of imprisonment for transporting opium substitutes, along with a fine of 200 yuan. If the fine is not paid, he will serve one day of imprisonment for every two yuan. Cai Zhaoming was sentenced to six months of imprisonment for aiding in the manufacture of opium substitutes. The number of days spent in detention before the final verdict will be deducted from the imprisonment term at a rate of one day for one day. The confiscated red pill manufacturing equipment and materials will be confiscated according to the list.

Zhu Xingde Dies Suddenly: Blood and Foul Odor Detected 180

Zhu Xingde, a Ningbo native and tenant of the Rongyao Coal Company at No. 864 Zhu Family Warehouse on Haig Road in Western Shanghai, suddenly died yesterday for unknown reasons. The landlady, Madam Zhu Xu, discovered this and reported it to the Sixth District Police at 5:30 PM yesterday. Zhu Xingde (34 years old from Ningbo) had rented a room on the second floor a week ago Monday, introduced by Madam Fang, a tenant on the third floor. He paid six yuan for one month's rent and moved in with his wife. The next day, his wife left Shanghai to return to her hometown. Zhu was originally a head cook in a Westerner's household, but was currently unemployed and looking for a job. It was heard that he had found a job and was scheduled to start on June 1st. He did not go to the shop to get tea the night before and was not seen all day yesterday. This morning, Madam Fang on the third floor asked Madam Zhu Xu to tell Zhu that a maid had been hired. When Zhu had not come out by noon, she went to his room and suddenly found him dead in bed, with blood flowing from his mouth and a foul odor. His skin was slightly swollen, and flies were swarming around. The cause of death was unknown. After receiving the report, District Chief Tan immediately sent Officer Cheng and Service Personnel Yin to investigate. At the same time, he ordered the local police to report to the Local Court for an autopsy and further investigation.

Wuhua Bank's Five-Year Savings Plan

Since Wang Jian'e took office as the manager of the Baxianqiao branch of the Wuhua Bank, he has been actively preparing for its opening soon. It is also learned that Mr. Wang has recently launched a five-year savings plan. Regular bank savings accounts typically have a 15-year term, and depositing and withdrawing money can be difficult. The bank has shortened the term to five years. The calculation method uses a progressive or compound interest system. Withdrawals often have odd small amounts, so extra interest is added to calculate as a whole number. For example, depositing five yuan per month will result in 400 yuan in five years, and depositing 125 yuan per month will result in 10,000 yuan. This is divided into ten different amounts. Savings plans at other banks require depositing over 130 yuan per month to obtain 10,000 yuan after five years. Compared to others, this plan has four or five hundred yuan of surplus, truly starting a new era in savings.

Jishenghui's Good Medicine Benefits the World

The Chinese Jishenghui in this city distributes various epidemic prevention medicines every spring and summer. A medicine called Shishasan can treat seasonal illnesses and is extremely effective. Dip a lamp wick in the medicine and apply it to the corners of both eyes. Apply it to all four corners in severe cases. Do not be afraid of the pain when applying it. Apply it two or three more times until the illness improves and it is no longer painful. If it is not a seasonal illness, the medicine will not hurt when it enters the eye, and you must seek medical treatment elsewhere. Tearing and pain indicate that the medicine is reaching the dantian. Numbness and coldness in the limbs indicate that the illness is improving. Remember that this medicine must not be ingested, as it can harm your health. We are making this clear in case women and children do not know and use it by mistake. Please note that one bottle of this medicine can treat three or four people. The treatment is effective when the patient's limbs are no longer numb and cold and the body feels comfortable. The medicine packet contains wicks. Wet it with warm water before applying. If a child has infantile convulsion or is severely hot without tears, applying this medicine to the corners of the eyes can open the sensory orifices. If an adult collapses from a stroke, applying the medicine in this way can also help open the orifices and provide emergency relief. All children and adults with the above symptoms can be treated according to this method.

To the esteemed chief editor of Shenbao Newspaper,

I am writing to you in response to the article published in your newspaper on May 26 regarding the Li Ruisheng fraud case, which stated that "the suspect confessed in the Sixth District Public Security Bureau that the British-owned Xīn Jì Yángháng at the intersection of Five Malu and Jiangxi Road was rebranding inferior playing cards to deceive Chinese people," causing great consternation. The suspect fabricated the facts in an attempt to evade responsibility because his fraud was unsuccessful, which is worthy of abhorrence. In addition to requesting the court to severely punish him, we hereby request that you quickly correct this information in your newspaper. Sincerely, Card Department, Xīn Jì Yángháng, May 28th

Issue 11

Reading News Edited by Shenbao Circulation Library Reading Guidance Department

Table of Contents (1) To the Participants of the Reading Club (2) What We Hope Readers Will Pay Attention To

To the Participants of the Reading Club 193

The reading club that everyone has been eagerly awaiting has not yet been formally established. This not only causes everyone anxiety, but it also makes us feel ashamed. The slow and difficult birth of the reading club also has its reasons. We always feel that when starting a new endeavor, we must not be negligent and should have detailed plans and adequate preparations. Now, everything is basically ready, and we are just waiting for the Youth Association to determine the date of the general meeting so that we can start. Regarding our preparations and the preparations that readers should make before participating, we should make the following report to readers.

(Preparation Process) 194

Since the announcement of the reading club in the fifth issue of Reading News, we have been preparing for it every day. The details have also been announced successively, so there is no need to repeat them here. However, it is necessary to tell everyone about our cooperation with the Youth Association. After we decided to hold the reading club, we contacted the Youth Association to borrow a venue. It turned out that the Youth Association was also planning to hold a reading club and wanted to invite us to jointly host it. We felt that since everyone's goals were the same, joining forces would be better to concentrate talent and resources. So, after discussing, everyone decided to join forces as one. After the decision was made, we held several meetings to discuss specific measures. As a result, everyone drafted a

(Draft Plan) 195

Originally, we wanted to only be responsible for convening and intended to have the organizational method generated by the first general meeting. Later, we felt that everyone would not be prepared for the first discussion, and the organizational plan would probably be difficult to concretely determine. Moreover, recently many applicants have sent in proposals and opinions. Therefore, we believe that it would be better to combine these valuable opinions from readers and draft a plan to submit to the general meeting for discussion. This draft plan is divided into eight items. Now, let's summarize the main points as follows:

There are four main objectives of the reading club: (1) To freely discuss academics with an objective attitude; (2) To assist the masses with lower cultural standards; (3) To study theories without forgetting practice; (4) To have extremely free discussions but not to engage in any social activities. As for the discussion methods, they are divided into elementary classes and advanced classes. In the elementary classes, readers with the same level, with everyone's consent, read a certain type of book and form a reading group. The advanced class takes the combination of theory and practice as the principle, and the content of the assigned readings is extended to the study of practical problems. We hope that everyone will soon

Prepare Yourself 196

According to your own interests, plan to participate in which class of research and send us a list of the subjects you want to research and the "certain type of book" you want to read as soon as possible, so that we can compile and classify them in advance. If you have great expectations for the reading club, then you must prepare yourself in advance before the meeting so that our reading club can be actively established. Only in this way will it continue to thrive and be full of vitality in the future. Therefore, in addition to the above minimum preparations, we also hope that you will consider more about (1) what methods should be adopted in the reading club to achieve our reading goals; (2) how to make group exploration better than individual research. Recently,

(Registration Location) 197

Has also been determined. Namely (1) Baxianqiao Youth Association, (2) Sichuan Road Youth Association, (3) This newspaper library. The procedures at the first two locations may not be ready yet, so please come to the reading room of this newspaper to

Sign up. There are also many

(Comrades from Other Places) 198

Who have written to request participation. This is a de facto limitation, and we cannot invite them to Shanghai. In the future, in addition to broadcasting our research reports in Reading News to repay these enthusiastic friends, we can only express our sympathy and regret.

(What We Hope Readers Will Pay Attention To) 199

Some things that we hope readers will pay attention to have been said repeatedly, but sometimes you still don't pay attention. Let's say it again here!

(Do Not Slack) 200

Previously, we stated that anyone who wished to participate in our research department, if they did not communicate with us for two months and did not submit a reading report, we would cancel their registration. However, some readers still make this mistake after joining. This phenomenon of slackness continues, which greatly hinders our work. Therefore, we are implementing our previous decision and canceling the registration of readers who are lukewarm in their interest. We welcome new friends to fill the vacancies. Here are eleven friends, Wu Fanzhou, Li Bing, Dong Ji, Wen Zhuangzhong, Chen Jing, Xiao Jiazheng, Zhu Jiming, Fan Fang, Shao Jiren, Pan Ruhai, Zhu Boyan, who have not come to the office to collect their registration certificates for a long time, and their registration is canceled. In addition, we hope that other registered members will pay attention.

(Reading Reports) 201

Readers asked us to introduce books and question us, but after doing so once, some readers stopped writing. This is what disappoints us the most. Because we don't know if they are satisfied with our reply; whether they have read the books we introduced them to, and whether they understand them. These are things we must know.

(Introduction and Criticism) 202

Although we spend all day finding good books for you to read, our knowledge is ultimately limited. If you have any books worth recommending, please send them to us, and it would be best to briefly point out the advantages of the book. Similarly, if you can point out the disadvantages of a book as much as possible, it would also be a meritorious deed, so please report it to us for our reference and to remedy our oversight. Recently, Mr. Zhu Xiafeng sent us a letter pointing out the errors in our "Reading Questions and Answers Collection" and the points he doubted, one by one. On the one hand, we thank him for his sincerity in caring for us, and we admire his reading spirit and attitude of seeking truth. We hope that readers can make extremely strict criticisms of our publications.

(Address Unknown) 203

Replies will not be sent to letters with unknown addresses. Please pay attention!
