Spring and Autumn

Royal Incense Floating Record 205

— Original by Princess Der Ling of Qing, translated by Qin Shouou

In the middle, there are two horizontal wooden supports, one in front and one in the back. Their position: exactly between the palanquin itself and the two horizontal beams at the head and tail, but slightly longer by one or two feet; each of the four corners also has two porters carrying it. So, when combined, there are sixteen porters in total.

The exterior of the imperial palanquin is even more brilliant! The front, back, left, and right are all made of thin silk bordered with gold thread, lined with yellow satin inside, making it exceptionally luxurious and magnificent, beyond description. Moreover, there are four blue flying dragons painted on all sides, making the atmosphere even more majestic and splendid! The style of the palanquin roof is completely made according to the style of a palace, with upturned eaves, painted with gold and green, glittering and shining. In the very center of the top, there is also a yellow sphere, about the size of a bunch of grapes; although this sphere is hollow, it is entirely made of pure gold.

There is one more thing we must recognize, although the style of this imperial palanquin is inevitably a bit ancient, its exterior, interior, upper part, and lower part are all very beautiful; it must also be very comfortable for people to sit inside! However, when it comes to sitting, I have never tried it. As far as I know, apart from the Empress Dowager herself, only Li Lianying, because he was responsible for cleaning and tidying up this imperial palanquin, could go inside to clean up when the Empress Dowager was not in the palanquin; no one else dared to stretch their legs and step inside, let alone ride in it! Even the "Eight Treasures" pattern embroidered on the yellow satin inside could only be used on things used by the Empress Dowager. From my long speech, it is not surprising that this imperial palanquin occupies a carriage alone on our imperial train, and it can also be said to be "as it should be"! (45)

Beggars of Shanghai 206

— Xianxian

Being too poor to eat and becoming a beggar is a matter of course in life. But in Shanghai, being a beggar is not easy either. The beggars of Shanghai are divided into categories, each with its own style, guarding its own territory, and not encroaching on each other. And within the same category of beggars, they each have their own territory, which is not allowed to be invaded.

Beggars on busy roads, in addition to begging from pedestrians, are not allowed to engage in any other means of asking for money. Moreover, the area allowed is only a certain sidewalk section from Road A to Road B and is not allowed to exceed the range. The same is true for rickshaw puller beggars on the bridges of Suzhou Creek. They are only allowed to operate on one side of a certain bridge. If they exceed the range, they are not allowed to fight back even if they are beaten. As for those beggars who collect leftover rice from restaurants and delivery men at the entrances of various lanes, the rules are even stricter. Not only are there territories, but each beggar has fixed households.

Red and white invitations also have territories and do not encroach on each other. Those who use naked children lying on the ground to beg for money from pedestrians also have designated areas, and they cannot walk around in the north and south markets. Only those who wear long gowns, hold bamboo tubes, and sing Taoist ditties are not restricted by territory.

Each of the above categories of beggars has its own leader. Each

leader has absolute authority and the ability to control every "small role." The lives of the leaders are very comfortable, and some even have wives and concubines like the people of Qi. The source of this lifestyle, needless to say, is the extraction of the surplus profits of every beggar. And the beggars are willing to be exploited by the leaders because, it is said, they cannot get "work" otherwise.

Passing the Butcher Shop at Night 207

— Chen Liang

There are no bright streetlights in this area, only the big moon in the sky is attached to that tall chimney, emitting a desolate glow. The light of the stars is dim and green, and the gloomy and uneven coal ash is slightly spread out in the sinister atmosphere. It's midnight, walking alone, the front is dark, and the following is also dark.

Turning a corner, it is still a fence, broken walls, factory buildings, and a rugged coal ash road. The smoke from the tall chimney still passes by, passing through the moonlight, as if covered by a layer of black gauze, even more dim. A feeling of depression overflows from my heart. Far away, a red star flickers. After walking a few steps forward, it is not a star, but a lamp, hanging under the eaves of a house. I am surprised that the family has not turned off the lights in the middle of the night.

When approaching that lamp, the midnight wind brings a tragic cry, like the cry for help from the victim of a robbery and murder, so sad that it makes people's hair stand on end and cold sweat seep from their pores. I am walking in front of the butcher shop, I dare not look directly at the door…

The tragic cry continues to come out of the door. Before my eyes, I vaguely see a bright sharp knife, a bucket of bright red blood, and the fierce face of a butcher. My body trembles, and I can't bear the gusts of wind blowing in the middle of the night. I can no longer bear to hear the death throes of the moment of killing, so I quicken my pace and walk forward like a fugitive. The front is dark, and the following is also dark.

There are no bright streetlights in this area.

A Portrait of Rural Bankruptcy 208

— Bao Zhi

People who grow up in cities only hear about the economic bankruptcy of rural areas, but they don't know the reasons for it. To put it simply, on the one hand, they are subjected to the economic aggression of imperialism and heavy exploitation, which is already truly terrible. On the other hand, the gradual bankruptcy of national capital and the difficulty of selling domestic goods also inevitably affect the rural areas directly and indirectly. In addition, there are frequent wars and natural disasters in the country, which have already made farmers unable to lift their heads. What's more, there are also general gentry and landlords who force land rent and lend at high interest rates, all of which are intensifying exploitation and destruction. Farmers are under several layers of oppression. Can they still have a chance to be reborn? Even if there is an occasional bumper harvest, a group of unscrupulous merchants will take the opportunity to monopolize and suppress prices. As a result, a year of hard work is not only equivalent to white farming and white planting, but even their own land and property are completely exploited.

This is all a result of rural bankruptcy. Now, Mr. Li Pingqian, the director of the Mingxing Film Company, has made a film called "Golden Grain" based on these materials, which can be exposed on the screen so that everyone can see why the rural areas are bankrupt.

At this moment, "Golden Grain" will be shown publicly at the Xinguang Theater in this city.

On the Third Day of the Third Month of Jiaxu, I did not participate in the rhyme gathering at Houhu, Nanjing, and got the word "Long" 209

— Fu Gong

Poems from Xuan Yin Cottage

Living in the countryside, I experience the four seasons, knowing the east wind first. Great is the power of creation, subtly rushing to Zhou Hongmeng. Taking care of things as if I have much leisure, I do not say that spring will end. A good time for a grand rite of spring purification, but I cannot follow the path of cultivation. Gazing at the clouds of Zhongshan, dense and rising high in the sky. Thinking of the Yonghe year, gatherings of gentlemen came to drink and chant, outstanding was Wang Youjun, his preface especially majestic, why grieve over life and death, anxiously caring for his own body? Could it be that he, a talented and elegant person, did not have a broad and open mind? Did he entrust his unrealized intentions to the vast and distant wild goose? The age of elegant style in the Eastern Jin Dynasty, deliberations were extremely high and lofty, looking up and down, they became past traces, endlessly for thousands of years. The Eight Kings and the Five Barbarians, how could one encounter careful beginnings? Great chaos lost the apes and cranes, what could there be for the sand worms? In the end, those who read later would be filled with emotion and tears would flow horizontally. The insignificant transmission of some books, the vulgar are startled by snake dragons, vast is the Yangtze River, flowing eastward for eternity, containing emotions that do not cease, who can see through it? In words beyond lamentations, the Way lies in not being stained by defilement or prosperity.

Four Northeast Company Commanders 210

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 29: Responding to the Oath with a Wounded Heart, Marking Myself as Living Alone. Listening to the Same Oath, Swearing Loyalty Together. Ji Zhi bowed to Madam Gan and smiled: Okay, thank you, Madam Liu. Let me be honest with you, I have figured it out now, I am not qualified to make friends, let alone get married. I am adhering to celibacy. Madam Gan laughed when she heard this: Don't mention this too early, mentioning it will make people laugh their teeth off. To be honest with you, I used to adhere to celibacy too, but now I have been a wife for many years. Men love every woman they see, how can you say that? Ji Zhi raised his head and smiled, Sister-in-law, look in the future. Saying this, he refused to talk more and went back to his room. In his heart, he thought that women like Yang Guizhi were somewhat unreliable, let alone others? If I cannot at least be an official with the rank of section chief, I don't have to think about getting close to women in this lifetime. With his hands behind his back, he paced back and forth in the room. Finally, he pulled out a stack of paper from the drawer, stood at the head of the table, picked up a pen, and wrote several slogans in succession, which read: The freest thing is celibacy, the noblest thing is celibacy, I only like living alone in the universe. These kinds of words all had the meaning of praising personal life. Not only did he write them, but he also posted them on the walls of the room. Standing in the middle of the room, he posted the slogans, read them, and shook his head, as if he was very proud of himself. Needless to say, this grumbling of his was entirely due to the letter from Yang Guizhi. But outside Xifengkou, in Ping'an Village, thirty miles away, slogans were also being posted. The person posting the slogans was none other than Yang Guizhi's husband, Zhao Ziqiang. His slogan also expressed the same sentiment as Gan Jizhi, namely, with the enemy in front, don't look back at home. That also meant that there was no need for love, but he was not doing public affairs. A slogan like this was posted high on the wall. (395)

Traces of Art

A Record of Quietness in the Flower Mound 211

— Huo Xueming

The faint setting sun is scattering on our bodies, on the white shirts fluttering in the light breeze, and it is not far from dusk. Dragging our rattan canes, after watching the reeds in Xixi, we returned along Qinting Mountain eastward, to a dilapidated roadside pavilion called "Kaihua." Monk Shipiao resolutely urged us to enter the Flower Mound to listen to the sound of the spring in the secluded ravine and the quiet chanting of the monks.

I had long read Qian Tang Chen Dian'an's miscellaneous poems about Xixi. His poems praising the Flower Mound jumped into my memory at this time. While following Shipiao, I silently recited:

Mountain villages are deep, this is even more secluded and winding. When the spring breeze arrives, it is like entering a valley of ten thousand flowers. The setting sun arrives late on the ground, outside the flowers are green peaks.

What meets the eye are deep green pines and cypresses and lush bamboo forests. In the distance and nearby, it is all cool shade. There is only a winding brick road, like a gray and white silver snake, becoming thinner and thinner as it goes up, and the thinner it gets, the more blurred it becomes. On the left and right are the mountain screens of Fahua Mountain, sealing off the entire Flower Mound with the dense green of the trees. Only where the bamboo and cypress are sparse can one look up and see one or two points of blue sky and the shadow of clouds that seem to exist and seem not to exist. There are not even the footprints of woodcutters here. We walked quietly, but the small streams hidden under the accumulated leaves under our feet, sometimes to the left and sometimes to the right, leaked out clear sounds like the strings of a zither, which really made people's bones feel comfortable.

There are also places where the high sky will write into the eyes, and a glimpse of a light and agile bird, the faint red evening glow, flows like a water rainbow towards our shirts, and everyone's body floats with a bright red. Moreover, the setting sun slants towards the west, secretly passing through the green forest, turning the leaves into the color of violet, and a cluster of white-walled thatched huts or the yellow-walled nunneries of nuns, set in the forest, add a layer of quiet, cool, and lonely mood.

Life in the deep mountains at dusk is no different from sitting in a large forest on a moonlit night and listening to one's own breathing, which is so calm. Almost the mountain spring is about to freeze. Occasionally, the sound of a hazy temple bell flies from afar, and the nearby bells continue to ring, but it is impossible to tell which thatched hut's bell it is, because all the thatched huts are hidden in unseen deep depressions. At this time, between the vast twilight sky and the narrow path, we smelled the smell of cooking smoke and saw the mountain smoke like a mirage, and the chanting of the monks also sounded one after another.

Unknowingly, lost in a deep dream, I ran towards the tip of Fahua Mountain with all my breath one day, and finally I realized the dumb drawing of the Flower Mound in the setting sun. When a dog barked from a villa buried in the golden sunlight on the top of the mountain, I suddenly looked up and saw three large characters in white on a black background: "Baiyun Dui" (White Cloud Pile). "We're here! Let's go up and borrow a place to stay." I really wanted to learn from the chickens and dogs of the King of Huainan and have a dream in the empty mulberry tree in Yin Huang. But Shipiao immediately said: The owner of Baiyun Dui lives in Hangzhou City and does not easily come here to enjoy a bit of non-worldly peace. The house is empty and there is no food or lodging available. When he said this, the excitement of coming up the mountain turned into wisps of smoke, and I couldn't wait to jump from the top of the mountain to the Kaihua Ancient Pavilion and take the bus from Xixi back to the lakeside. Why leave the house empty and not give it to yourself, and at the same time refuse others?

Seeing that the sky was really getting dark, although the night in the mountains was another wonderful scene, when we didn't bring flashlights and there was no moon in the sky, everyone fumbled down the mountain and couldn't succeed without falling down.

Our Delegation Returns to Shanghai from the Philippine Islands Yesterday 212

(Wang Zhengting Talks About Opposing the Illegal Dissolution of the Far Eastern Games)

(It is not a pity if the Far Eastern Games cannot be preserved)

(Our country should first cultivate strength to participate in the World Games)

New Asia Restaurant Banquet Last Night 213

Dr. Wang Zhengting, the chief representative of our country's delegation to the 10th Far Eastern Games, along with all the athletes, returned to the country on the President Jackson some days ago. Except for the Guangdong and Hong Kong athletes who disembarked in Hong Kong on the 24th, the rest spent a night in Hong Kong and then took the original ship to Shanghai. They arrived in port yesterday afternoon. Mayor Wu, on behalf of Zhang Tingrong, and others welcomed them. There were five or six hundred people. After disembarking, the athletes from this city returned home or to school separately, while the athletes from other cities stayed at the YMCA, rested for a night, and then returned to their respective provinces separately. The China National Amateur Athletic Federation also held a banquet at the New Asia Restaurant last night to welcome Mayor Wu and all the delegation, and to entertain reporters from various newspapers. The delegation reported on the experience of attending the Games. Details of each situation are recorded below.

Warm Welcome at the Customs Wharf 214

All the athletes of our country's delegation to the Far Eastern Games returned to the country on the President Jackson. It was originally scheduled to arrive in port at 1:00 PM yesterday, but because the weather was fine yesterday, it entered the port at 9:00 AM and stopped at Floating Pontoon No. 16 in Yangshupu. They took a small boat and disembarked at the Customs Wharf at about 12:00 PM. Many representatives from all walks of life went to the ship's port and took small boats to welcome them. They included Mayor Wu's representative Zhang Tingrong, as well as Qian Xinzhi, Zhang Ming, Liu Yunfang, Wu Kaisheng, Ren Tianfang,

as well as representatives from the City Party Headquarters, the City Chamber of Commerce, the Chinese YMCA, the Baihong Sports Association, the Qinfen Bookstore, and various schools, and reporters from various newspapers, about five or six

hundred people.

The Athletes' Ship Arrived Early 215

The company's small boat docked at the New Customs Wharf at about 12:00 PM. All the welcoming personnel stepped forward to shake hands and express their condolences. The ship was originally scheduled to arrive in port at 1:30 PM yesterday. Later, because it arrived early, the Federation's authorities did not have time to notify, so many of the welcoming personnel failed to arrive in time. After 1:30 PM, the wharf was still crowded, and representatives of various countries continued to

Athletes and Representatives Returned to Their Residences Separately 216

After disembarking, the male and female athletes from other cities took pre-arranged cars and returned to the YMCA on Baxianqiao and the Women's Apartment on Pobo Road to rest. The athletes from this city, as well as Wang Zhengting, Shen Siliang, Zhou Jiaqi, and others, went directly to their private residences. The luggage was taken care of by Chen Bingde and transported to the YMCA and the Federation by the China Travel Service, waiting for the athletes to pick them up.

(North China Athletes Return North Today) 217

The North China athletes are scheduled to take the Shanghai-Ping train at 4:00 PM today, led by Coach Ma Yuehan, to go north. There are more than 80 representatives arriving in port this time. Li Huitang, Tan Jiangbai, Ye Beihua, Liu Mao, etc., were unable to come with them. Situ Guang and Luo Qing were temporarily staying in Guangdong. The athletes were full of energy and beautifully dressed, but their faces were darker than when they left. It is said that it was due to the hot climate in the south.

Our Country's Far Eastern Games Delegation Landing at the New Customs Wharf (Photo by Qichang)

Wang Zhengting Talks About Japan and the Philippines' Absurdity 218

Dr. Wang Zhengting, the chief representative of our country, said to reporters yesterday that this time Japan colluded with the Philippines to illegally dissolve the Far Eastern Games, which have a history of more than 20 years, with a small number of members. Our country absolutely cannot recognize this. The Philippines and Japan's desire to withdraw from the Far Eastern Games is their own right within their scope, and our country cannot interfere. If they want to dissolve the Far Eastern Games based on the approval of the two countries, it is not known where their power comes from. It is really absurd. Whether the Far Eastern Games can be restored and preserved, and whether the Philippines' attitude can be salvaged and changed, are all between possible and impossible. Before leaving the Philippines, I (Wang's self-称) had a conversation with Quezon, the President of the Philippine Senate. Quezon was still ill and had not recovered, but he was very clear about right and wrong and felt regret and remorse for the actions of the Philippine Athletic Federation. How the future of the Far Eastern Games will develop is still under negotiation. Wang said at the Customs Wharf yesterday to reporters from various newspapers that the Far Eastern Games are a part of the World Games, and our country is a member of the World Games, so we have decided to submit this matter to the World Olympic Games for resolution. Even if we do not get justice, we will have to think of other ways. However, it will take four years to convene the next Games. During this period, how will personnel change, and how will the international situation change? All of these cannot be predicted. Consider how Germany in 1914 differed from Germany in 1918 in those four years. This is a lesson from the past. Our country and the Philippines have always had extremely friendly relations. This time, the Philippines was deceived by Japan, resulting in this incident. Afterwards, the Filipinos also regretted it. Our country will still take the responsibility of the host country for the next Games and strive to prepare and invite various member countries to participate. I know that the Dutch East Indies and the Philippines will be able to participate. If Japan is unwilling, then so be it.

(Hao Gengsheng Talks About Perseverance) 219

Hao Gengsheng, the representative of our country, said that in this Far Eastern Games, our country can be said to have still achieved victory in defeat. The spirit of perseverance and refusing to participate in the pseudo-organization has remained consistent from beginning to end. Although Japan was able to collude with the Philippines to illegally dissolve the Far Eastern Games, it will never be able to make our country's fighting spirit submit. Hao has already returned to Beijing by night train last night to report to the Ministry of Education.

(Shen Siliang Talks About Public Opinion Support) 220

Shen Siliang, the main director of the National Amateur Athletic Federation of our country, shouldered a heavy responsibility in the plenary meeting of the executive committee this time because the chief representative, Dr. Wang Zhengting, was unable to attend due to illness, and fought bravely against the illegal elements. His spirit is commendable. Shen said that the actions of our country's delegation in the Philippines this time were able to gain the support of the public opinion circles, and all unanimously condemned the illegal actions of Japan and the Philippines. The Manila Daily Bulletin even published a strong editorial attacking the Philippine sports authorities. Shen specially distributed the original text of the newspaper to reporters from various newspapers for reference.

(Ma Yuehan Talks About Progress) 221

Head coach Ma Yuehan said that in this Far Eastern Games, our country has made significant progress. For example, Chen Baoqiu's iron ball and Fu Baolu's pole vault, although ranked second, have not yet reached their personal best records. In addition, there are several athletes who, although they did not score, were able to exceed the national records, which is very commendable. Liu Changchun's failure was indeed due to being overweight, so his results could not match others. As for Leng Peigen and Situ Guang, it was expected that they would be able to score, but unfortunately, they were nervous before the battle and played wildly. After a long period of training, there is great hope for the future.

(Record of the Banquet at the New Asia Restaurant) 222

At 7:00 PM last night, the China National Amateur Athletic Federation held a banquet at the New Asia Restaurant to welcome Mayor Wu, the delegation's staff, and the athletes, as well as reporters from various newspapers. More than 100 people, including Mayor Wu, attended. Wang Zhengting personally hosted the event. During the banquet, Wang reported on the experience of attending the Games.

(Account of Attending the Far Eastern Games) 223

In short, I knew there would be many difficulties attending the Far Eastern Games, including not only the Games themselves but also political difficulties. Before the meeting, Japan had already proposed the participation of a puppet organization. At that time, Japan sent Yamamoto to our country and the Philippines to lobby for this. We sternly rejected their proposal, and the Philippines also denied it based on their regulations. Therefore, the round table conference was held in Shanghai and was ultimately rejected. However, Japan did not give up. Thus, starting from May 19th, during the representatives' meeting held in the Philippines, Japan was the first to propose amending Article 3 of the regulations and demanded a vote based on the provision of Article 14, which required a two-thirds vote of the attending members. However, I declared that the regulations could not be changed without unanimous approval. By the third meeting, the Philippines, knowing that amending the regulations could not achieve their goals, did not modify Article 3 but instead changed Article 10, adding the phrase "or specially invited to participate" to the original text of the first clause, "Only amateur athletes who are members of this association may participate in the Far Eastern Games." Our representative immediately questioned, "Who has the right to invite?" The Japanese representative was speechless and remained silent for a long time, but still insisted on putting it to a vote. Our side immediately declared that if a vote was taken, we would withdraw from the meeting. This would mean that the quorum for the meeting would not be met. However, the chairman did not consider this and abruptly put it to a vote. Our representative immediately withdrew from the meeting. However, our representative withdrew from the meeting, not from the Games itself, so we absolutely do not recognize the illegal dissolution by Japan and the Philippines. After our withdrawal, Japan and the Philippines held two more private meetings, deciding to dissolve the Far Eastern Games and organize the so-called East Asian Amateur Games. We immediately protested and submitted it to the current chairman, Philippine President Quezon. He also expressed dissatisfaction with this matter and promised to consider it further. Therefore, I have a very solid legal argument on this matter. However, the future development and extent of this are still unpredictable. I will continue to report on the future progress.

(The Attitude of the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation) 224

Mr. Wang continued to state the attitude of the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation, saying that our country and the Philippines had jointly founded the Far Eastern Games more than 20 years ago. If someone destroys it, the responsibility for the destruction certainly does not lie with us. Once it is destroyed by someone, we should strive to preserve it. Therefore, if it can be preserved, we should try our best. If we cannot preserve it, it is not a pity. Our country's promotion of sports should strive to make it widespread and must start with young children to solidify the foundation. We must also have a long-term vision and pay attention to the world. With our country's large population, if we work hard to promote sports, we should be able to occupy a place in the world's games.

(Mayor Wu's Speech) 225

Next, Mayor Wu Tiecheng delivered a speech, briefly stating that the athlete representatives were passing through Shanghai on their return to China. He had originally intended to host a banquet to fulfill his duty as the host, but the athletes from various regions were eager to return home and could not fulfill his wishes, which he was very sorry for. Next year, the National Games will be held in Shanghai, and representatives from various provinces will be able to attend. At that time, they can gather in one place and he will host them again. He then said that the survival of the nation and the rise and fall of the people are not accidental. If we can act according to principles, we will certainly become strong. Our country has faced great difficulties due to various past darknesses. However, if we can overcome this difficulty, the future will be infinitely bright. Our country's future depends on the youth of the country, especially the students in school. Education is the central undertaking of society, and student activities are also the central activities of society. If young students can get on the right track, the undertakings of the country and society will develop vigorously. At the end, Wang Zhengting led the crowd in shouting "Long live the Republic of China" three times and dispersed.

(The Philippines Succumbs to Japanese Coercion) 226

According to a certain gentleman in the delegation speaking to reporters,

This time, the Philippine authorities succumbed to the Japanese side and accepted their illegal demands, dissolving the Games. The people of the Philippines strongly opposed this. Local newspapers criticized this arrogant move, and the Manila Daily Bulletin believed that this action by Japan and the Philippines was tantamount to expressing "cowardice and unreliability" towards our country. Most officials in the Philippine sports community also believed that this move was a disgrace to the country. However, the Philippine authorities did this with political motives. The Philippines' request for independence had just been recognized by the U.S. government. When Philippine President Quezon returned from the United States, he passed through Japan, where he may have reached a tacit agreement with Japan. Therefore, Philippine newspapers accused the authorities of having a prior agreement. However, Japan's threats were very blatant. At a certain banquet, the Japanese consul in Manila said, "Today, Japan has sent more than 170 athletes to participate in the competition, which is very joyful. If we sent more than 170 warships here, what would you think?" and "The Philippines is about to become independent and must maintain friendly relations with neighboring Japan." The Philippine authorities were ultimately coerced and willingly echoed Japan, and their fear of Japan is evident.

Tense Situation in Shanghai Open Handball Singles 227

Que Ke Ling Defeats Sun Daosheng

Bao Shanli Defeats Zhu Kuan

In the first Shanghai Open Handball Tournament, the match between youth and veteran players Sun Daosheng and Western Youth Champion Que Ke Ling was very intense. They won one game each, showing how fierce the competition was. Que was fierce and good at fighting, and his right-handed bottom kill was unmatched for a time. Sun was good at using tricks and specialized in attacking the left side, killing whenever there was an opportunity. Que won the first game with a score of 21 to 16. Sun won the second game with a score of 21 to 14. At the beginning of the third game, the difference in scores was very close. However, after reaching the teens, Sun's physical strength was insufficient and he failed. Que won again with a score of 21 to 13. In the singles match between Zhu Kuan and Bao Shanli, something abnormal happened. Zhu Kuan was unexpectedly defeated by a score of 0 to 2. In terms of skill and experience, Bao was far inferior to Zhu. Perhaps Zhu's bad luck was upon him and he made consecutive mistakes. This can be seen in the first game, which was 21 to 23, and the second game, which was 17 to 21. However, Zhu Kuan's hope for a trophy still exists. However, the order sheet outside the handball room stated that Bao Shanli lost to Kramer and then withdrew from the competition due to illness against Luo Tai. As Luo Tai left Shanghai, Zhu Kuan, Sun Daosheng, and Que Ke Ling are left to compete. Today, the sports officer of the association stated that Luo Tai withdrew against Bao Shanli. Who is responsible for the error in the order? Today's doubles competition features Kramer and Ma Luofu against Que Ke Ling and Bao Shanli.

Tennis Tournament's First Sound: China Tennis Club Performance Record 228

Xu Chengji Loses to Lin Baohua Due to Travel Fatigue

Xu-Qiu Team Wins 2-1 Against Lin-Zheng Team

The China Tennis Club officially opened yesterday, inviting our country's Far Eastern Games athletes Xu Chengji, Qiu Feihai, the Wang sisters Chunwei and Chunjing, and Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia to perform. The usually deserted Singapore Road suddenly became congested with cars, greatly increasing the liveliness. There were about four to five hundred spectators. Xu and Qiu had just arrived in Shanghai at noon and were fatigued from the journey, resulting in reduced performance. In the singles match, Lin Baohua won 6-3, 6-1 against Xu Chengji. In the doubles match, the Xu-Qiu team won 2-1 against the Lin-Zheng team. Finally, Xu and Ms. Wang Chunwei played a mixed doubles match against Lin Baohua and Wang Chunjing to add to the fun. As a result, the Xu-Wang team won 6-4. As for the construction of the courts, it is not yet fully completed. The stands and court structure are very exquisite. However, the courts are very loose and must be properly maintained. The details of the competition are described below.

Lin Baohua Defeats Xu Chengji 229

Xu's hitting technique seems to have improved compared to the National Games. However, due to travel fatigue and reduced energy, he seemed to be struggling. Lin Baohua, on the other hand, was well-rested and naturally had an advantage. The performances of both were very outstanding. Their shots were fierce and confident, and their serves were especially characteristic, making for a rare and wonderful performance. As a result, Lin won 6-3, 6-1.

First Set: Lin served first and won easily. Xu returned the favor in the same way. Lin then won the serving game with a slide. Xu also added a game, making it 2-2. The two gradually engaged in a fierce battle. However, Xu showed signs of fatigue and lost three consecutive games, giving Lin the victory at 6-3.

Second Set: After a short rest, the competition continued. Xu lost repeatedly, except for winning the first serving game, losing six consecutive games. Because his arm strength decreased, he could not control the ball, resulting in repeated mistakes. In addition, Lin's vigor was strong, and his backhand and forehand shots were more advanced than before, making Xu struggle to cope. Lin then won again with a score of 6-1.

Doubles Review: Qiu Wins Against Lin Zheng 230

After the singles match, the doubles match began. Xu Aji and Qiu Feihai teamed up to fight Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia. It was far less exciting than the singles match. Qiu's performance was greatly reduced, and he completely lost control, with many self-kills and net balls. Zheng Zhaojia was sometimes good and sometimes bad, with no certainty, but his serves were quite good. Lin and Zheng could have won, but unexpectedly, they were defeated. Xu and Qiu won 1-6, 6-3, 6-4.

First Set: Lin served first and immediately won a game. Xu relied on the power of his serve to win a point. However, Lin and Zheng's cooperation was excellent, and they used fierce attacks. Xu and Qiu made repeated mistakes and were at a loss. Lin and Zheng won 6-1 easily.

Second Set: Xu and Qiu gradually cheered up. Zheng Zhaojia made repeated mistakes, and Lin also lost his calm attitude. Xu and Qiu's fierce attacks left them unable to support themselves, forming a situation of 5-1. Lin and Zheng worked hard to cheer up, sweeping shots to both sides or the center. The ball was very fast and often had miraculous effects, but they only caught up two games and were eventually defeated by Xu and Qiu with a score of 6-3.

Third Set: Lin and Zheng continued to make mistakes. Wild balls and net balls reappeared repeatedly, almost completely losing control. Xu and Qiu again took the lead with a score of 5-1. In the sixth game, Xu won four consecutive points with his serve, earning a lot of applause. However, in the seventh game, Lin also won the game with his serve. In the next game, both sides showed great skill in blocking and high-pressure shots. Lin and Zheng added two more games, eventually losing 4-6.

Mixed Doubles: Xu Wang Wins 231

Finally, a mixed doubles match was played to add to the fun. Xu Chengji and Wang Qing played against Lin Baohua and Wang Chunjing, but the performance was ordinary, with no interest. The audience gradually dispersed, so only one set was played. As a result, the Xu-Wang team won 6-4.

Other Locations 238

Our Chinese Student in Japan, Ye Muhua, is Murdered, Ambassador Jiang's Reply Confirms, Protest Lodged with the Japanese Side 239

(Nanjing, 28th) Ye Muhua, a Chinese student studying at the Nagasaki Overseas Chinese Secondary School, was invited by two students from the Japanese Commercial High School on the 24th and beaten to death by a group of people. After hearing the news, the government telegraphed the embassy in Japan to inquire about the truth. Ambassador Jiang Zuobin replied by telegram to confirm and lodged a protest with Japan. The protest was submitted to the local government by Liu Ruxiang, the acting consul in Nagasaki, demanding that the Japanese side punish the murderers, provide compensation, and guarantee that the same thing will not happen again in the future.

Recent News from Polish Culture 240

Members of the Sino-Polish Cultural Association recently translated several pieces of news about Polish culture, which are excerpted below: (1) "The Chopin Society is Established in Warsaw" The Chopin Society has been established in Warsaw, the capital of Poland, to study the great Polish musician Chopin. The society is named after Chopin and is supervised by the Ministry of Education. Most of the famous figures and artists in Poland are members of the society. The society will hold music concerts, organize meetings, and organize the Chopin Museum and Library, and cooperate with societies of the same nature at home and abroad. (2) "Statistics on Film Screenings" The Polish Central Film Bureau recently published statistics on film screenings in Poland in 1933. According to the statistics, a total of 1,483 films were screened in Poland last year, of which 157 were filmed in Poland, 1,259 were produced in the United States, 70 were produced in Germany, and 20 were produced in the United Kingdom. (3) "International Wireless Radio Broadcasting Conference" The International Wireless Radio Broadcasting Conference, which will be held in Poland this year, is actively preparing. The conference will discuss several issues related to wireless radio broadcasting law. Major countries around the world will participate, and our country will also send representatives to attend. (4) "International Aviation Competition" Last year, Poland won the championship in the International Aviation Competition, so this year the competition will be organized by the country. Aviation clubs from Germany, France, Italy, Czechoslovakia, and Poland have all registered to participate in the competition. The competition will begin on August 28 and end on September 7. On the last day, there will be a 6,000-mile round trip flight, starting and ending in Warsaw, passing through many countries, and landing in Africa for the first time. The competition has numerous prizes, the first prize being worth about 20,000 yuan in national currency.

Local News 243

The City's Education Community is Preparing for the Citywide Teachers' Celebration Conference 244

Preparatory meetings will be held in the coming days. Teachers' Day on June 6th is fast approaching. In order to celebrate, the Shanghai Secondary School Teachers and Staff Union has initiated preparations for the Citywide Teachers' Celebration Conference. It is now soliciting the participation of associations such as the Shanghai University Teachers and Staff Union and the Primary School Principals Union to discuss the process together. Preparatory meetings will be held in the coming days to discuss everything.

The City's Children's Happiness Association to Hold Family Education Seminars Decided to Open on June 15th, Inviting the Mayor's Wife and Others as Members 245

In order to arouse social attention to family education and promote children's happiness, the City Children's Happiness Committee has established family education seminars, scheduled to open on June 15th. The Mayor's wife, Mrs. Pan, Mrs. Chen Hecin, Liu Wang Liming, Mrs. Hu Shuyi, and others have been invited as members. The implementation methods are recorded as follows: (1) This association has established family education seminars in order to arouse social attention to family education and promote children's happiness. (2) The scope of the family education seminars is as follows: 1. The importance of children's status, 2. A discussion of parental responsibilities, 3. The importance of family education and its implementation methods, 4. The relationship between family environment and children, 5. Women's parenting knowledge, 6. Children's health knowledge, 7. The importance of children's education and its implementation methods, 8. The cultivation of children's physical education, 9. The cultivation of children's moral education, 10. The cultivation of children's intellectual education, 11. Other important theories and methods regarding the implementation of family education. (3) Family education seminars will hold lectures once a week. (4) The time and place of the family education seminars will be determined by the association and the lecturers in advance and announced to the public. (5) The lectures in the family education seminars are divided into radio broadcasts and public lectures, which will be determined by the association and the lecturers in advance and announced to the public. (6) In addition to the members of the association, the lecturers in the family education seminars will be responsible for inviting leaders in the city's women's community and experts in children's education or science. (7) Family education seminars will have five members selected by the association. (8) The powers and responsibilities of the members of the family education seminars are as follows: 1. Control the time of the lecturers' lectures, 2. Contact the location of the lectures or the radio station for broadcasting, 3. Discuss the materials for the lectures, 4. Matters for public announcement to the society, 5. Other matters. (9) Members and lecturers of the family education seminars are all voluntary positions, but transportation expenses may be provided as appropriate when necessary. (10) If there are any imperfections in these methods, the association may revise them at any time. (11) These methods will be announced and implemented after being approved by the association.

The Public Concession Private School Association held its first executive meeting the other day. Those present included Cui Jianwu, Xu Xingchu, Weng Guoxun, Huang Daping, Chen Jicheng, and Zhang Lingfei. Huang Daping was the chairman, and Sun Yucai was the secretary. (3) Chen Hecin, director of the Chinese Education Department of the Public Concession Engineering Bureau, will be invited to be the first speaker in the Education Lecture Series, and Liu Zhanen will be invited to be the second speaker. (4) An observation tour will be organized to visit famous Chinese and Engineering Bureau schools in the city, with Cui Jianwu as the leader. (5) An education discussion forum will be organized, with Zhang Lingfei fully responsible.

Memorial Service for Ms. Zhao Jinying 247

The Shanghai Girls' Middle School on Ximen Xieqiao Manufacturing Bureau Road held a memorial service for Ms. Zhao Jinying at the school's auditorium at 3:00 PM yesterday. A total of more than 600 teachers, students, and their families attended. First, mourning music was played, and a eulogy was sung. Then, the students reported on Ms. Zhao's life and read the eulogy. Ms. Zhao was an excellent student with good character and treated her classmates with courtesy, so many students cried bitterly. Principal Wu and others also gave speeches. Finally, the family gave a thank-you speech and the service ended.

Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts to Hold Summer Art Teacher Training Workshop to Appoint Important Staff and Lecturers 248

The Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts has been holding its first summer school since it opened in the ninth year of the Republic of China, providing convenience for art teachers in primary and secondary schools in various provinces and cities to continue their studies. In order to promote the Ministry of Education's implementation of art education and meet the needs of the times, the school will hold an art teacher training workshop this summer, inviting members of the Ministry-appointed art curriculum drafting committee and experts in art education to serve as instructors, so that art teachers in primary and secondary schools in the interior can use their holidays to study the implementation of the new curriculum and seek to improve their teaching skills. It has been approved by the Ministry of Education under Order No. 5832. It is known that the main staff includes honorary presidents Cai Yuanpei, Li Shizeng, Sun Ke, Wu Tiecheng, Ye Gongchuo, Qian Yongming, president Liu Haisu, vice president Wang Jiyuan, general secretary and director of academic affairs Wu Mengfei, general secretary and director of logistics Mo Yunxuan, director of affairs Liu Hairuo, secretary Yan Kechang, director of the fine arts group Zhang Chenbo, director of the Chinese painting group Zhu Wenyun, director of the Western painting group Wang Yuanbo, director of the music group Tang Fengmei, director of the labor group He Mingzhai, and the main lecturers include Wang Jiyuan, Wang Yiting, Huang Binhong, Wu Mengfei, Tang Xueyong, Tang Jun, Wang Yuanbo, Zhang Xuan, Pan Yuliang, Pan Tianshou, Zhu Wenyun, Xie Gongzhan, Tang Fengmei, Jin Lusheng, He Mingzhai, Zhang Gengbo, and more than 40 others.

Modern Thought Society Holds Seventh Lecture 249

Wu Xingya Gave a Lecture at the Law School Yesterday

The Spirit and Action of the National Revival Movement

The Modern Thought Society held its 7th lecture at the Law School Auditorium yesterday at 11:00 AM. Mr. Wu Xingya, Director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, was specially invited to give the lecture. More than 500 members of the society and students from the Law School attended. The event began with introductory remarks by Wang Longzhang, Executive Director of the Society, and Shen Juru, Dean of the Law School. The lecture, recorded by Chen Dongbai, was titled "The Spirit and Action of the National Revival Movement." It briefly stated that at a time when the slogan of the national revival movement is sweeping the country, especially college students and young revolutionary comrades have a fervent sympathy under this slogan and actively engage in its realization. However, to realize this movement, we must establish a solid foundation in both spirit and action to define our goals and steps. Otherwise, it can easily become chaotic and disorganized like the revolutionary movements of the past twenty years, leading to many unexpected events. First, let me talk about the spirit of the national revival movement. Sun Yat-sen's motivation for revolution stemmed from the fact that since the Opium War, the nation and the country have been declining day by day. The Qing government was muddle-headed and confused, and international imperialism was actively invading. Recognizing the crisis of the nation's future, he determined that the national revolution should start with the ethnic revolution. Through three to forty years of continuous effort, with a spirit of perseverance, he overcame many difficult and challenging environments. Therefore, today, in carrying out the national revival movement, we must take the spirit of the Premier as the fundamental spirit. Under the leadership of the Central Government and Chairman Chiang, we must unite and first establish a foundation for the spirit of the national revival movement so that this movement can achieve its goal. Second, the action of the national revival movement. Action is the most urgent need. Having the spirit of the national revival movement, we must have practical action. The general malady of the Chinese people is that they can talk but not act. The reason for the failure of the past revolutionary movements lies in this. From now on, when we engage in the national revival movement, we must bury our heads in hard work and not just talk empty words. The perilousness of the international situation, the urgency of the world war crisis in 1936, the survival or death of the Chinese nation all depend on whether we are prepared today to cope with this overall situation as a turning point. Now, looking around China, internally, the communist bandits have not been eradicated; externally, national defense is empty. The last thing I want to say to you is that the New Life Movement advocated by Chairman Chiang is the basic work of the national revival movement, and it can also be said to be the mobilization meeting of the national revival movement. It requires the entire nation, every individual, to start from themselves. I hope that everyone will carefully read the outline of the New Life Movement and proceed step by step from the easy to the difficult. The first step is to transform the individual, and the second step is to transform the society. Only then will the foundation of the national revival movement be sound, and only then can it achieve its goal.

Free Talk

Leisurely Mood 250

— Ana

If Ana were to transform into a lady, she would definitely not love this kind of young man:

In terms of appearance, neither tall nor short, neither too fat nor too thin, long hair, combed and shiny; delicate eyebrows and eyes, a pointed nose; a round face, often coated with "Butterfly Cream" or similar; a Western suit, faintly fragrant, ironed straight, leather shoes that squeak, always wearing white gloves in all seasons, a cigarette hanging from his mouth, glasses on his nose, and silver dollars always jingling in his pocket...

In short, the epitome of fashion, discarded like worn-out shoes. Why? Because of deep disgust! One should not judge by appearances, but that refers to natural appearance. Natural appearance may be beautiful or ugly, and there is nothing one can do about it. But people always wear clothes, and once they wear clothes, the difference between high and low becomes apparent. There is the so-called high that is actually base and vulgar; and there is the so-called low that is actually noble and refined. Common people look at clothes to distinguish between the rich and the poor, which is not delving deep enough. It seems that many young people today could do without dressing like that.

Secondly, this kind of "generic product" is useless, always accommodating in every way, without one's own subjective opinions, without ideas. Their hearts are muddled, hence their round faces. Manifesting on the face and swelling in the back, the ancients emphasized that a person's cultivation can be seen somewhat from the outside, no matter how deep and silent they may be. Those who are useless cannot succeed in their work. Those who listen to others' commands will never achieve anything.

Thirdly, this type of person lacks depth, not loving enough, nor hating deeply enough. "Fickle as waterweed," the ancients scolded women, but it is appropriate to transfer this to modern young people today. If they are taught to obey, their temperament is of great concern. If they can obey me, how do I know they will not obey others? Therefore, the ancients had deep meaning in training servants and inspiring loyalty. There is also another layer; the good is never beautiful, and the beautiful is never true. Truth, goodness, and beauty can never be united. If there is truly such a thing as love, it does not arise from beauty, but from truth and from goodness. All these modern manners are just like fleeting smoke, here one moment and gone the next.

With these reasons, I deeply abhor and detest them.

Random Memories of Liang Garden 251

— Youjun

1. Second Hometown

Whenever someone asks about my hometown, after answering "X County," I think in my heart: I should say Kaifeng!

Yes, I miss Kaifeng, I miss the clear spring waters of Pan Yang Lake, I miss the ancient and lonely Yuwang Platform, I miss the Qilu Park with its blooming spring flowers, I miss the imposing Iron Pagoda. In this desert-like spring beyond the border.

Leaving my hometown, the first city I stepped into was Kaifeng. There, I received modern education, and there, I spent several years of wandering. There, I drank the sweet wine of love and the bitter wine of love, I tasted the warmth of human affection and the coolness of human affection. However, this stranger in this wandering year finally left this hometown-like alien land and drifted to another alien land.

The fragrant grass at the edge of the world, the ancient post station in the setting sun, whenever I wake up from a midnight dream with a lonely lamp like a bean, I think of Kaifeng.

Ah, the second hometown that binds people's dreams!

2. Pan Yang Lake

"Looking afar, the lofty and cold tower overlooks Bianzhou, the Fantai Iron Pagoda floats with the clouds, ten thousand families have no trees and no palaces, only the Yellow River rolls on."

This is Kang Youwei's poem inscribed at Longting. It is carved on the stone archway east of Longting. After Longting Park was changed to Zhongshan Park, many slogans overthrew the ancient and elegant couplets, only it still survived, adorning the remnants of boiling cranes and burning zithers.

As the poem says: in autumn, you walk on this old Longting, look at the high and empty sky, the vast clouds and mist shrouded ten thousand houses, only the Iron Pagoda stands alone like a crane in a flock of chickens. The wild geese in the air are loud. At this time, you look around,

Truly have the feeling of "thinking of the vastness of heaven and earth, feeling alone and weeping."

Down Longting, the arrangement of this so-called park, flowers and trees are chaotic, vulgar. Out of the park, two autumn waters on both sides of the road are Pan Yang Lake. In the past, there was a legend of Yang Qing and Pan Zhuo, but now they are both equally turbid green. At this time, the west wind blows the clothes, cool into the skin, if you sit alone in a small boat, paddling leisurely, Yanghu South has the pavilion of the Henan Library protruding into the lake, in the middle is a newly built thatched pavilion, to the north is reeds, water birds floating. A lonely boat in the middle of the stream, cool wind sleeves, fluttering like riding the wind. If you are not tired of swimming, you can turn back to the lake, driven from under the bridge into the Pan Lake. Putting in the middle, looking around the water and sky, the northwest corner of the city is desolate. The setting sun reflects into the water, brilliant as gold. The sound of pounding clothes on the lake side is bleak, unbearable. If you have read the Book of Songs, you will probably sing the poems of autumn water and reeds with a sigh.

What I can never forget is the dusk of the autumn of the eighteenth year: I went with a few friends, walking along the lake in the yellow light of the setting sun, tired and leaning on the bridge, suddenly glimpsed that Ying, who had already broken off contact, came slowly with a few classmates, when our sight met, she turned back and went away.

Last year, I came to Liangyuan again, revisiting the old trails, already gone without a trace, face peach, only increased the sigh!

Now wandering in the border, lonely and bleak, the past is like a dream, once a thought, once lost.

3. Yuwang Platform

Into the Henan Agricultural and Forestry Experimental Field, past a small river artificially excavated, you will see a few rows of weeping willows dancing in the wind, Yuwang Terrace is towering in the green willows. Into the fight, is the wooden square of "Ancient Blowing Terrace". On the stage is the Yuwang Temple. In front of the temple gate are two drum-like pieces of wood, said to be things from the time when Yuwang controlled the water. Police are stationed in the main hall of Chao Nei, prohibiting visitors from entering the temple, and there is a stone tablet with Kang Youwei's inscription on the east corridor. Behind the temple is a so-called Imperial Stele Pavilion, with a poem carved on the stele by Qianlong, which seems to make sense but does not. Ancient cypresses soar into the sky on the stage, looking around, you can see ten thousand houses and trees, hazy and vast. The wilderness is wide and the sky is low, the sound of the wind enters the ear, making people feel with emotion.

In the summer of the eighteenth year, because of the impact of the situation, when we felt that the school was about to dissolve, I strolled on Yuwang Terrace. I met Kui and Zhi next to the tea pavilion, walking leisurely by the man-made river, watching the gurgling water. They were wearing the same blue cloth uniforms of the school. If you had never met them, you would have doubted that they were students of the same sex. At that time, I looked at Kui and nodded, he smiled unnaturally and walked away.

In those days, among the classmates, who did not envy this pair of young lovers! However, human affairs are difficult to know. Who would have thought that in the following year, they would break off contact because of family relations? Later, when I talked to Kui about their relationship, I asked him about his impression of that trip, he just pondered silently.

Now Kui has been newly married for several years, but I know: he will not forget Zhi.

May all lovers in the world become families!

4. Qilu Park

Picking up the pen, I wanted to recount the travels of Qilu Park in the season of blooming spring flowers, but when I thought of Qiu, who had traveled with me, had passed away, I couldn't stop the dark tears falling!

Qiu, your white bones may have been transformed, but your pure love will always exist in my thoughts. Especially that trip together.

I still remember: at that time, we came out of Songmen, passed through a few deserted streets, and then arrived at Qilu Park. At the gate was a cluster of rockery, strange rocks standing tall. In the garden, flowers are dense, and on the man-made river, there is a pavilion, now I can not remember the names of these terraces. We walked through the flower path, wandering between the flowerbeds and sparse bamboo. Around the woods in the north, around the grape racks in the south. Resting under a thatched pavilion. Silently watching the blooming spring flowers. Watching the colorful butterflies flying. After a while of rest, we silently left this garden and went home, treading on the warm sunshine.

Human affairs are like turning into a moth. I finally failed her and drifted to the edge of the world alone.

The year before last, I received the news of her death; without sorrow, without pain, I was silent for a few days, quietly shedding tears.

I never had the opportunity to make up for it!

This regret should be until the end of time.

5. Iron Pagoda

In the desolate northeast corner of Kaifeng, what can still attract a few tourists every day is the imposing Iron Pagoda.

Under that blue sky, the Iron Pagoda stands tremblingly. Looking from afar: behind the few lonely temples, stands a dark mass, layer by layer rushing into the sky? If you walk to the bottom of the tower and look up, you can't see the top of the tower, you will doubt that it has rushed to God's throne.

Into the tower gate, inside is dark, if you see the light, you have reached the first floor of the tower. If you have the courage, it is best to climb straight to the top of the tower, on that tower peak: the panorama of Kaifeng will unfold before your eyes, in the mist, you can vaguely see the ancient Longting, fish-scale-like houses, factory chimneys, Zhongshan University (should be Henan University) auditorium, like an inverted face basin. To the north of the tower, it is desolate, the distant clouds and trees are hazy, there is a river like a line, that is the Yellow River. At this time, if the day is about to end, you can see the clouds shining, the setting sun like a golden basin, bursts of returning crows noisy night, "the sunset is infinitely good, but near dusk!" You will be quiet and happy.

After climbing the tower, the travel interest is tired, if you do not feel leg sour bones after the tower, then I really want to give you a thumbs up, say a "admire"!

But at this time I am in the border, away from Bian thousands of miles, I know when can I come to Liangyuan again to quickly ascend!

Ah, Iron Pagoda, I hope you will not be washed away by the turbid currents of the Yellow River, we will always have a future. (End)

Home, Bodhisattva, Opium 252

— Chuan Ren

In northern Sichuan, the three major topics of home, Bodhisattva, and opium are struggling, and the crux of the great contradictions is appearing from time to time. Although there are more important and significant issues, more than just the three: home, Bodhisattva, and opium! But as far as my prejudice extends, I only like to talk about this. Traveling thousands of miles away, I can't help but gently sing the poem East and West, Home is Best. But in the places I have arrived, they are doing their best to abolish the home. The people of northern Sichuan, like me, are typical Chinese temperaments, willing to starve to death rather than leave their not-so-good old home. Therefore, those who advocate abolishing the home become their enemies. Those who advocate abolishing the home want to eliminate the ethical relationships of father and son, husband and wife, and so on, but the Chinese, who advocate ruling the country by managing the family, fundamentally do not want to do this. Whether in power or out of power, whether scholars or laborers, the Chinese want to maintain family relations for thousands of years to come. The Chinese Republic lasts for ten thousand years is what they shout on the surface, but the longevity of my family and the longevity of my flesh and blood descendants are what they truly believe. This is a self-evident and supremely authoritative doctrine, and with this doctrine, no matter what doctrine can beat it. Because northern Sichuan is China, naturally there can be no exception, so once the enemy withdraws from northern Sichuan, the family is the only weapon to resist the enemy!

China does not have religion, if it does, it is only the external Bodhisattva. The people of northern Sichuan are as devout to the Bodhisattva as those who believe in the Bodhisattva elsewhere. Therefore, those who destroy the Bodhisattva are their enemies. Since the enemy came, although the temple exists, the Bodhisattva is gone. Land gods, Guanyin, Arhats, Ksitigarbha, all suffered misfortune and were thrown into the pit, but all the stone walls were engraved with enemy slogans. In this way, our devout believers in the Bodhisattva are unwilling to comply, hence the contradiction, and the struggle. As a result of the contradiction and struggle, most of the devout believers in the Bodhisattva have triumphed again.

Smokers are prevalent in northern Sichuan. Among all coolies, eight or nine out of ten are opium smokers. They love opium as much as their lives. Whoever does not want opium is whoever does not want their lives. Opium has become a second life, no wonder they curse the eradication of opium seedlings! It should be said that opium is cheap to one big copper coin a mouthful, three big copper coins a cup. Although the income of coolies is small, it is naturally more than enough to deal with such cheap opium! In the enemy's land, not a single opium seedling can be seen, which shows the strength of its eradication, but the most unwelcome are the majority of northern Sichuan smokers. They believe that this is tantamount to destroying their lives. The most ridiculous thing is that because of their belief in the Bodhisattva, they took their most precious opium and smeared it all over the unspoken mouths of the Bodhisattvas, black opium paste replacing red animal blood. This strange phenomenon is most seen in Guangyuan County, which is close to Shaanxi and Gansu. According to the locals, the "Bodhisattva" is not effective without eating "opium" smoke, and cannot bless their "home." Alas! Opium, Bodhisattva, home, the three formed such an important relationship.

The Republic of China is thus saved!

Stepping Ladder (2) 253

— Cao Ming

One day, A-Mei was hit by a playing companion, and anger filled her two cheeks. She immediately ran to Grandma Huang, and cried leaning against her knees.

"Hurry up and shut up. You can't take being hit once? Who told your parents to take fifty dollars and then not want you?" Grandma Huang said angrily, annoyed by the disturbance, and then bent her fingers to count: "Huang A-Sheng owes five dou, Chen Yong owes four dou three sheng..."

A-Mei was startled by this cold treatment. She raised her tearful eyes and looked questioningly at the woman immersed in bitter calculations, her mind returning to her aunt's place.

"Why are you being so dull?" Grandma Huang shouted.

"I, I, why hasn't Aunt come yet, will Dad take me back?"

"Ha! Don't dream," the woman smiled casually, "pick up the broom and sweep the floor, listen to me, if you're afraid of being beaten, don't go outside..."

The earth is like a waterwheel, days are moved away one by one, and the growing child also gradually moves the world she lives in into her simple mind. Obviously, A-Mei's life experience is increasing day by day. Besides her aunt and Liu Fuhe, there are still many things that she can't figure out even after daydreaming for a long time; her not-so-well-nourished body also takes on part of the daily affairs.

Every night, when Grandpa Huang and his wife slept in bed, A-Mei took turns in the middle to beat their bones, and the adults often ridiculed his tenant farmers with excitement, and sought pleasant data from the miserable facts. These constant cruel laughs and scolds often scorched A-Mei's suppressed heart, but the result of the struggle between her inner heart and external forces often made her tired. Once, she beat Grandpa Huang's urinating device, and Grandma Huang's face turned blue and white:

"You little bitch, good, don't sleep tonight!"

She used a rope to tie A-Mei to the wooden pillar near the door, put out the lights and went to sleep, until A-Mei cried as if she had been grabbed by evil ghosts, then she untied her.

The bustling situation of the market and all the complex sounds of the people, the groans of the poor, could not blow into Grandpa Huang's house. In this lonely hell where no light can be seen, A-Mei is exploring something that she doesn't understand and is eager for. In A-Mei's eyes, the only woman in the house who cooks becomes a closest friend.

"Sister, when you go to buy vegetables, take me out for a walk." A-Mei earnestly asked.

"A twelve or thirteen-year-old child, can't you go by yourself?" The second sister said, looking at A-Mei, and after a while, she gently shook her head and said, "I think you're like a chicken in a cage! I tell you, people can't live like this," the second sister continued to say to A-Mei, who was impatient to listen, "just like a chicken, raised in a cage until it's fat, and when people kill it and cook it to eat, although they praise it for being fat and tender, what about the chicken itself? Not to mention that, chickens are for people to eat, but people have souls!"

A-Mei gradually grew thin and long, but she didn't know where her soul was hiding. Her eyes looked at the things she came into contact with blankly and timidly. Her duties also increased with her height. Grandma Huang said smugly to her husband:

"The one in our family is as good as a working bull, but she's very stupid, she really only takes one step after being beaten! Her gloomy eyes are really annoying, I don't know what she's being dazed about all day long, this kind of person doesn't seem to have good fortune!"

In the year when A-Mei was seventeen, it didn't rain for three whole months, and the soil in the paddy fields was like the cracked feet of a farmer in winter: the tenant farmers who had "taken over" Grandpa Huang's fields came to Grandpa Huang's door with bitter faces. They all ran out because the landlord ignored them.

"A-Mei, if a tenant farmer comes to find me, say I'm not at home!" Grandpa Huang ordered loudly.

Having received the order, he sat at the door, mending his own clothes.

Deng Shiye, who often came, appeared in front of A-Mei with dense steps, his eyes flashing wantonly under the gold-rimmed glasses, and said: "Is Grandpa Huang at home?"

A-Mei nodded and stepped aside to let the fat man pass.

After a while, a tenant and a household came, and stopped upon hearing A-Mei's prevention.

"Grandpa Huang is not at home!" she said, and lowered her head to work.

"He'll be back in a moment, I'll sit here and wait for him," the farmer said cautiously and sat down.

"Why do you have to run here? There's nothing fun here," A-Mei said in a low voice? covering her face with her hands. The man seemed not to hear, and remained silent. Later, three companions came, and they sat down in the same way, and talked to each other.

Commercial News

Financial Support for Silver Tax Flourishes, Gold Market Steadily Rises by $2.20 254

(Exchange Market Eases, But Foreign Dollar Ultimately Struggles to Maintain Position)

The gold market was quite stable yesterday, with major buyers showing considerable interest. At one point, it was bullish enough to break through the $20 mark. However, the exchange market was normal, with arbitrage providing supply and struggling to profit. Later, the domestic market remained firm, eventually retreating within the $20 range. The morning began with overseas silver markets showing a slight decline in England and stability in the United States. Forward silver prices rose in the near term but remained flat in the long term. Exchange rates declined slightly. Spot gold in London fell by half a penny, while American cotton rose by ten points, and American wheat showed negligible fluctuations. Reports indicated that the US House Ways and Means Committee had passed the silver bill proposed by the President, with Davis strongly supporting it, advocating a 50% tax on silver profits. However, there was also talk that the President had the power to collect silver to repay war debts. As a result, raw materials opened high, gradually rising from $14.50. After the opening, the situation stabilized. HSBC's listed price remained unchanged, and the domestic market was quite stable. The market atmosphere was calm. Since the US had much higher spot silver prices than the government was willing to buy, people remained optimistic. When rumors of the Central Bank offering spot silver emerged, major players began to cover their short positions, stimulating the gold market and pushing it beyond the $20 mark. Buying interest surged, but the banks' domestic market was not very firm, fluctuating despite the rise. Later, banks continued to offer silver, and the exchange market remained loose, with arbitrageurs still providing supply. Public sentiment gradually weakened, making it difficult for the gold market to sustain its gains, eventually retreating back within the $20 range. The day's market conditions showed few special changes, with the situation mostly sideways. The price of pure gold was estimated at $1030. The day's market conditions are recorded below:

The morning opened at $1016.70, a slight decrease of one cent from last Saturday. Raw materials opened at $6.30. The exchange market opened with near-term selling prices of 1 shilling 3.5 pence for British currency and $32.875 for American currency. Heng Yu Shun Li Yuan Chun Yu Qing Yong Yuan, Feng Yong and others offered strips. HSBC bought August US dollars at $1.875, rising from $6.30 to $7.50. Yong De Yuan Mao Yong Jin had mixed transactions. HSBC's listed prices for British and American currency remained unchanged. At this point, there was much sideways movement. Later, Tian Feng Yuan Mao Yong Jin bought, while Da Kang Yi Feng Yong sold, causing a decline to $6.10. Yu Qing Yong Lai bought, but Ying Feng Heng sold, resulting in more struggle. Hong Xing Heng Xing made small gains, rising to over $7. Da De Cheng Yong Feng Bing Xing Yi Feng Yong Zhao Feng Chang Ding Chang Da Xing Yong Shun Mao eagerly bought, breaking through the $20 mark. Shun Mao Yi Feng Yong Zheng Chang Heng Yu further increased to $1 and some cents. At this time, Da De Cheng Heng Tai sold off, causing a pullback. However, public sentiment turned bullish. Zheng Chang Yi Feng Yong Da Fa Yong Chang Sheng Yong Fu Yu Fu An Da Kang Hong Li Da Chang Xiang Heng Xing Heng Xing Yuan bought up to $24.70. Da Kang Yuan Mao Yong Yu Qing Yong Lai sold, causing a decrease to $2.70, likely because the banks' appetite was normal. Bing Xing Da Kang still covered their positions, raising it to $3.60. High Cost of Mulberry Leaves Causes Many Silk Farmers in Jiangsu and Zhejiang to Lose Money 278

(Xiaoshan) The model silkworm area in the eastern part of the county achieved better results and higher cocoon prices. However, there were many silkworms but few leaves, causing the price of mulberry leaves to rise. Many farmers in the northwest township raised local breeds of silkworms, but the weather was unfavorable, resulting in significant losses. New cocoons have been on the market for several days. The cost of raising silkworms is already high. The highest price for improved breed cocoons is only 35 yuan, and local breed cocoons are 25 yuan, causing farmers to suffer losses.

(Chang'an) New cocoons in the town have been on the market for four or five days. This year's cocoon production is better with the improved breed, yielding a 60-70% harvest. Cocoon merchants have been open for business for several days. However, due to unified control, cocoon prices are low, and farmers' costs are high, resulting in losses. Farmers are preparing to produce native silk themselves. Cocoon merchants are reluctant to raise prices. Currently, the average price for improved breed cocoons is 32.3 yuan, and the price for local breed cocoons is 23.4 yuan. Each merchant has only collected a few dozen to over a hundred dan of cocoons in recent days.

(Huaiyin) The county's agricultural station sent staff to distribute improved breeds and encourage farmers to raise them. The silkworm rearing in the first, third, and fifth market areas is not weak, while the amount reared in the second and fourth market areas is lower. Many local breed silkworms were lost midway. The improved breed silkworm eggs developed smoothly. The early batches are experiencing vigorous leaf eating during the first sleep stage, while the later batches are also entering the first sleep stage. The latest batches have reached three sleep stages and require ample leaves. The supply of mulberry leaves cannot meet the demand, causing the price of leaves to rise. Each dan of leaves costs 1.5 to 1.6 yuan.

(Jiangsu) Recently, the Construction Department, in order to strictly enforce the unified control of the cocoon industry, fears that cocoon merchants in various regions will violate the unified control regulations. Therefore, it specifically issued a notice to the directors and deputy directors of various model and improved areas, specifically instructing all silver and money businesses not to allow any cocoon merchants who have not registered in accordance with the cocoon industry unified control measures and have not paid the guarantee deposit to open for business. Loans made in agreement with silver and money businesses should be rejected; otherwise, they should be reported immediately and penalized.

Silk Sales Show No Progress Last Week 280

Japanese merchants continue to aggressively sell new silk... silk prices remain difficult to increase.

European firms lower prices to purchase... Chinese merchants suffer losses and struggle to sell.

Last week, the local Shanghai foreign firm silk market showed no progress. European and American silk mills have significantly increased their consumption of raw silk and demand new and old silk. However, Japanese silk merchants continue to aggressively dump old silk, and new silk from Yokohama is entering the market. Japanese merchants are actively selling in overseas markets, making it difficult for both spot and futures silk prices to increase. The standard Japanese silk price in New York remains around $1.20 (US dollars) per pound. Japanese silk prices in England and France have fallen rather than risen, causing no improvement in Chinese silk exports.

Overseas telegrams indicate that silk prices in New York are only 530 yuan (spot for old factory silk), and new factory silk is only slightly above 500 yuan. Old silk in Lyon and England is only 570 to 580 yuan, and new silk is 540 to 550 yuan (both B grade). Various manufacturers believe that the losses are too great and are reluctant to sell. European and American firms continue to think about lowering prices and hoarding. Inland silk merchants have recently purchased over one thousand bales of white factory silk. Given the declining silk prices overseas, they are adopting a wait-and-see approach. Last week, only British and French firms replenished their inventories, resulting in a total transaction volume of two to three hundred bales of spot silk and an export volume of five hundred bales.
