Talks

The Queue-Keeping Society 281

— Cen Lou

A Shen Bao dispatch from Kaifeng the other day: a Queue-Keeping Society with long queues has been discovered in the area bordering Shijia Lian in Anyang, Yinlin County, Northern Henan. It is said that this is a reactionary group colluding with traitors and local hoodlums and has a bizarre slogan "good wine needs no bush". This is truly a "bizarre" piece of news.

Queue-keeping is undoubtedly a Manchu custom. When the Manchus entered the pass, there was a slogan at the time, which said "keep the queue, lose the head; keep the head, lose the queue". The so-called queue referred to the hairstyle prevalent during the Ming Dynasty, in which the hair was fluffy all around and not shaved. When the Manchus entered the pass, they wanted to shave the hair all around, leaving only the important part on top, which was braided into a queue. This was a Manchu hairstyle. The Manchus wanted to rule the "world" of the Ming Dynasty, and at the same time, they did not allow the existence of Ming Dynasty hairstyles, so the aforementioned slogan was born. By the time the Qing Dynasty was about to fall, the revolutionaries cut off their queues and shaved their heads into monk's heads, flat tops, or Western hairstyles. Thus, monk's heads, flat tops, or Western hairstyles all became symbols of rebellion. It is said that when Puyi cut off his queue a few years ago, some old officials cried for several days and nights. This shows how important the queue was to the rule of the Manchu Qing Dynasty.

Although the Queue-Keeping Society in the area of Shijia Gou in Anyang County, Northern Henan, cannot be expanded into an organization that supports the rule of the Qing Dynasty, and the queue is no longer a symbol of the rule of the Manchu Qing Dynasty, even Puyi, the only descendant of the Manchus, has already cut off his queue. It can be seen that this organization is ultimately just a bizarre organization, and it will not have much practical effect. However, while the tangible queue-keeping may not have much practical effect, the intangible queue-keeping is controlling a large part of China's land.

The Japanese putting the puppet Puyi on the throne is very intentional, one aspect is to invade Mongolia to the west to deploy a defense line against the Soviets, and the other is to use this name to enter the customs, to "recover" this "lost land" of the Manchu Qing Dynasty. They are arranging things this way now, and they will launch it in this way in the future. It was once rumored that Puyi would enter the pass to worship the imperial tombs, and that was a signal. At that time, although we may not have the same kind of queue-keeping disputes as in the late Ming Dynasty, the slaves and subjects of Manchuria are fully qualified to do so. Whether or not to keep the queue is actually irrelevant to the overall situation. But Wu Sangui of the Republic of China era is now standing in front of us, and that is the most terrifying thing.

Sports Meet 282

— Xiang Ding

The sports meet has begun, as it is mandatory to hold one "according to regulations."

The atmosphere seems a bit tense. More than a thousand students in the whole school are all good men, and this is an opportunity to "make heroes out of the situation." Who wouldn't want to get a few "medals" and show off a bit?

Those few athletic stars who are "usually famous" have now been hired as inspectors and are restricted from participating, the reason being "to avoid monopolization and promote popularization." Therefore, the ambition of the students to try has been directly increased. Many friends who are usually unfamiliar with the sports field are also participating ambitiously, so much so that even an archetypal figure like Old Chen, a "Book-Worm," is said to have felt a little "uncontrollable" in his heart! Some people say, could it be that the Chinese nation is about to be revived?

In the center of a very large sports field stands a tiny "command platform," the arrangements are simple and the furnishings are shabby, which makes the heroes feel a little discouraged when they see it. A clerk said, "This is just a matter of doing things 'according to regulations'!"

After the tedious and vulgar opening ceremony was hastily concluded, the competition began. Although there were very few spectators, fortunately, they still accounted for about 30% of the school's total, which didn't make the venue too embarrassing. What is most commendable is that there are actually more than a dozen "misses" who have never set foot on a sports field in their lives, graciously

Page 18

honoring it with their presence. It is rare for them to get up so early, covered in dust, and not be afraid of breaking their waists by stepping on coal cinder in their high heels!

100 meters, long jump, high hurdles, shot put, discus... One by one, the performances passed by blandly, and the spectators all seemed to lack energy. Strolling back and forth, they all vividly showed a bored face. Who came to appreciate art?

However, having said that, when the six unique female heroes perform, it is another matter. Before they even brushed their legs to run, they had already made the spectators panic. All they saw was people scrambling forward and backward, a chaotic scene!

When they threw the discus, everyone squeezed together like a small alleyway to get a clear view, so that the discus flew directly into the crowd twice. Although fortunately, a few more "martyrs" were not added to the school, there was still enough warning!

"Why does it always make people excited when women do things? What philosophy does it contain?" I don't know who said it in the crowd, but no one had the ability to answer this question.

Whenever the six female heroes finished performing a program, more than a dozen cameras would surround them and look at them carefully. Some people say that they are the real art appreciators!

"My goodness! The girls are really lucky! So many people have spent money to take pictures of them!" This is what Ah Er, the school's chauffeur, said. Everyone laughed. Unfortunately, during the triple jump, something very unusual happened: one of the athletes exerted himself too much, and with a "crack," he broke his shinbone! His face was pale, and he fell to the ground, able only to pant. In a moment of uproar in the whole venue, this unfortunate person was carried to the sanatorium, and the sports meet ended hastily.

That evening, when the students were eating, there was an extra topic of conversation out of thin air, but other than the "relatives and friends" of this unfortunate person, no one cared to "talk" about it!

Biography of Frustration (13) 283

— Forget Me

Pawn 284

— Dao

The two of them dug into their pockets as much as they could, only managing to find more than a dozen copper coins. The sky outside had darkened completely, and their stomachs were rumbling with hunger. They couldn't think of any other ideas. So, I suggested to my friend that the only option was to pawn something, but neither of us had ever done it before, and the first attempt was bound to feel a bit awkward. My friend pushed me to go alone, and I pushed him to go alone. We pushed back and forth without settling on anything. "Hurry up! I'm starving to death. We don't have time for this." In the end, we went together.

However, the first obstacle arose. Because we lived in an apartment, taking a large item out at night would definitely be obvious to the concierge. Wouldn't that be a public embarrassment? After some discussion, we decided to sneak out, one person taking it first, followed by the other, avoiding people's attention.

Once on the street, each of us was carrying a package. Even we ourselves were bewildered. Our hearts kept pounding nervously. What was so shameful about it? Although that's what we told ourselves, whenever a passerby accidentally glanced at us, it felt as if our secret had been discovered, and we couldn't help but feel anxious. Sweat almost beaded on our foreheads, and our hearts beat even faster, our faces burning hot.

An unsettling feeling, like we had done something wrong, accompanied us as we walked down the bustling street, feeling deeply ashamed. We almost lost the courage to even look up at people, and just hurried forward with our heads down. We walked past several streets, and even past several shops of our potential client. We wanted to go in, but we didn't dare. Seeing the many people coming and going, the idea immediately stopped, as if someone had poured a bucket of ice water on our heads, and our whole bodies turned cold. Looking at the golden sign with the word "Pawn" on the wall, we both sighed heavily, cursed under our breath, and then despondently ran away. We didn't dare act in crowded places, nor on main streets. So, we had to go to quieter places. After loitering around for half a day, we still hadn't succeeded. The inner anxiety and the running around made our skin burn, and sweat flowed in waves, soaking our backs. At this point, we were also worried about accidentally running into someone we knew, which would be even worse. Our stomachs were growling and we were getting dizzy with hunger, making us feel extremely anxious.

After walking a bit further, we finally arrived at a place we thought we could go in. Our hearts were pounding frantically. We had to do it. We were afraid that those guys inside would become suspicious, thinking we were pickpockets who had stolen

things, which would be disastrous. So, we stood at the door for a moment, trying our best to calm down before finally summoning the courage to run inside.

When we came out, it was as if we had become different people. Our bodies were as light as swallows, and our spirits were high. Listening to the jingling sound of the silver coins in our pockets was like hearing the latest pop song broadcast on the radio. However, when we thought about how furtive and uncomfortable we had been earlier, we couldn't help but smile bitterly.

Decisiveness 285

— Hong

Perhaps because the nation is too large, most of our compatriots have a regrettable and hateful character flaw: procrastination, hesitation, timidity, and complacency. To put it bluntly, the decades of being bullied and carved up by various countries, as well as the infighting and disputes among our own people, are all disasters brought on by this character flaw.

In the past, this character flaw seemed to only affect middle-aged and older people.

But now, it has spread even more widely. Even the usually energetic youth have been infected, and everywhere one sees the moans of procrastination, hesitation, timidity, and complacency. There are no calls for courage, decisiveness, brilliance, and progress; only the muffled humming, not the joyous slogans.

People generally deceive themselves and others in this way, with talk of "maturity and prudence," "composure," and "consideration for the environment," using various methods to evade responsibility, causing this character flaw to progress daily and become more widespread annually.

This can only be said to be the source of weakness of the Chinese nation and the reason why the country never makes progress.

The times are advancing, and the world is changing rapidly. How can our compatriots, who are deeply afflicted with this character flaw, keep up? They are bound to suffer endless hardships.

I believe that the most pitiful people in this world are those who are indecisive and hesitant, those who wander aimlessly when faced with difficulties, those who do not know where to turn, those who have no principles of their own, cannot make decisions, and only listen to what others say. People who are indecisive and lack decisiveness can never gain the trust of others, nor can they build a progressive and brilliant life for themselves.

There are so many people who are simply indecisive in everything, fully displaying their character flaws of procrastination, hesitation, timidity, and complacency. They dare not make decisions about various matters because they do not know, do not have confidence, whether the result of the decision will be good or bad, auspicious or inauspicious. They fear that if they decide this way today, they may find that the decision was wrong and regret it later. These people, accustomed to hesitation, have completely lost confidence in themselves, so they always lack decisiveness when faced with events. Some people are very capable and have good character, but because of their habits of procrastination, hesitation, timidity, and complacency, their lives are wasted.

I believe that this habit, this character flaw of the Chinese people, should be urgently reversed, especially for our young people. We should strive to eliminate it and actively cultivate the spirit of courage, decisiveness, brilliance, and progress. Whenever there is an event before us that requires us to make a decision, we should decide promptly, and not leave it until tomorrow, or seek irresponsible opinions from others. We should practice making quick and firm decisions at all times. Regardless of the size of the matter, we should not hesitate in everyday life.

Of course, it cannot be said that everyone is without mistakes. But I believe that even if a person who is decisive and courageous makes mistakes, it does not matter. Because no matter how many times he makes mistakes, his progress in his career will always be more promising and useful than those who are timid and hesitant. A person who stands on this side of the river, considering and hesitating, will never be able to cross to the other shore.

Of course, before deciding on a certain event, we should see all aspects, we should consider carefully, and we should use all our reason to guide us before making a decision. But once a decision is made, it should be allowed to stand, to be final, and should not be reviewed or reconsidered.

This kind of decision has endless benefits for an individual. Not only does it build confidence in oneself, but it also gains the trust of others. Gradually developing into a lifelong habit, its stability is like the water at the bottom of the sea, unaffected by emotional fluctuations, nor easily swayed by the criticisms of others or the attacks of the outside world.

Remembering My Hometown in Early Summer 286

— Yuan Zhi

With a blast of southern wind carrying the heat of the tropics, I suddenly woke up from a dream and realized that spring was over and it was now the season of early summer.

Truly, in this metropolis devoid of the tangible shift of seasons, how would you know that it was early summer if the balmy wind didn’t tell you!

Early summer, just thinking of the phrase, a strange emptiness fills the heart, as if a wave of wistful emotion is washing over. And yet, it's also a time laced with ardent yearning and love.

Early summer makes me think of my hometown.

Early summer in my hometown is lovable. Scarlet pomegranate flowers are strewn across the verdant summer hills. Walking along a mountain path, wafts of the clean fragrance of grass and trees fill your nostrils. The scent immerses you, intoxicates you.

In the small, clear, rippling pond, the surface is covered with yellow flowers – the bright and lovely water chestnut blossoms. A few lively ducks are swimming in the pond, completely at ease.

The fields are vast, the green wheat shimmering with a light, pale yellow in the vibrant sunlight. Soybeans and peas are already laden with pods, beckoning you to pluck them.

Chirping swallows weave through the willow branches; mournful turtle doves cry out in plaintive tones.

Ah! The hometown of my memory in early summer is so

poetic and worthy of longing!

The Beggar 287

— Qing

A beggar who was begging along the street looked to be at least forty years old, but his body was particularly short, barely three feet tall. He walked with a limp, and if you didn't pay attention to his face, anyone would think he was a child. In this way, he became a monster in everyone's eyes. A group of people followed behind him, muttering and talking, wondering why he was in such a strange, unclassifiable state. The people following him just thought it was fun, like watching a two-headed freak at the Great World amusement park. He went to every shop, holding out his hand for copper coins. Normally, when they saw these people, they would either scold them or insult them. Even if they were lucky enough to drop a copper coin for the people they considered most repulsive, they would definitely make a nasty face. But for this deformed figure in front of them, perhaps because of his deformity, he aroused people's curiosity. They all gazed at him with a comical expression, looking him up and down.

Page 19

But the dwarf kept muttering and repeating his plea, holding out his hand for copper coins. He stood there for a long time. A person in the shop was about to throw out a copper coin, but another person stopped him, saying: "Wait, let's take another look." He was both admiring and making fun of him as much as he could. He seemed completely unaffected by the expressions and ridicule he received around him. In fact, these encounters were common everywhere, and he was used to it. His only hope was for the copper coins. Even if someone spat on his face, he couldn't do anything about it. Unfortunately, his parents gave birth to him as such an odd and unclassifiable creature, making him subject to ruthless mockery in addition to the cold reward people gave him. But sometimes, misfortune is exactly the lucky part. This dwarf was able to beg for some copper coins from almost every shop along the street. Because people were using him for a joke, they didn't care about a copper coin, but only about watching a moment longer, or making things difficult for him for a little while.

When their interest faded, they let him go, waddling along in a stumbling gait like a duck on land. The people making fun of him followed along as well, shouting and laughing loudly, clapping their hands, expressing their happiness.

Insults, teasing, and mockery were very common. These people did not need anyone's sympathy at all; they only sought to get the copper coins.

Sending Tangmei Abroad 288

— Wang Ci

Tangmei:

What are you hesitating about? Go! Don't ever look back. Your friends don't want to see you lingering in your homeland.

Are you still attached to your home? What has your past home life given you? Haven't you seen your hardworking father, barefoot, still turning the same waterwheel as hundreds of years ago? Haven't you seen your mother eating rough barley and wheat porridge? Tangmei, in the past, you only pitied them, and you once shed tears for this image. But, Tangmei! What's the use of your pity? What's the use of your tears? If you pity them your whole life, you will still see them die pitifully in their old age. If you cry your whole life, they will still turn the ancient waterwheel and eat barley porridge their whole lives! Tangmei, can't you bear to leave your beloved wife? Hey, haven't you seen the archetype of your mother? Her youth will be crushed by the ancient waterwheel!

Tangmei, are you attached to Shanghai, your homeland? Ah, last year, when I knew you were pacing in the night scene of North Sichuan Road, didn't you feel grief and indignation at the faint music coming from the ×× dance hall? The year before last, when you and I trampled on the ruined former war zone of Zhabei, didn't you clench your lips to express your excitement? Tangmei, Shanghai is Monte Carlo; Shanghai is Paris in Prussia! Don't be nostalgic!

Tangmei, are you worried about finances? I have already written a 20,000-word short story for you. Your travel expenses shouldn't be a problem! Just take the "Nagasaki Maru" on the 19th! Just go! If you still have some luck, then your living expenses in Tokyo for a month or two should be covered! When you arrive in Tokyo, immediately write me a mailing address. If I am lucky enough to receive the manuscript fee, then on the 12th, you can go to a late-night snack bar by yourself for a slightly more lavish "self-cleansing meal." Tangmei, don't worry!

Tangmei, what are you hesitating about? Go! Don't ever look back. Your friends don't want to see you lingering in your homeland.

Amateur Mailbox

All Evictions, No Exceptions 289

Dear Editor:

Shanghai is the largest city in the country. Generally, citizens are experiencing economic difficulties due to the impact of the January 28th Incident. We now have difficulty enjoying abundance and fulfillment in clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and the high cost of rent, which is a difficult burden, fully demonstrates this. Therefore, it would be a wonderful thing if landlords could deeply understand the principles of the Rent Reduction Committee to save the economy of the citizens! However, those private interests who occupy a superior position not only ignore this, but also increase rents.

I am a tenant at No. 18, Lane 969, Zhonghua Road. I am now receiving a notice of eviction from lawyer Zhu Zhenlu on behalf of the landlord, Dunhetang. I have exhausted all plans, but I don't have the proper ability to uphold the contract. Therefore, I earnestly request you and the general public to make steady plans to help me solve my difficulties. I will first write out the lawyer's notice:

"Our building is dilapidated and beyond repair. To prevent danger, all tenants must move out by the end of May. No exceptions."

According to my investigation, the house I live in was built by the Hu Wenji Construction Factory (that's me) in the seventh year of the Republic of China. At that time, a warranty was issued, guaranteeing its solidity for twenty years. The construction cost was only over three hundred yuan, and after renting it to me, the monthly rent was ten yuan, which was later increased by 20%. During the January 28th Incident, the landlord defied the clear order of the municipal government and still has not complied with the rent reduction order. They also collect rent using the old lunar calendar, exploiting the tenants' economy, and it has been more than five years from the spring of the eighteenth year of the Republic of China to the present. The landlord absolutely refuses to allow tenants to offset the rent with the property tax they paid on behalf of the landlord, resulting in tenants paying over thirty yuan in property tax. According to the city's building regulations, if a building is dangerous, the Public Works Bureau will inspect it and notify the tenants to evacuate. Now, the lawyer claims that it cannot be repaired, which seems difficult to justify. A lawyer who has never studied construction techniques makes an arbitrary eviction, and their intention to expel tenants is clear. How great will our displacement and sacrifice be? Those who are unversed in the law know that they cannot fully resist such unreasonable infringement and oppression. Therefore, I earnestly request you to provide assistance by publishing this in the Amateur Mailbox column. Please help me and those who uphold justice to solve my difficulties, and I hope you will express your opinions on the rent reduction matter. Respectfully, Hu Gengsheng of Hu Wenji Construction Factory

Answer: According to your letter, the landlord is forcing you to move out without any reason. You can reasonably argue with the landlord. If the landlord does not agree, you can also file a lawsuit in court based on the contract, requesting performance. So your problem is not difficult to solve. As for the generally high rent, we should propose rent reduction, but this issue is quite important. Since you have raised it for discussion, let's talk about how to do it.

In this year of economic panic, the lives of ordinary citizens are extremely difficult, and the burden of rent is particularly heavy. Therefore, when they have no other choice, they try to tighten their living expenses as much as possible. Cutting back on clothing and food may only make personal life less fulfilling, but it does not cause much harm to the body. If housing standards are lowered, it will inevitably be detrimental to both personal and public health. Therefore, reducing rent not only allows ordinary citizens in economic difficulty to relax slightly, but the entire municipal administration and all citizens will benefit from it. However, the last rent reduction movement, although lively for a while, was initiated by only a few people, and the general public did not actively work for this matter, so this movement had no strength, and the result was limited success, which can be said to be a failure. Therefore, for the sake of the future of the city and for the sake of reducing the burden on the general public, the municipal authorities and all citizens must revive this movement. And to make this movement a success, all citizens must unite and jointly make demands on the landlords, and rent reduction can be realized. Otherwise, relying solely on government orders, the matter of "still not complying with the rent reduction order" like Mr. Hu's landlord is still feared to be unavoidable. In short, rent reduction is everyone's business, not a matter for one or two people. Mr. Hu has ironclad reasons such as his own warranty, so he can argue reasonably. If it were someone else, what else could they do besides complying with the eviction? Therefore, I hope that everyone will not ignore this issue and should pay considerable attention to it. Editor

Announcement to Authors: From next month onward, this publication plans to revise the method of receiving manuscript fees. Please clearly indicate the author's address and real name after each manuscript. Thank you. Editorial Department of the Additional Edition of This Publication

MADAM X (7) 290

— Dai Ni

"Shanghai doesn't look up to beautiful women admired by the manager of the World Trading Company!" The mysterious madam spoke in Shanghai dialect.

The handsome man in Shanghai was indeed clever. "You've won!" he said, hugging her tightly and kissing her passionately.

"You haven't failed either!" she said, laughing as she nestled in his warm embrace.

"Can you tell me your name?"

"MADAM X," she said frankly.

The next day, the day after today, the Shanghai morning after the Shanghai night, Mr. Wang Minsun, the manager of the World Trading Company, woke up from a sweet dream. His first act was to reach out his excellent fingers from the warm quilt to fix his Chaplin-esque hair. He seemed to sense that the beautiful Beiping madam had disappeared. No, now he should say, a woman who was a secret goddess of the city. His arm stretched across the pillow, and he barely opened his Kaulmen eyes. A wisp of lily fragrance left over from last night wafted into his Chevrolet nose. "MADAM X," he hummed softly, striking a hugging pose! Ah! Last night's dream, a sweet dream, a dream of a full moon and blooming flowers...

"MADAM X," he heard the sound of water splashing in the bathroom.

No answer.

A strange idea grew in his heart. He quietly left the bed, slipped on his slippers, and stood up stealthily like a thief. A note with a few lines written on it caught Kaulmen's eye.

He stretched out his excellent fingers, took it from the table, and sat down on the edge of the bed.

Mr. Wang:

I'm sorry, I need a sum of money right now. The six thousand yuan check has been taken away, but you haven't failed. You don't need to seriously search for a MADAM X without a real name among the three million people. If it is unfortunately publicized in the newspapers, it may be detrimental to your position as the manager of the World Trading Company. Thank you. We may have a chance to meet again. MADAM X

Snatching the beige suit he had casually taken off last night, and the platinum-chained Omega slipped out of his small pocket, eleven o'clock sharp.

The gentleman completely lost his manners, and hurriedly left the bedroom in his undershirt and shorts. The long windows of the outside balcony were open, and the spring breeze was blowing the tasseled curtains, blowing the calendar on the wall:

March 31st, Saturday. (End)

Movie Supplement, Tuesday, May 29th

The Shun Pao Screen Section

Observations on the Current State of Chinese Cinema (Part 1) 291

— Ya Qun

In recent years, Chinese cinema has progressed, which is an undeniable fact. At the same time, Chinese audiences have also progressed rapidly, which is an even clearer fact. There is obviously a ratio between these two, that is, the latter is progressing faster than the former.

Isn't that right? Chinese audiences, especially those in the petty-bourgeois class, have strong demands on filmmakers. We can obtain evidence of this fact from many films. "Humanity" gained a wide audience, and "Raging Torrent," "Spring Silkworms," and "Little Toys" also gained a wide audience. In addition, the box-office success of "Twin Sisters" broke the world's box-office record. Going down the line, "Life," "The Wrath of the China Sea," "Salt Tide," and even "Pear Blossoms in a Rainstorm" and "Wind" all made audiences very excited. As for "City Night," "Morning in the Metropolis," or "Light of Motherhood," there is no need to mention them.

From these films, we can know what audiences demand from filmmakers and what their needs are. They demand that filmmakers reflect the reality of current society. When they are destroyed by the cruel reality of their past dreams, they hope to find a solution to their own depression in the movies. Because the above films have all proposed and solved some social problems to varying degrees, although there are individual misconceptions or intentional distortions about the analysis and solutions, each work has explored the ordinary and universal reality so that most audiences are not alienated from everything in the film. On the contrary, they have a close connection with their own lives and emotions.

Of course, it still needs to be repeated that the ability of "Humanity" or "City Night" to attract audiences has its own harmful elements, especially "Twin Sisters," which caters to the backward worldview of the petty-bourgeois class and has become a work that we should pay great attention to. However, this does not unequivocally prove that the audience has no ability to distinguish or is willing to receive the wrong instructions in the film. Objectively, on the one hand, the author explored topics that could excite them, and on the other hand, individual authors used strong means to rape the will of the audience.

Of course, we don't need to ask filmmakers to blame themselves from the bottom of their hearts here, but filmmakers with a new and correct worldview, due to the emphasis on spontaneous justice! They will not deliberately deceive the audience. Furthermore, in the near future, outdated writers will inevitably be abandoned by progressive audiences. Only the integration of their opinions is the most just judgment.

The above fully illustrates how enthusiastically Chinese film audiences demand filmmakers, and at the same time, they retain a strong judgment to monitor whether the filmmakers have fulfilled their responsibilities.

So, until now, how have filmmakers satisfied the demands of the audience? As mentioned earlier, in many films, those progressive writers have classily adopted the method of contrasting poverty and have seen the promising future of the oppressed class to some extent. This aspect should be the most significant achievement of Chinese cinema after the January 28th Incident, and it is also the minimum victory of the petty-bourgeois audience.

However, because the environment does not allow it and every day feels like a struggle, on the one hand, there are shameless and distorted film critics who use the "bright tail" as an excuse to sneer and ridicule, attempting to destroy this tendency in the cold laughter like a smokescreen. Coupled with soft film critics and those who oppose slogans beating the drums on the sidelines, some of the more fragile writers felt even more embarrassed. However, stubborn and firm writers will not be shaken by this. If they have accurately recognized reality, their works will inevitably receive the strong support of thousands of audiences, and therefore their existence will not be shaken by any evil forces.

There is a most important condition here, that is, the author must be loyal to the audience, as important as being loyal to art. Their works should not only be accepted by the audience, but also become a weapon of struggle. Therefore, it may be helpful to put forward a few points here as a decision on the current urgent task. (To be continued)

Audience Opinion

Review of "Red Powder Iron Blood" 292

— Ding Ding

The story depicts the sins of a warlord.

What deserves our praise here is the director's technique. He unfolded the plot of the whole play very tightly, and the connection between shots was so close and concise. For example:

(1) From the scene where Gao Yan molests Li Xuejuan in Lu Yuanfu's house, the close-up of his hand merges into the scene of Lin Zhenxiao's two feet stuffing into high leather boots. He prepares to go out at his own home. Because the key to the door was taken away by Xuejuan, he could not get his belt with weaponry, so he ran to Lu's house to find her, thus discovering Gao Yan's ambition.

(2) After Lin Zhenxiao discovers the evil plan of Lu Yuanfu and his wife, he destroys the furnishings in their house. The almost destroyed clock and the photos of the couple merge into the clock in Lin Zhenxiao's house and the photos of his couple, followed by the arrival of the crisis.

There are few other small techniques interspersed. Two climaxes, one is the scene where Gao Yan teases Lin's wife and Lin breaks into the door and discovers it. The other is when Gao Yan is about to insult Lin's wife and is killed by Lin, which is also arranged very appropriately.

But there are a few small places that we should discuss:

(1) Would the wife of a battalion commander, with such luxurious equipment in her home, actually cook for herself?

(2) Judging from Gao Yan's arrogant attitude and lawless behavior, giving him the title of a brigade commander seems too small. Wouldn't it be more appropriate to say that he is a military commander or a division commander?

(3) After Lin Zhenxiao was driven to the brigade commander, Lin's wife waited for her husband to return home for a long time, she must be very anxious and uneasy. This is a scene that can enhance the power of the play and easily move people. It should not be ignored. Why can't a single shot be found on the screen, completely forgetting it?

Among the actors, Fan Xuepeng has made significant progress compared to "Spring Dreams in the Dance Hall." After her husband was innocently arrested, the sad expression when they met in prison, and the helpless state of enduring his insults when she went to beg the warlord to save her husband, was so natural and touching! Wu Yuanlong's performance is experienced and profound, with his own unique insights. Tang Jie's evil warlord is not bad either, but Xiao Zhengzhong's crying face, who played Lu Yuanfu, was too exaggerated.

The photography is mediocre.

Writing Before the Performance of "Humiliation" 293

— Luo Ba Gao

Since "A New Life" was released in Shanghai, Soviet film products have added a powerful team to the camp of Chinese cinemas, although their products shipped to China are not many.

This "Humiliation" is the first Soviet production with sound dialogues. In order to occupy a place in foreign markets, the film, like German productions, is added with very brief English explanations.

The main theme of "Humiliation" is the success of a production and construction movement of steel factory workers in a group; a masterpiece after the initial implementation of the five-year plan. The original name of the film is "Shame" “Sbame”, but it became "Humiliation" when it came to China. The word "Humiliation" can also be established, because the evolution of the play is that the factory workers successfully planned a huge kilowatt wheel, and the result was tearing up the shame flag, and finally won the victory through unyielding efforts.

I am afraid that only the Soviet film authorities would be able to have such an understanding of using production and construction as the theme of the film! I think only the Soviet film authorities have a deeper understanding of the film being regarded as social mass education! They used films to greatly assist in the social mass education in the implementation of the government's five-year plan. In terms of the theme of the play, they believe that love is a part of individual life, and production and construction are the whole of mass life. For example, in "Humiliation," what they construct is: personal aspects in love get a happy family, and especially in construction, the production people, and the factory workers' group get the final achievement. The greatness and solemnity of consciousness cannot be compared with American films.

The oppression and bullying of the nation originally had a certain self-humiliating nature of corruption and insect breeding. This is naturally because the mass production and construction movement is ignored. Selfishness and self-interest violate the conditions of being a human being today, and the group's production and construction is towards the masses. I believe it cannot be ignored.

In terms of film art: "Humiliation" is also successful. The playwright's thoughts are very meticulous, and the structure can also unfold the solemn and great theme in the evolution of the play in a tortuous way, with tight and undulating peaks and waves. Like the playwright's thoughts, it has a meticulous organization. Montage is undoubtedly right. Regarding the actors, each has undergone a good training, so the performance is calm and natural, and it is hard to find among the famous stars in Hollywood. In short, the performance of the whole play makes the previous silent Soviet production "A New Life" unable to monopolize the front.

I think "Humiliation" is not produced under the conditions of entertainment. Its serious significance, in the education of social masses, will of course get the greatest efficiency. Film practitioners who pay attention to social mass education will not neglect this "Humiliation"!

Fudan University Performs the Eight-Act Play "The Emperor Jones" 294

The masterpiece "The Emperor Jones" by the American playwright O'Neill has been adapted into a film in the American film industry, which is "The Fall of the Tyrant" previously performed at the Nanjing Grand Theater. Now, Mr. Hong Shen and Mr. Gu Zhongyi have translated its original text into Chinese, and the Fudan Drama Club has selected it as the repertoire for its sixteenth public performance. It is scheduled to be performed on campus at Fudan University at 8:00 tonight. It is said that at 7:30 last night, a school bus stopped at the intersection of Xizang Road and Baike Road. By taking this bus, you can go directly to the theater at 8:00. After the show, the school bus will take you back. The ticket price is forty cents, and the bus fare is twenty cents each time.

Movie Novel

(Love—Never Again) (2) 295

— Xin Fu

Qin En walked past several sailors' meeting places, because he had to break off relations with women. He ran into obstacles everywhere. Later, he came to a coffee shop, which was a place for sailors to indulge in pleasure. After Qin En went in, he saw men and women hugging each other. How dare he open his mouth there? But things happened by chance. On this day, several sailors were jealous of each other, and as a result, they were secretly plotted against by a woman. They reported to the police, who came to arrest them. After they discovered this, they knew that they had been tricked by the woman. They were extremely resentful. Because it was inconvenient to stay on the shore, they were eager to go sailing. Qin En saw through their secret, knew that the time could not be lost, and went forward to contact them. Of course, it was a success with one word.

In addition to these desperate sailors, Qin En also found a cook - a black man, an engineer! A Spaniard, a builder! A Parisian, and a doctor, Basque, who is said to have escaped because he could not stand his mother-in-law's complaints. On the day the yacht set sail, Mike came to the boat in his captain's uniform and summoned all the crew members to hold a speech. Their first commandment was not to go ashore to get close to women. After a while, the whistle blew. In the song "Goodbye, Love!" the yacht set sail. Everyone on the boat believed that evil women were now cut off. Everyone was energetic and happy.

March 23, 1926, passed Fire Island... March 11, 1931, passed the Gris Cape Lighthouse, day after day, year after year, their five-year period was almost full, but lust is the nature of life and can never be permanently cut off. At this time, except for Mike, everyone had long felt sexually hungry, often hallucinated, stood on the bow of the boat, and saw the beautiful shadows of women appearing on the water. Sleeping in bed, they had sweet dreams, and each of them was about to become a madman soon. They jumped and made trouble in the cabin, shouting and cursing. Mike ran up, wanting to stop them, but unexpectedly aroused their resentment. Everyone shouted together: "We have had enough of life on the boat! We want to go ashore!" "Then what about your contracts? What about the money you took?" Mike replied like this. "Money?" everyone said with crazy laughter, "We have money and nowhere to spend it, what do we want it for!" Mike knew that he could not reason with them and quietly left.

The next morning, Mike was standing on the bow of the boat when he suddenly saw a human body floating on the sea. He quickly sent the sailors to lower the lifeboat to rescue them, but it turned out to be a stunning beauty wearing a bathrobe, with snow-white skin and soft muscles. This water lily was seen by those men who had been longing for women day and night, how could they be indifferent? So one by one gathered around, laughing and making trouble. Mike really couldn't stand it anymore, and said to them: "Why are you all staring like this, haven't you ever seen a woman before?" At this time, the rescued woman was still unconscious, and he turned around and said to Qin En: "Quick, get a glass of brandy!" (To be continued)
